caturtho'dhyāyaḥ |

brahmovāca |

tathā tau balasampannau vajrakālau mahābalau |
pṛṣṭavān graharājendraṃ bhārgavaṃ bhṛgunandanam
bhagavannasmattāttena preṣitā vinayaṃ prati |
diśo gatāstathā deśāḥ saptadvīpā vasundharā
nirjitāḥ saptapātālā vaśe kṛtvā ca tatprajāḥ |
nṛpānuśāsane sthāpya tava pārśvamihāgatāḥ
kenopāyena indrādīn jitvā svarga jayāmahe |
| etadeva mamācakṣva sarvavidyākṛtaśrama |
śukra uvāca
jambūdvīpaṃ samastantu saptadvīpā vasundharā |
pātālāḥ sukhasādhyāstu divaṃ duḥkhena sidhyati
yasmiṃstiṣṭhati deveśaḥ sarvadevanuto hariḥ |
viṣṇuḥsarvātmako devo brahmā vedaviśāradaḥ
bṛhaspatirmahāprājño arthaśāstrakṛtaśramaḥ |
indro mahābalaścaiva dhanado vahrirniṛtī
marūdvāyuryamo yatra yatra candradivākarau |
viśvedevā vasurudrā graha nakṣatra tārakāḥ
anyathā dharmataḥ prāptaṃ rājyaṃ nāśamupaiti hi |
mārjāramūṣikaṃ yad vadyuddhaṃ dhvāṅkṣolūkaṃ yathā
mahiṣāśvaṃ yathā yuddhaṃ yathā dantimṛgādhipam |
evaṃ yuṣmatsuraiḥ sārdha yuddhamekāṅgamucyate |
yuddhabhogaṃ tathā kālaṃ deśañcaiva na jānatā |
asmadripubalāśaktiṃ ye yudhyanti narādhipāḥ |
ātmanāśaṃ vrajantyete nṛpā nayaparāṅmukhāḥ
nayo hi balavān yuddhe daivasampatsamanvitaḥ |
tathā puruṣakārantu buddhvā yudhyanti ye nṛpāḥ
te jayaṃ śatru nāśantu labhante avicāraṇāt |
pṛthvī puravarairyuktā saśailavanakānanā
yāvajjīvaṃ sthirā teṣāṃ yeṣāṃ nīti kramāgatā |
dharmeṇa prāpya rājyaṃ te dharmādevajayo bhavet
devāśca-rudra-brahmendra-keśavā-ravi-candramāḥ |
teṣāṃ yo yodhamiccheta sa kathaṃ jāyate sukhī
na yuddhena vinā devāḥ sidhyanti hi kvacit dviṣāḥ |
yuddhe ghātaṃ bhaved vatsa bandhu vargaparikṣayaḥ
kṣayaṃ yāti dhanaṃ yuddhe aśvadantimahābalāḥ |
same'pi punarviṣame yatra śaṅkarakeśavau
kāla uvāca
dṛṣṭīviṣā mahāghorā anantādyā mahoraghāḥ |
nirjitā asurā rakṣāḥ pātālatalavāsinaḥ
na hi me śakyate jetuṃ śaṅkareṇa mahātmanā |
kimpunardevarājena brāhmaṇena varākiṇā
vajradaṇḍasahāyasya mama khaḍgakarasya ca |
saṅgare ko bhavecchaktaḥ kālapāśena karṣitaḥ
brahmā vā yadi vā rudraḥ sarvadevanamaskṛtaḥ |
asmākaṃ nirjitā pṛthvī tathā pātālagocarā
svāmino darśanādeva divaṃ prāptaṃ tato yadā |
jayastathā bhavet kīrtiḥ parājayaḥ parāgatiḥ
prasthitā grahaśārdūṃla anujñāṃ dātumarhasi |
evaṃ śukraṃ samāpṛcchaya nabho māse tu cottare
diśañcottaraṛkṣe ca dvitīyāyāṃ tato gatau |
nandanaṃ tau vanaṃ gatvā sarvasainyena tiṣṭhataḥ
yamāntakaḥ pūrvadiśi merau ghorastu cottare |
paścime vajradaṇḍastu kālo dakṣiṇataḥ svayam
evaṃ te veṣṭayitvā tu koṭikoṭiguṇena tu |
āruruhuḥ purīṃ yāmyāṃ merorurdhvamadhiṣṭhitām
aneka parikhopetāṃ vaivasvatīṃ mahojjavalām |
tatra te kṛṣṇaghorāsyā daṇḍapāṇimahābalāḥ |
yamaścāruhya mahiṣaṃ kālapāśakarodyataḥ
tataḥ sā dānavī senā yuddhamānā mahāhave |
dāritā yamarājena svabalena mahātmanā
tāṃ bhagnāṃ sahasā dṛṣṭvā krodhena tu sudīpitaḥ |
uttthan hālāhalaḥ śakra mahābalaparākramaḥ
parśunā tu satejena sūryāyutaprameṇa ca |
jighāṃsan yamajāṃ senāṃ padminīmiva dantinaḥ
yamāntakastathā cakre mahāmāyātmakaṃ balī |
mahiṣaṃ yamabhaṅgāya mahiṣasya mahābalam
kāle caiva kṛtānte ca daṇḍinā vinipātite |
ekadhā daśadhā cāpi śatadhā ca sahasradhā
ayutāṃ lakṣakoṭīni māyāvī vai vinirmame |
tairdṛṣṭvā dharmarājastu cātmānaṃ śatadhāvṛtam
vāhanāstrāṇi santyajya gatavān pāvakīṃ purīm |
durnirīkṣyāṃ ripu rghorastasya dṛṣṭvā tu vāhinīm
ajāruḍhāṃ samastāste vahninā saha saṅgaram |
taṃ vahniṃ jvālālakṣeṇa kālānalamivotthitam
dadāha sahasā śakra vajradaṇḍasya vāhinīm |
purī tejasvatī tasya tāmra prākāra toraṇā
struvahastāstathā viprā utthitā bahulakṣadhā |
dhyānena te'dahan sarvāṃ vāhinīṃ vibhughorajām
evaṃ dṛṣṭvā tathā kālo daṇḍinā sarvagena ca |
māyā megha samutthena vāriṇā tūpaśāmayet
cetasāmṛtadāvānyaiḥ sarvān krūrān prarohayet |
evaṃ tacchamitaṃ tejo vahnikrodhasamudbhavam
vavarṣa paṅkaśaivāla kadalīndīvarāṇi ca |
evaṃ tat pāvako dṛṣṭavā svasainyaṃ daṇḍanirjitam
tyaktvā tejo'bhimānantu gata indrāmarāvatīm |
indreṇa tau samāyātau dṛṣṭvā yamahutāśanau
mahākṣobhaṃ samāsthāya gajarājaṃ ruroha saḥ |
udāyacalasaṅkāśaṃ sindūrāruṇavigraham
ghaṇṭākiṅkiṇīśabdāḍhyaṃ cāmarairupaśobhitam |
caturdantaṃ mahānāgaṃ suraśatrubhayāvaham
āruroha surādhyakṣo vajrapāṇirmahābalaḥ |
mātaliñca puraskṛtya viśvedevāstathāpare
vaiṣṇavā vāruṇā saumyā aindrāścāndrāstathaiva ca |
kubero dhanadaścandro vāyurvaruṇa eva ca
śrutvā devendrasaṅgrāmaṃ sarve tatra yuyutsavaḥ |
āgatāḥ kṣaṇamātreṇa svāyudhodyatapāṇayaḥ
evaṃ te tridaśāḥ śakkra saśakrāḥ saṅgarotsukāḥ |
śrutvā devaḥ svayaṃ tatra hyāgato garuḍadhvajaḥ
indrastu paramaṃ deva śaṅkha cakra gadā dharam |
dṛṣṭavā papāta caraṇe bhaktyā stotreṇa pūjayet
indra uvāca
namaste devadeveśa sarvadevamaya prabho |
śaṅkha cakra gadā hasta vanamālā vibhūṣaṇa
śrīvatsāṅka mahākāya kaustubhoraskamaṇḍita |
devārināśa deveśa vedagarbha namostu te
devamūrtira mūtiśca veda yajña phalaprada |
trimūrtistrigatirdeva bhaktānāṃ bhayanāśana
sama mitrāryudāsīna ripuṇāṃ kulanāśana |
trāhi māṃ devadeveśa pītavāso jagatpate
dānavairbādhitā devāstvāmeva śaraṇaṃ gatāḥ |
nirjito yamayajñeśo bahnirdīptisamanvitaḥ
evaṃ tvaṃ bhagavan prāptaḥ kiṃ karomi tadādiśa |
tathā śrutvā vaco viṣṇuḥ kṛpayā śakrabhāṣitam
provāca vihasan devo mā bhaiṣīrmama sannidhau |
yadyapi devadeveśa umā dehārdha hāriṇaḥ
āgatastasya devendra tathāpi arirhanyatām |
kintu kāraṇasadbhāvaṃ kathayāmi śṛṇuṣva tat
viṣṇuruvāca
āsīd dundubhirnāmā'sāvasurāṇāṃ prabhūttamaḥ |
tena jitāḥ surā sarve brahmavaraprabhāvataḥ
ajeyo brahmasūryāṇāṃ yamasyāsmākameva ca |
tadā nirjitya devāṃstu svarṇāccayāvayate kila
tāvat tasya mahābāho īśaḥ śailaṅgamo'bhavat |
tadā paśyati deveśīṃ śaṅkarasya tanusthitām
tāṃ dṛṣṭvā kṣobhamāpannaḥ kāmavihvalacetanaḥ |
devīṃ samudyato vaktuṃ devena ca sa īkṣitaḥ
tataḥ sa sahasā dagdho netrajenānalena tu |
devadevasya kopena dānavo bhasmatāṃ gataḥ
sāyudhaḥ sarathaḥ krūraḥ sapadātiḥ savāhanaḥ |
sahasā bhasmībhūtaṃ taṃ daṣṭavā devastrilocanaḥ
raktapītāsitaśyāmā bhaṣmāddhūritameva ca |
gṛhītvā sitabhasmena devīñcāpyavadhūnayat
tasya hastakarāsphālād bandhūnanāvasānataḥ |
uddhṛtā mahati vartiḥ sarvavarṇakabhūṣitā
tāṃ tapantīṃ samālokya umāṃ devanamaskṛtām tasmin samudbhavācchāyā sarvalakṣaṇalakṣitā
dvitīyaṃ devabhāgantu yācamānā mahābalā |
tadā umā dadau śāpaṃ smṛtvā ghoraṃ mahāsuram
gaccha pāpa durācāra bhūtalaṃ tvaṃ mahābala |
tathārūpo bhavedghoro nīla megha sama prabhaḥ
mahārūpo bhayaṃ dattvā sasurāsurarakṣasām |
devena taṃ tadā dṛṣṭvā kimetadbhavatīkṛtam
sa eva nirjitaḥ śatrurasmākaṃ vadhamudyataḥ |
na yuktaṃ śatrupakṣasya vṛddhiṃ dātuṃ kadācana |
yaśca kāraṇadravyāṇāṃ saviśeṣaṃ kṛta mudā |
mocate kṛpayā mūḍhaḥ sa eva nidhanaṃ vrajet
nipātya sākhilaṃ sarvaṃ mūlaṃ yasya na khanyate |
sa eva syād balī bhūyo badarī iva śobhate
tathā tvamapi durbuddhe rmayāyaṃ vinipātitaḥ |
devānāṃ vidhnakartā ca ṛṣi-brāhmaṇa trāsakaḥ
na yuktaṃ dvijadevānāṃ śatruvargasya vardhanam |
mandabuddhe sadā bāle srīsvabhāvena varttase
ityuktā śambhunā devī kruddhā tamavalokya sā |
madbhaktiparamo bhūtvā sarvadevān jayiṣyati
viṣṇubhāvaḥ paro hyeṣa avadhyo'yaṃ bhaviṣyati |
kuśadvīpapuravāsī candraśobhāṃ bhaviṣyati
saptadvīpāḥ sapātālāḥ sapta lokāḥ savāsavāḥ |
etadājñākaro bhūtvā ajeyo'yaṃ bhaviṣyati
niśamya vacanaṃ devyā unmārgagatibhāṣitam |
śaśāpa roṣamāviśya tvañca marttyaṃ gamiṣyasi |
tatra caiṣa durācāraḥ patitvaṃ yācayiṣyati
tathā krodhānalādīptā sā śapetāsurādhipam |
nīla megha nibhākāraṃ yama mahiṣa mivāparam |
krīḍamānā haniṣyāmi pañcānana vyavasthitā
uvāca kūpitā devī devo'pi ca tathaiva tām |
evaṃ pūrvaṃ surādhyakṣa śambhunā vajranirmitaḥ
dundubherdehajo bhūtvā mama bhaktiparāyaṇaḥ |
candraśobhāpurāvāsī madīyārcāsadodyataḥ
tasyedaṃ śāsanaṃ prāptaṃ brāhmaṇairapi duḥsaham |
kimpunaḥ sarvayatnena sabalo yadi dānavaḥ |
āgato ghoranāmā'sau rudrādīnapi saṃharet
tacchutvā tathāśrutvā ka tu harervākyaṃ kiṃ karomi prabho vada |
tvayā dattaṃ mama svargaṃ yajñā sarvāśca rakṣitā
indrāṇāmÌ tvaṃ prabhuḥ svāmī devānāṃ tvañca pālakaḥ |
ityukte vadate viṣṇuḥ śṛṇu śakra samāhitaḥ |
tatrāgato mahābuddhi rvācaspati rbṛhaspatiḥ
bṛhaspatiruvāca
yasya śāsanamātreṇa sarve devāḥ sabhāskarāḥ |
śamitā vasuyuktāśca vāriṇā iva pāvakaḥ
tasya kaḥ śakyate yuddhe sabalasya nipātitam |
brahmā vā yadi vā rudraḥ sāma naya vivarjitaḥ
ajeyaḥ sarvadevānāmetad dattaṃ tvayā prabho |
umayā tacca pūrve ca sarva devāri kaṇṭakaḥ
sarvāṃstra-tattva-vettā ca sarva-dharma-parāyaṇaḥ |
tathā bhaktiparā deva tathā bhāryā pativratā
lokapālaḥ prajāpālo dharmavartmanyavasthitaḥ |
tathā prabhūtabhūpālāḥ koṭi koṭi guṇāhatāḥ
dantināṃ yasya mattānāmaśvānāñca caturguṇāḥ |
airāvatasamāḥ sarve sacalā iva bhūdharāḥ
nārāyaṇāstra brahmāstra śivāścānye'tha vāruṇāḥ |
tasya evaṃvidhaḥ śatrorvināśaḥ kena kriyatām |
deśakālakramañcāpi ekāṅgaṃ pratibhāṣate
muktastrāsakṛtairdoṣaiḥ krodhajaiśca tathaiva ca |
ekādīn sapta yo vetti sa guṇī guṇināṃ varaḥ
aśva mahiṣa mārjāra-ākhu kākolukaṃ yathā |
na yuddhaṃ śreyase deva uragā nakulaiḥ saha
iti śrīdevīpurāṇe (brahmopadeśe) bṛhaspativākyāni nāma caturtho'dhyāyaḥ

pañcamo'dhyāyaḥ |

bhagavānuvāca |

satyameva mahāprājña bṛhaspati vacaspate |
tvameva vedituṃ yogyaḥ sarva nyāya vivecakaḥ
śambhugītā nayā yasya auśanāśca tathā nijāḥ |
madīyā brahmagītāśca vetti yaḥ sa vacaspati
tvayā indrasya nāthena sacivena mahātmanā |
ko na bādhayituṃ śakya śūlapāṇirapīhayā
sarvaguṇapradhānā ye durvijñeyā mahātmabhiḥ |
yogibhiḥ ṣaḍguṇā eva mantribhiḥ sandhivādibhiḥ
vibhinnāḥ sandhisandhāne samadoṣāśca bādhayaḥ |
sandhatte samatejastu saciraṃ bhiṣajau varau
tvaṃ trikālanayaṃ vettā sarvavidyāviśāradaḥ |
vadāsya yadbhavedyuktaṃ surarājasya sattama
vṛhaspatiruvāca
devadeva surādhyakṣa śaṃkha cakra gadā dhara |
tvadīyā me matirbhadrā na nijāsuranāśana
madānubhāvo deveśa tava pratyakṣato vayam |
yad vadāmo mahātmānaṃ dhṛṣṭā kulavadhūriva
tava vāco guṇāviṣṭā niṣkrāmantisma manmukhāt |
tathāpi kiñciddeveśaṃ hitāhitakaraṃ prabho
tavājñākāriṇo bhūtvā sukhamicchanti divaukasaḥ |
tiṣṭhantu tasya vācāyāṃ yāvaddevaṃ trilocanam
toṣayitvā jayāṃ devīṃ vindhayācalanivāsinīm |
evaṃ te mantrayitvā tu śakro viṣṇurbṛhaspatiḥ
nāradaṃ preṣayāmāsu rvajradaṇḍasya śāsane
viṣṇuruvāca
tvaṃ devarṣe viprendra brahmaputra mahātapaḥ |
gatvā vadasva taṃ pāpaṃ ghoraputraṃ surāriṇam
gatavān viṣṇorādeśānnārado yatra so'suraḥ |
tamāyāntamṛrṣi dṛṣṭvā kālo vajraśca pūjya tau
nārada uvāca
tava ghorasuto vajra sakālasya mahābala |
śāsane saṃsthitā devā devī kāntatarā ca te

kiṃ punaḥ śatayaṣṭā vā brahmaṇo viṣṇutatparaḥ |
bhuñja svargaṃ mahīṃ yāvaddevadevī tavāntakau
ṣaṣṭayā mindrāgni devasya śāsanaṃ ghorajaṃ divi |
kṛtvā bṛhaspati rviṣṇu rjagmu ryatra pitāmahaḥ
(iti śrīdevīpurāṇe devyavatāre haribṛhaspatyo)
(rbrahmasadana prāptirnāma pañcamodhyāyaḥ ) |
|
ṣaṣṭho'dhyāyaḥ |
brahmovāca |

namaste viśvarūpeśa viśvabhāva namo'stu te |
sarvadevamaya śrīman vāsudeva namo'stu te
bhūta-bhavya-bhaviṣyāṇāṃ kāraṇākāraṇau namaḥ |
anādirādi-madhyānta-parakāraṇa-kāraṇa
bhaviṣyarūpa sadbhāvaṃ matsyarūpaṃ namo'stu te
dhātrī-dharaṇa kūrmeśa varāha narasiṃharāṭ |
sarvavedapate vedya vedāntānta namo namaḥ
vāmanāya namastubhyaṃ rāmarāma namo namaḥ |
vāsudeva namastubhyaṃ kṛṣṇadeva namo namaḥ
śuddha-sadbhāva-bhāvāya śuddha-buddha-tanūdbhava |
rāgadveṣavinirmukto raktavāso namostu te
aśvārūḍha mahobāho kalidharma-pravartaka |
digambaradharo deva śūdradharmapravartaka
mlecchavargaṃkuloccheda namaste kalkirūpiṇe |
yugānta yuga-utpatti-yugadharma-pravartaka
namaste devadeveśa ! īpsitārtha-pradāyaka |
yadicchāmi bhavet tvatto mama deva tathaiva ca
mama kāryeṣu kāryāṇāmīpsitānāṃ surottama |
bhaviṣyāṇāñca vastūnāṃ sāhāyyaṃ kuru keśava
tatastuṣṭo mama viṣṇuḥ purā āsīt surādhipa |
varado'bhūd yathākāmaṃ sāhāyyamīpsiteṣu ca
evaṃ yo vaiṣṇavaṃ stotraṃ prātarutthāya bhāvayet| madhyāhne sandhyākāle ca tasyecchā kāmasiddhidā
putrārthī labhate putraṃ dhanārthī labhate dhanam |
vidyārthī labhate vidyāṃ sukhārthī sukhabhāg bhavet
ita śrī devīpurāṇe devyavatāre viṣṇustavaḥ samāptaḥ |

brahmovāca |

mayā pūrvai ca tvaṃ deva uktamāsījjanārdana |
asurāṇāṃ varaḥ śreṣṭho na deyo madhusūdana
labdhavarā madodrekādasurāḥ sura-bādhakāḥ |
bhavanti devadevānāṃ dvija-yajña-vināśakāḥ
tathāpyevaṃ mahāvāho ! vināśāyāsurasya ca |
cintyatāṃ brahman govindo vācaspatirbṛhaspatiḥ
brahmovāca |

tvameva sarvavettāsi tathāpi surasattama |
kāryāgatantu vaktavyaṃ nahi doṣastrivikramam
tadbhavet tatpurā kalpe bhautye manvantare hare |
devadevo mahādevo yo'sau paramakāraṇaḥ
svargaḥ sarvavyāpī ca anādi-nidhanaḥ śivaḥ |
tasyecchārthaṃ surādhyakṣa sthitaḥ pālayitā prabhuḥ
sutaḥ kālāgnirudrasya rudrapāṣāṇa mūrdhani |
tasmin hālāhalo nāpa mahābala-parākramaḥ
upanetātmajaṃ ghoraṃ dvitīyamiva pāvakam |
taṃ samprekṣya tadā deva mudgareṇa hataṃ tvayā
prabuddho'sau tadā bahniḥ śuddhakrodhena dīpitaḥ |
tasya niśvāsajā jvālā nirgatāstu diśo daśa
tadā tvaṃ mohasampanno mama śaṅkā tadābhavat mayā sañcintito rudraḥ khaṭvāṅga-karabhāskaraḥ
sa ca karaṇasadbhāvo dhyāna-siddhi-varapradaḥ |
preṣayāmāsa cāmuṇḍāṃ kālānalasamaprabhām
rakṣaṇāya tavāsmākaṃ hutāśanaśamāya ca |
tasyāḥ prekṣaṇamātreṇa sā ca jvālā śamaṃ gatā
tadāsau vadate devaṃ hālāhala hutāśanaḥ |
kathyatāṃ kāraṇaṃ viṣṇo yenāhaṃ tāḍitastvayā
tvayā ca yācito deva jagāma taṃ hutāvaham |
pūrṇaḥ saṃvarttate kālo māṃ brahmasya ca pāvakaḥ
tena vodhitavān rudro yo'sau kālāgni-viśrutaḥ |
vadato kāraṇaṃ brūhi yena tvaṃ mama kṣobhakaḥ
viṣṇutvamāgato deva jagato dahanāya ca |
uttthitastāvat kālāgnirmahājvālaughabhāsvaraḥ
śamitastasya devyā yaḥ pratāpaḥ punareva saḥ |
tadā tvayā mahādeva jñātvā śaktiṃ mahābalām
jagadutpattipālāya nidhanāya vayaṃ purā |

asmākaṃ marttyapātālāḥ śakradyāśca tathāmarāḥ |
sādhitāḥ kāladevasya prasādena mahābalāḥ

nāradaṃ preṣaya viṣṇo asurasya vimohanam |
karoti yena sa gatvā adharmeṣu niyojanam
veda brāhmaṇa devānāṃ bhaktiṃ kṛtvā upāgataḥ |
tasya patnī hyadharmeṣu yāti dharmabahiṣkṛtā
adharmaniratāḥ sarvāḥ prajāstasya na śāntidāḥ |
yena kenacidupāyena tenedaṃ kuru mādhava
evaṃ pṛṣṭastadā viṣṇurnāradaṃ sa samādiśat |
tvaṃ brahmaja mahāprājña sarvaśāstra-viśāradaḥ
kuśadvīpaṃ vraja brahmaṃstvamadharmavighātakaḥ |
tatheti taiḥ samādiṣṭo devārthe kṛṣṇavigrahaḥ
āgamadhyānayogena svatantra ṛṣipuṅgavaḥ |
kuśadvīpaṃ aṇāt prāpto yatra rājā mahāsuraḥ
dvāḥsthena taṃ samāyāntaṃ dṛṣṭvā brahmasutottamam |

rājarāja mahābāho dvāre brahmasutottamaḥ |

labdhādeśastadā dvāḥstho nāradamānayata tataḥ
ta trāsau viṣṇubhaktātmā ghoro devadvija priyaḥ |
taṃ prekṣya utthito rājā bhūbhyāṃ jānugataḥ śiraḥ

sukhaṃ saṃviśa devarṣe ityukto nārado'vadat

bhūpatitvaṃ sadā bhogyāḥ striyo vā navayauvanāḥ
ātmānaṃ paramaṃ devaṃ toṣaṇīyaṃ budhaiḥ |

ṛṣikanyāprakīḍāya gato dāruvanaṃ kila |
sa ca devo mahādevaḥ paratattvārthavedakaḥ

candra indra surā brahma sarve ca sukhamarthinaḥ |

vijñāya nāradācchakra ghora tanmativartmagām |

yathā tāta mama svāmī candraśobhamahātmanaḥ |
tathaiva tvaṃ mahāmātyo mama bharttānupālakaḥ
tava sarvāṇi śāstrāṇi vidyā-ānvikṣikādayaḥ |
vasanti udare yasya sa kathaṃ mucyate pathaḥ
amātyavaśagaṃ rājyaṃ vaśo rājā sumantriṣu |
tanmate bhuñjate pṛthvīmanyathā tu viparyayaḥ
tvayā tāta samasteyaṃ pṛthvīpātāladevarāṭ |
nāthena bhavatā prāptā sa kathaṃ na vaśastava
yadā hi vyasanāsaktaṃ nṛpaṃ buddhiviparyaye |
vijñāya sa tadāmātyaḥ prākṛtaṃ darśayedbhayam
tava bhinnāḥ sutā bhāryāḥ sāmāntāḥ pravarā nṛpāḥ |
madīye tvaṃ mate varttan svayaṃ tannahi vetsyasi
tvaṃ punaḥ sarvabhāvena tasyājñāmanuvarttakaḥ |
na hi iṣṭaṃ sadāmātyaṃ rājño rājyaṃ kathaṃ bhavet
yasya samutsavā vaidyā amātyā nṛpavākkarāḥ |
na hi rājyaṃ sthiraṃ tasya kapimālevamūrddhagā
amātyapravaraṃ rājyaṃ bhūtā dvāḥsthā avekṣakāḥ |
mahānasaḥ striyaḥ śayyāpānatāmbūladāyakāḥ
ete hi yasya sadūvṛttāḥ sa rājā-sukhabhuk sadā |
vibhinnairbhidyate tāta sikatā iva setuṣu
dharmādharmasya saṃsiddhiḥ svāminaḥ sukhamicchatām |
bhṛtyānāṃ bhavata tāta anyathā nirayāstava
ṛjuvraṇatvaksāramahāvaṃśā yathā gṛham |

tathāpi mama kṣantavyaṃ bālānāṃ na hi ruṣṭatām
evaṃ sabāndhavaṃ mantraṃ candrabuddhiḥ prahṛṣṭavān provāca saṃstutaṃ vākyaṃ devī tvaṃ devatāsvapi
suṣeṇa uvāca |

sarvasampattisampannaḥ samastabalavāhanaḥ |

tāvat kālena mahatā parikrāman paraṃ kila |
dvīpaṃ śākāhvayaṃ nātha tasmin krīḍan yathāvidhi
so'śṛṇot puṣkare kāyāmṛṣe khpasamanvitām |

sā kanyā bhadranāmā ca tāmudvāhasamutsukaḥ
kāmārtto vihvalībhūto na vindyādaparaṃ vavacit |
anicchamānāpi tathā gṛhītā pāṇinā kare

tathā sa tāṃ bhuñjayitvā gato dvīpaṃ narādhipaḥ

tena sā vimanā dṛṣṭā rudamānā tu kanyakā |

sanatkumāraṃ varadaṃ tapasā dhūtakalmaṣam |

sanatkumāraṃ varadaṃ koṭisūryasamaprabham |

pūrva jñānāgamaṃ kṛtvā virakto dharmamācaret |
atiprasaṅgo jñāneṣu na kāryaḥ siddhimicchadā
dharmaḥ prayatnataḥ kāryo yogināntu viśeṣataḥ |
nāsti dharmādṛte yoga iti yogavido viduḥ
yathādeśaṃ yathākālaṃ yathādravyaṃ yathukramam |
yathopadiṣṭaḥ karttavyo dharmo dharmaphalārthibhiḥ
na sukhāni ca dharmaśca nādharmaścāsukhāni ca |

varaṃ nopārjito dharmo na caivāparirakṣitaḥ |

anyathā kriyate dharmo anyathā copadiśyate |

aviśeṣā viśeṣebhyaḥ kāraṇatvāt parāḥ smṛtāḥ |
ahaṅkārāt parā buddhiḥ sarvataścāgrajo mahān |

sarvakāraṇibhirgūḍhairyasyānto nopalabhyate |
tacca viṃśatitamaṃ tatvaṃ puruṣādīśvaraḥ paraḥ
yaḥ śreṣṭhaḥ sarvabhūtānāṃ kāraṇānāñca kāraṇam |
tamīśānaṃ śivaṃ jñātvā naro nirvāṇamarhati
aṣṭau prakṛtayo jñeyā vikārāścaiva ṣoḍaśa |

iti sanatkumārīye yogaśāstre dvitīyaḥ paricchedaḥ

yogaḥ  tṛtīyaḥ paricchedaḥ |

īśvaraḥ puruṣo vyaktaḥ ye'rthāḥ prāgapi sūcitāḥ |
savasūkṣmādyanutpannāḥ sarve sarvagatāśca te |
sarve nityā hyakampāśca sarve saṃsargadharmiṇaḥ
avyūhikā avaṣṭabdhāḥ sarve niravayavāśca te |
bhūtapretasya liṅgāśca pradhānapuruṣeśvarāḥ
triguṇaṃ prasavaṃ dharmamaṅgaṃ bhogyamacetanam |
asvatantramaśuddhañca pradhānamiti cocyate
nirguṇau cetanau śuddhāvubhau prasavadharmiṇau |
jñānatvamatha kartṛtvaṃ bhoktṛtvamubhayorapi
anekaguṇa sampūrṇaḥ procyate guṇavṛddhibhiḥ |
sāpekṣo'darśakārī ca asarvajño hyasarvakṛt
ekaḥ patiḥ samaḥ pūrṇo aprāpto guṇavṛddhibhiḥ |
nirapekṣo darśakārī sarvajñaḥ sarvakṛcchivaḥ
asvatantramidaṃ sarvaṃ jagat sthāvarajaṅgamam |
yat sāṅkhyānāñca budhyante rudramāyāvimohitā
anantaśaktirbhagavān sarvayogeśvareśvaraḥ |
paśūnāmarthasiddhyarthaṃ sarvārtheṣu pravartate
kāraṇāt sarvabhūtānāṃ saṃsāraparivartinām |
īśvarasyāprameyasya pravṛttimṛṣayo viduḥ
agraṃ duṣṭaṃ tāmasānāṃ vidhatte rajasā duḥ khaṃ rājasānāṃ vidhatte |
paramaṃ saukhyaṃ sātvikānāṃ vidhatte karmāpekṣā hīśvarasya pravṛttiḥ
iti sanatkumārīye yogaśāstre tṛtīyaḥ paricchedaḥ |

yogaḥ pañcamaḥ paricchedaḥ|
śūnyāgāre gavāṃ goṣṭhe vṛkṣamūle catuṣpathe |
nadītīre śmaśāne vā devatāyataneṣu ca
apracchanne nivāte ca niḥśabde janavarjite |
asaṃsakte śucau deśe yoga-doṣa-vivarjite
snātvā śucirupaspṛśya praṇamya śirasā bhavam |
yogācāryān namaskṛtya yogaṃ yuñjīta yogavit
padmakaṃ svastikaṃ vāpi sthālikaṃ jalikaṃ tathā |
pīṭhārdhaṃ canadradaṇḍañca sarvatobhadrameva ca
āsanaṃ ruciraṃ baddhvā ūrdhvakāya udṅmukhaḥ |
nānya padmāñjaliṃ kṛtvā niśacalaḥ susamāhitaḥ
indriyāṇīndriyārthebhyaḥ sarvebhyo vinivarttayet |
sarvasaṅgān parityajya ātmanyātmānamāśrayet
uttamān madhyamān mandān sagarbhāstrividhāṃstathā |
prāṇāyāmān śanaiḥ kuryāt kumbharecakapūrakān
prāṇāyāmairdaheddoṣāna dhāraṇābhiśca kilviṣam |
pratyāhāreṇa viṣayān dhyānenāpīśvarān guṇān
gāyatryā yogasirdhtha japaṃ kuryāt samāhitaḥ |
vācikaṃ bāhyajaptaṃ vā bhaktyā mānasamameva ca
japyantu cintayennityaṃ na ca śūnyo bhaveddvijaḥ |
sthitvā kālāntaraṃ kiñicadomityetadanusmaret
oṃkāraṃ praṇavo brahma akṣaraṃ paramaṃ padam |
ityete dhyāyanopāyā ṛṣibhiḥ parikīrtitāḥ
yama-niyama-ratānāṃ bahu-vighna-bhayeṣu ca labdha dhairyāṇām |
bhavati jayo viduṣāṃ prāṇa-vāyu-dhāraṇa-labdha-lakṣaṇānām
iti sanatkumārīye yogaśāstre pañcamaḥ paricchedaḥ |

yogaḥ ṣaṣṭhaḥ paricchedaḥ |

yamānāṃ niyamānāñca avāntarakriyāsu ca |
sarvadigdeśakāleṣu yogābhyāso viśiṣyate
yadi syāt pātakaṃ kiñcid yogī kuryāt pramādataḥ |
yogameva niṣedeta nānyaṃ mantraṃ kadācana
sarveṣāmeva mantrānāṃ yogamantraṃ viśiṣyate |
tasmād yogaḥ sadā sevyaḥ sarvāvasthāgatairapi
yastu kāyakṛtān bhogān dhyāyamānantu sevate |
alpavīryaṃ hi tadyogaṃ yogaśāstreṣu garhitam
yo dhyātvā yuñjeta dhyānaṃ yajjñeyaṃ yatprayojanam |
sarvāṇyetāni yo vetti sa yogī yoktumarhati
ātmā dhyātā mano dhyānaṃ dhyeyaḥ sūkṣmo maheśvaraḥ |
yattat paramamaiśvaryametaddhyānaprayojanam
dve brahmanī veditavye śabdabrahmaparañca yat |
śabdabrahmaṇi niṣnātaḥ paraṃ brahmādhigacchati
antaḥ śarīraprabhavamudānapreritañca yat |
vāguccārya śrotravṛtti śabdabrahma taducyate
śabda brahma paraṃ brahma tasmin kṣīṇe yadakṣaram |
sadā taṃ manasā dhyāyed yadīcchecchreyaḥ ātmanaḥ
vaktukāmo yadā vācyamartha samprati padyeta |
buddhyahaṅkārasaṃyukto tathā dhyānaṃ samācaret
upalabdhiḥ smṛtirdhyānaṃ saṅkalpaḥ praṇavaṃ prati |
kalpanā bhāvanā cintā dhyānamityabhidhīyate
pavanavirahito yathā pradīpaḥ sthita iva lakṣyate niścalasvabhāvaḥ |
viṣayavirahitaṃ tathā hi cittaṃ sthitamiva lakṣyate'mitapravṛtti

yogaḥ saptamaḥ paricchedaḥ |

dhyāyamānastamoṅkāraṃ prāṇairyadi viyujyate |
tasya tat paramaiśvaryaṃ bhinne dehe pravarttate
oṃkārād bhraśyate cittaṃ kṣiptaṃ kṣiptaṃ punaḥ punaḥ |
śabdādibhirasampṛktaṃ bhūyastasmin niyojayet
anirviṇṇastu yuñjānaḥ śrāntaḥ śrāntaḥ punaḥ punaḥ |
kālena tadavāpnoti guhyādguhyataraṃ padam
deva-mānuṣa-tiryakṣu jantuḥ karma-vaśānugaḥ |
tāvad bhramati saṃsāre yāvadyogaṃ na vindati
nivṛttaṃ sarva saṅgeṣu buddhayā cādhiṣṭhitaṃ manaḥ |
cittamoṅkārasaṃyuktaṃ yogāya na nivarttate
anena kramayogeṇa yasyoṅkārādhivāsitam |
tasyoṅkāraṃ parityajya cittaṃ nānyatra gacchati
ekamātraṃ dvimātraṃ vā trimātraṃ kṛtsnameva ca |
hṛsvaṃ dīrghaṃ plutaṃ śāntaṃ śāntena manasodvahet
tailadhārāmivācchinnāṃ dīrghaghaṇṭāninādavat |
oṅkārasantatiṃ kuryād viśuddhenāntarātmanā
viśuddhamanasā yuktaḥ śāntātmā mohavarjitaḥ |
āsādya paramaṃ yogamakṣayaṃ labhate padam
oṅkāreṇa viśuddhātmā paraṃ brahmādhigacchati |
pare brahmaṇi sandhyāya saṃsārādvipramucyate
yo jñātvā bahu-vidha-doṣa-duṣṭametat saṃsāra satatamabhipravarttamānam |
yogāya pravarttate yogamārgavettāsau bhuṅkte phalamatulaṃ śivaprasādāt
iti sanatkumārīye yogaśāstre saptamaḥ paricchedaḥ |

yogaḥ aṣṭamaḥ paricchedaḥ |

ekāgrapraṇidhānañca apramādāt tathaiva ca |
yuñjānastu sadā yogaṃ yogadvāraṃ prapaśyati
yogadvāraṃ paraṃ guhyaṃ sarvatāpapraṇāśanam |
pavitramatulañcaiva durddarśamakṛtātmabhiḥ
na taṃ paśyanti vibudhā na tiryañco na mānuṣāḥ |
kāmabhogaparivyagrā bahūpakṛtakilviṣāḥ
yogadvāreṇa yatayo yuktātmāno dṛḍhabratāḥ |
oṅkārarathamāruhya gacchanti paramāṃ gatim
yogadvāramatītānāṃ nānyo loko vidhīyate |
yadgatvā na nivarttante prāsādācchaṃkarasya ca
yathā pathi hitaṃ mārga gamanāyopapadyate |
tad brahmamayaṃ tattvamaiśvaryāyopapadyate
tasya brahmamayaṃ tattvaṃ bhittvā manasi varttate |
avaśasyāpi satataṃ tasya siddhirna dūrataḥ
yena yena hi bhāvena manaḥ saṃyujyate nṛṇām |
tena tanmayatāṃ yāti viśvarūpo maṇiryathā
iṣṭadravyaṃ yathā kaścit praṇaṣṭamiva cintayet |
tadvat susūkṣmoṅkāraṃ praṇaṣṭamapi cintayet
guruvacananiyuktā jñānavijñānatṛptāḥ kalikaluṣaviyuktāḥ sarvadharmānuraktāḥ |
vividhaguṇamahāntaṃ śaṃṅkaraṃ vā'nuraktāḥ praṇavaniyatacittāste kṛtārthā dvijendrāḥ

dhāraṇāṃ sampravakṣyāmi kartavyā yā prayatnataḥ |
manaso hṛdyavasthānaṃ dhāraṇetyabhidhīyate

tadvad viśuddhe manasi niṣkalaṃ brahma paśyati
yathā jñānaprakāśena susūkṣmārthān prapaśyati |
tadvat susūkṣmamoṅkāraṃ praṇidhānena paśyati

rātrau jāgaraṇaṃ kuryyādiṃdramaṃtrānukīrttanam
purohitaḥ sadaivajñaḥ śubhaśāṃtirataḥ sadā |
chatrapāto nṛpaṃ hanyātpatākā mahiṣīvadham
piṭake yuvarājasya sasacivamanukaṃpane |
rāṣṭraṃ toraṇapātena dhvajena annakṣayo bhavet
patite śakradaṃḍe tu nṛpamanyaṃ samādiśet |
kṛmijālakautthāne śalabhāttaskarādbhayam
susame saṃsthite śāṃtirnṛpasya nagarasya ca |
yāvaducchritaṃ tiṣṭhanti tāvatpaurā hṛṣṭāḥ sadā
ketorniratāyajane bhuṃjīyādviprakanyāśca |
pūjā yādṛśī utthāne kuryātpāte tathaiva ca
rātrau śubhakṛtpātanaṃ dṛṣṭaṃ kākakāpotaiḥ |
yāti nṛpaḥsaharāṣṭraṃ kertuṃyaścaiva kārayet
nagare vā pure kheṭe paurā yadyevaṃ kurvate |
puranagarasya dvāre vṛṣasiṃha-khagotthitam
ketuṃ samasta ghorāṇāṃ nāśanaṃ jayadaṃ matam |
evaṃ pūrvaṃ hariḥ ketuṃ prāptavān vṛṣavāhanāt
tathā brahmasya tenaiva brahmaṇaḥ śakramāgatam |
tena somasya tato dakṣe taṅgantuṃ samāgatam
tadā prabhṛti kurvanti nṛpā adyāpi ucchrayam |
evaṃ yaḥ kārayedrājā ketuṃ vijaya kārakam
tasya pṛthvī balopetā sadvīpā vaśagā bhavet
ityādye śrī devīpurāṇe devyavatāre dhvajalakṣaṇaṃ nāma dvādaśo'dhyāyaḥ
trayodaśo'dhyāyaḥ |

agastya uvāca |

etat te sarvamākhyātaṃ ketukhyāpanamāgatam |
bhūyaḥ kiṃ pṛcchase rājaṃstanno brūhi vadāmi te
nṛpavāhana uvāca |

kathitaṃ vidyāmāhātmyaṃ yogaṃ nārada-pṛcchitam |
ketoḥ samucchrayaḥ puṇyaḥ sarvakāma-sukhapradaḥ
bhūyastāta punaḥ pṛcchet kathaṃ ghoro mahābalaḥ |
nāradena sapatnīkaḥ sahamaṃtrī vimohitaḥ
agastya uvāca |

yathā sa pṛṣṭavānvatsa śakrastvasurasattamaḥ |
evaṃ pitāmahaṃ pūrvaṃ vidyāyogasya kautukam
devaṃ bhūyo'pi saṃpṛṣṭo ghora-buddhi-vighātanam |
kathaṃ kuryyānmahābāho nārado munisattamaḥ
brahmovāca |

tasya japanaśīlasya pratāpāt surasattamaḥ |
devānāṃ mahatī vṛṣṭiḥ sarvvā sukhapradā bhavet
vanaspatiḥ samastāśca phalapuṣpaiḥ suśobhitāḥ |
mohitā ghorasenā tu sahamaṃtripurohitā
vidharmapathagā sarvvā bhartturanveṣaṇe ratā |
vaṃcane tasya dārāderdhanasya vibhavasya ca
sanmārga satpathaṃ tyaktvā tena te mohitāsurāḥ |
vikarmaniratā vatsa vidharmamatiśīlinaḥ
tāñca śīlamatīṃ rājñīṃ digambaraparāyaṇām |
aneka vrata-bhūyiṣṭhāṃ hetuvāda-manonugām
pāṣaṃḍa-sarva-dharmasthāṃ śiva-viṣṇu-jugupsitām |
na cāgniharaṇe bhaktirnātithau gṛhapūjane
na mātaro mahābhāgā na gāvo na ca brāhmaṇāḥ |
evaṃ sā nāradocchiṣṭān dharmān kuryyāt sadā satī
evaṃ vidharmmamādhāya tasya ghorasya vai sabhāḥ |
supathamujjhayitvā tu unmārgena pravarttire
ghora uvāca |

brahmaputra mahābāho śailaputryā naye mama |
ko yogyo hyatra yodhānāṃ drutakāryyasya brūhi naḥ
nārada uvāca |

yataḥ śaśāṅka-sampūrṇā bilāñchana ivānanāḥ |
tāṃ dṛṣṭvā munayaḥ kṣobhaṃ kiṃ punarasurādhipāḥ
tathā tvaṃ sarvva-sainyena eko vā vigatāyudhaḥ |
vrajasva yatra tāḥ kanyāḥ śailarāja-sutottamāḥ
dakṣiṇā sārvadaivatyai paurṇamāsyāṃ samāyayau |
savāhana-balāmātyaḥ sapurohitaḥ sāyudhaḥ
suṣeṇa kuru huṅkāraṃ devala-vibhu-dāruṇaiḥ |
vāṇa-keśava-cāmuṇḍa-anuhrāda mahābalaiḥ
sāmantapravarairyyodhairmmaṅgalairāśibhistathā |
muhūrte abhijinnāmni madhyāhne tyajate puram
tasya nirgacchato vegāt śvāno vāsthimukho'bhavat |
dhvaje ruroha kāpotaḥ śivā śyāmā ca dakṣiṇā
piṅgalā rūrūgodhā ca śūkarī kabalāstathā |
gaja-bānara-senāja-śikhicchivā ca vāmataḥ
panthānaṃ bhindate sarpaḥ kumbhodakaṃ vyaśīryyata |
rūrāva vānaro ṛkṣo mārjjāro hyatibhairavam
taila-takra-tṛṇa-keśa muṇḍābhyaktādi darśanam |
vāntonmatta-jaḍa-mūka kṣutkṣābha-nakrajaṃ varam
tuṣa kārpāśalavaṇaṃ ninditānāñca darśanam |
raktāmbaradharaṃ muṇḍaṃ paṅkāmiṣaṃ tathā vasām
lalāṭaṃ śakrajaṃ cāpamulkāpātā dhvajānanāḥ |
diśāṃ dāho mahīkampa sarajaḥ kaluṣaṃnabhaḥ
nistejāstapate bhānurnadyaḥ pratimukhāvahan |
uṣṇodakaṃ mahākūpaṃ dāruṇaṃ dīrghakāsu ca
akālavikṛtiḥ puṣpaphalānāmabhavat tadā
śīta uṣṇa virpayyāsā meghanādāśca dāruṇāḥ |
āraṇya-sattvā grāmeṣu grāmajāraṇyavāsinaḥ
kṛṣṇa sarpa samūhāśca śaśaścala pipīlikāḥ |
dhvāṃkṣāṇāṃ mahatī senā mṛgāṇāñca tathaiva ca
ete ca pura prākāre nipatanti vasanti ca |
durgandhaḥ śarkaro vāyurdīnā yodhā hata prabhāḥ
śakṛnmūtrāśrupātāni gajā aśvā pracakrire |
dhvajacchatra patākānāṃ sphuṭanaṃ daṇḍa bhedanam
kalaṅkamasi-cakreṣu nāhaitād dundubhe ravaḥ |
jyātala truṭanaṃ cāpe nārācānāñca kuṇṭatā
gadānāṃ mudgarāṇāñca śīrṇatādāya bhinnatā |
śuṣkaprarohaṇañcārkaḥ sārdrapātastathaiva ca
pratimārudat prasvedaṃ mṛtakānāñca jalpanam |
gavāṃ rāsabhamārohaḥ strīṇāñca bahvapatyatā
strī sute aviddāgādi ajamṛta suśobhanam |
bālānāṃ ghātanaṃ yuddho nistriṃśaḥ sakalāḥ prajā
makṣikādaṃśamuḍukā bahuśo nāśa darśanam |
nistejā dahane vahniḥ sadhūmaḥ sphuṭate muhuḥ
evaṃvidhāstathotpātā dṛṣṭā ghoreṇa vāsava |
prapṛccha nāradaṃ so'pi kimetacca kṛtaṃ dvija
nārada uvāca |

śailarājaḥ kṣitidhārīḥ vāsavāṃśaḥ śivātmakaḥ |
devānāṃ tā striyaḥ kanyāḥ hiyatāmasurādhipa
sāgnidevagaṇāstatra tenedamākulaṃ jagat |
prayāhi mātraṃ tvaṃ tiṣṭha kālo hi bahudoṣakṛt
tadā sa nāradenoktaḥ prayayau śīghragāmibhiḥ |
vindhyācalasya rasanā narmmadā yatra nimnagā
yatra sā vīcikallola-kala gīta -mahotsukā |
matta mātaṃga saṃghṛṣṭa taru-parvvata-saṅkulā
yatra kurarakāraṃḍa cakravākopaśobhitā |
yatra varhiṇa pārīndra kalahaṃsopanāditā
rājahaṃsa mahāvāta kāla kelīvaddiddibhaiḥ |
pārāvāta śuka siddhi sārikai rūpapāṭibhiḥ
nakraṃ matsya mahāgrāha makarākula codakā |
bhramarī sari carmmāra kala sairandhri vallikā
kāpaṭṭa mahāsena pāṭhina jhaṣarohitāḥ |
gahvarāḥ siṃha tuṇḍo jīvā jalajātayaḥ
tatra gatvā mahābāho ghorasenāvatiṣṭhata |
yatrāsau bhūdharendrāṇāṃ vindhyo nāma mahāgiriḥ
yatra dārita-mātaṅga-keśarī-nakha-muktibhiḥ |
yatra śūkara saṃghasya śūkarāśca bhayapradāḥ
khaḍgi-dvīpi-mahāganḍaiḥ rurū-mahiṣa-śalyakaiḥ |
tarakṣu-ṛkṣaśārddhūlaiḥ śākhāmṛga-mahāmṛgaiḥ
kṛṣnasāraiḥ sadācāraiśvavaradbhiḥ svecchayānvitaiḥ |
munidārakasaṃśaktaṃ satataṃ samidhānane
puṣpapatra-phalāhārā kandamūla-phalāśanāḥ |
vādyamvukaṇaśākānna pakvamāṃsasamāśanāḥ
veda-vedāṅga-tattvajñāstatkriyā dhyānatatparāḥ |
yogābhyāsaratā nityaṃ śiva-viṣṇu-parāyaṇāḥ
aneka śākhaśākhāntā nivasanti tapo'rthinaḥ |
veṇu sambhava santāna sambhūtā barbbarā varāḥ
pulīṃdāḥ śavarātaṅkāḥ kapāli mleccha jātayaḥ |
kandamūla phalāhārāḥ yatra valkala-dhāriṇaḥ
guñjābharaṇa kuṣmāḍgā mālā hārāvalamvinaḥ |
śatapatra-kṛtā voḍhā śuka-picchavibhūṣaṇāḥ
dhātu-maṇḍita-sarvāṅgā nityaṃ-mudita-mānasāḥ |
kāntāṅga krīḍanasaktāḥ karikumbha karacchidaḥ
nistriṃśaprasāśatṛṣṭi daṇḍamudgaradhāriṇaḥ |
vasanti yatra mātaṅgāḥ saṃghaśo dantadhāriṇaḥ
gṛheṣu kṛta-saṃskārāḥ śākhicchāyā kṛteṣu ca |
aśoka cūta bakulamādhavī dhanabeṇuṣu
ariṣṭa biṣṭa kapālu tamālārjjuna pādapaiḥ |
praṇaṣṭa sūryyasantāpāḥ śālatālai nabhaspṛśaiḥ
iṅgudodumbara kharjjūraiḥ mātuluṅgaiḥ sadāḍimaiḥ |
phalaistṛptiṃ prapadyante bālā mātaṅga jātayaḥ
pataṅgakara saṃghāta chāditāśca supūjitāḥ vasanti yatra nīraugha-mucaḥ saṃvarttakādayaḥ
atha tasmin mahāśaile ghorāṇīkāvatasthire |
hayena rathapādātaṃ bahudhā samāvasata
vādyacinhakhodghuṣṭā nagnabṛnda-prapīḍibhiḥ |
ajāyata mahānādaḥ sahasā giri-pūrakaḥ
kandareṣu vicitreṣu nādāḥ pratīmukhāhatāḥ |
mṛgendratoṣajanakāḥ kapisainyānuvartinī
praṇirgatā prahṛṣṭātmā vāsavāya varapradā |
vicitradāma-śobhāḍhyā bālā-bharaṇa-bhūṣitā
akrīḍata sā bālābhiḥ kanyakābhiḥ samāgatā |
mārkaṇḍaṛá¹ṣayāvāsaṃ pāpaughatamanāśanam
tatra tāmāgatāṃ dṛṣṭvā munīnāṃ sarvvasiddhidām |
ghorāharapravṛtyartha devyā hetoḥ samāgatā
dānavāpi tadā kṛṣṭāḥ kālapāśena vāsava |
śailendraṃ bodhayāmāsuḥ bhāsvarādyā mahābhaṭāḥ
aja pāde tathā ṛá¹kṣe dānavasya baruthinī |
sa cāśvina-prathamāhe girindramavarohayeta
tadā durmmukha nāmānaṃ mahābala-parākramam |
agragaḥ sarvva sainyasya pradadau sa tu dānavaḥ
tatraiva vijayā devī krīḍanāya samāgatā |
sa ca tāṃ prekṣya daityendraḥ kāmavihvalacetanaḥ
karaṃ prasārayed devyā devī tamavalokya ca |
gatāsuśca sa duṣṭātmā papāta dharaṇītale
saṃdhyāyāṃ vijayā gatvā kāraṇāya nivedavet |
āgato dānavo devi mayā sa dharaṇotsukaḥ
yāvat kraddhvā prapaśyāmi tāvat sa vigatāsavaḥ |
tat śrutvā cintayed devī ghoro hyatra samāgataḥ
ghātanīyo mayā duṣṭaḥ pūrva śāyena śāpitaḥ |
ghoro'pi svapnān paśyet niśānte śṛṇu vāsava
abhyaṅgā kaṭutailena raktāmbaravibhūṣitaḥ |
kurūṃḍakusumāmoda puṣpamālābhimālitaḥ
udvāhakaraṇaṃ prekṣya pakvamatsyāmiṣāṇi ca |
nṛtyante dānavāḥ sarvve kṛṣṇavastravibhūṣaṇāḥ
kṛṣṇāyasāḥ sālaṅkārāḥ kṛṣṇa-srag-gandhya-carccitāḥ |
kṛṣṇāmvaradhara-strībhiḥ sarva-daityā vagūhitāḥ
ūṣṭrāruḍhaistathā pumbhiḥ pāśadaṇḍodyatairmahān |
nīyate hyavaśāḥ sarvve tuṣakeśāsthisaṅkulaiḥ
tamondhakāre kāntāre paṅkakūpagatāḥ pare |
śṛgālaiḥ śvabhirbhakṣyante hyapare vigatāsavaḥ
apare vāyasairgṛdhraistarakṣairvānaraiḥ paraiḥ |
evaṃvidhairmahāsattvaiḥ mahāsainyānupādrutāna
dṛṣṭvā kṣubhito ghoraścharddhi mūrcchādi vihvalaḥ |
papāta śikharārūḍhastato bhairavarūpiṇī
jayāpuṣpakṛtā śobhā gardabhārūḍhavāhanaḥ |
asthimālā lasadgrīvā mahāśukarānanā
nirmāṃsā kekarākṣī kuddhakeśā bhayaṃṅkarī |
āgatya sahasā nārī pāśāṅkuśakarodyatā
dhūmrāyamāṇā ca tathā gṛhīto'yaṃ nirāyudhaḥ |
yāmyāya tathā nītaḥ ananta patha devalaḥ |

evaṃ dṛṣṭvā tadā ghoraḥ prabuddhaḥ śarvarīkṣaye |

ityādye śrīdevīpurāṇe ghoravadhe svapnadarśano nāma trayodaśo'dhyāyaḥ
caturdaśo'dhyāyaḥ |

indra uvāca |

evaṃvidhaistathā svapnaiḥ dṛṣṭai ghoreṇa padmaja |
prabhāte kimabhavat tasya śubhaṃ vāpyathavāśubham
kiṃ vā sā vāhinī tasya tathā mantri purohitau |
cakāra tat samākhyāhi kautūhalaparā vayam
brahmovāca |

śṛṇu vāsava tatvena vadato hyakhilaṃ mama |
utthāya sa tadā vīro devamantramanusmaran
tāvannaṣṭāḥ smṛtistasya mahāmohavimohitaḥ |
pratīkṣya vāsarāt paṃca tāvat-kālaḥ samāgataḥ
tena śrutvā hataṃ vīraṃ durmukhamarisūdanam |
śailarājendra-kanyāyā vinā kopānnirāyudhaḥ
tataḥ sa kālakālena prerito vadate'surān
kāla uvāca |

tayā nipātito vīro durmukho hyarimarddanaḥ |
tāṃ kanyāṃ kutra paśyāmi tanno vadata suvratāḥ yadi parvatarājendro rakṣate saha śaṃbhunā
tathāpi pratyanighnāmi yadi vā keśavo bhavet |
ityuktvā tadā kālaḥ pūrṇakālo mahābalaḥ
nivāritaḥ suṣeṇena mantriṇā na ca saṃsthitaḥ |
kāla-bhairava-cāmuṃḍā piṅgalākṣā mahāsurāḥ
āruhya parvataṃ vīrāstarjjayaṃstāṃ ca kanyakām |
tān dṛṣṭvā uṣṭrāruḍhān kecit syandana-saṃsthitāḥ
jayā ca aśvamārohat gajamiva mahābalam |
kṛpāṇa pāṇinī tarjya tadā kālaṃ mahābalam
māyārūpaṃ surāstrajñaṃ yuddhaśāstra-viśāradam |
māyotthaṃ nirmmame siṃhaṃ gajarājabhayaṅkaram
mahiṣaṃ ca mahāghoraṃ yamasya iva vāhanaṃ |
bhairavaṃ taṃ samāsthāya vijayāmabhimardayet
yamāntakastathā raudraṃ vibhuṃ prahlāda-dundubhiḥ |
ajitāṃ mṛgamārūḍhāṃ mardayet sahasā tadā
vāmanairduṣṭa-lobhākṣairhālāhala-bhayaṅkaraiḥ |
daśadhā veṣṭitā devī yā sā nāmnāparājitā
daśadhā śatadhā caiva tathāyutāthalakṣadhā |
nigūḍhajaṃtavaḥ śakra devāḥ paśyanti śaṅkitāḥ
tataḥkarṇika-nārāca-bhuṣuṇḍi mudgaraistathā |
vavarṣa dānavī senā devīnāṃ sahasopari
tadā jayā tu saṃkruddhā śarapātena pīḍitā |
prāsaṃ prakṣepayet kāle tasyāḥ siṃha nipātanam
taṃ prāsaghātāhata-chinnabandhaṃ nistriṃ śamādāya tadā tu kālaḥ |
carmmeṇa vāmaṃ bhuja pūrayitvā jayāmukho'dhāvata kruddha kopāt
dṛṣṭvā tu kālaṃ sahasā patantaṃ kṛpāṇapāṇiṃ suvivṛddha-manyum |
jayā mumocopari tasya śaktiṃ kṛpāṇa-ghātādapi tāṃ jaghāna
śaktiṃ hatāṃ paśya tadā jayā tu nārāca-dhārā jala vāri vāhaiḥ |
kālasya senopari sā vavarṣa kālo'pi bhinnaḥ śatavāraṇaghātaiḥ
sa devighātāhata bhū-niṣaṇṇo labdhvā tu ceṣṭāṃ suvisrabdha cetā |
ādāya vajrāśani vajrakopaḥ khuraṃ pramumoca sutīkṣṇadhāram
tamāpatantaṃ tu devī śarebhyaściccheda yānyānyapi tasya moca |
ekena yānamapareṇa aśvānanyena chatraṃ sapatākadaṇḍam
ciccheda sā kāla mahābalasya devīṃ śaraistasya vivṛddhamanyuḥ |
tathāpi kālo gadatāṃ mumoca devīmukho dhāvituṃ sampravṛttaḥ
cakreṇa taṃ kāla bhaṭasya taṃtaṃ devī vimuktena gatā svabhūmau |
kālaṃ hataṃ bhairava sannirīkṣya niṣaṇṇamṛtyuḥ sa vivṛddhamanyuḥ
gadāṃ samādāya jayāṃ pravṛttaḥ kharapraghātādapi so gatāyuḥ |
evaṃ sa kālo hata-bhairavañca cāmuṇḍapiṃgākṣa mahābalaśca
māyāvino mattamataṅgarūpā devyā samāsādya jvalantakopāḥ |
te devi vāṇāśani bhinnarakṣā gatāsavaḥ pretapathaṃ prayātāḥ
evaṃ hate kālabale aśeṣe devā mumocopari puṣpavṛṣṭim |
meghāśca śītojvalavārivindūn vātā vavāhāpi divyagandhāḥ
nṛtyanti vidyādhara-siddha-saṃghā mahāpsarā-kinnara-cāraṇāśca |

iti śrīdevīpurāṇe devyavatāre kālavadhonāma caturdaśo'dhyāyaḥ
caturdaśo'dhyāyaḥ |

indra uvāca |

evaṃvidhaistathā svapnaiḥ dṛṣṭai ghoreṇa padmaja |
prabhāte kimabhavat tasya śubhaṃ vāpyathavāśubham
kiṃ vā sā vāhinī tasya tathā mantri purohitau |
cakāra tat samākhyāhi kautūhalaparā vayam
brahmovāca |

tena śrutvā hataṃ vīraṃ durmukhamarisūdanam |
śailarājendra-kanyāyā vinā kopānnirāyudhaḥ
tataḥ sa kālakālena prerito vadate'surān
kāla uvāca |

tayā nipātito vīro durmukho hyarimarddanaḥ |
tāṃ kanyāṃ kutra paśyāmi tanno vadata suvratāḥ yadi parvatarājendro rakṣate saha śaṃbhunā
tathāpi pratyanighnāmi yadi vā keśavo bhavet |
ityuktvā tadā kālaḥ pūrṇakālo mahābalaḥ
nivāritaḥ suṣeṇena mantriṇā na ca saṃsthitaḥ |
kāla-bhairava-cāmuṃḍā piṅgalākṣā mahāsurāḥ
āruhya parvataṃ vīrāstarjjayaṃstāṃ ca kanyakām |
tān dṛṣṭvā uṣṭrāruḍhān kecit syandana-saṃsthitāḥ
jayā ca aśvamārohat gajamiva mahābalam |
kṛpāṇa pāṇinī tarjya tadā kālaṃ mahābalam
māyārūpaṃ surāstrajñaṃ yuddhaśāstra-viśāradam |
māyotthaṃ nirmmame siṃhaṃ gajarājabhayaṅkaram
mahiṣaṃ ca mahāghoraṃ yamasya iva vāhanaṃ |
bhairavaṃ taṃ samāsthāya vijayāmabhimardayet
yamāntakastathā raudraṃ vibhuṃ prahlāda-dundubhiḥ |
ajitāṃ mṛgamārūḍhāṃ mardayet sahasā tadā
vāmanairduṣṭa-lobhākṣairhālāhala-bhayaṅkaraiḥ |
daśadhā veṣṭitā devī yā sā nāmnāparājitā
daśadhā śatadhā caiva tathāyutāthalakṣadhā |
nigūḍhajaṃtavaḥ śakra devāḥ paśyanti śaṅkitāḥ
tataḥkarṇika-nārāca-bhuṣuṇḍi mudgaraistathā |
vavarṣa dānavī senā devīnāṃ sahasopari
tadā jayā tu saṃkruddhā śarapātena pīḍitā |
prāsaṃ prakṣepayet kāle tasyāḥ siṃha nipātanam
taṃ prāsaghātāhata-chinnabandhaṃ nistriṃ śamādāya tadā tu kālaḥ |
carmmeṇa vāmaṃ bhuja pūrayitvā jayāmukho'dhāvata kruddha kopāt
dṛṣṭvā tu kālaṃ sahasā patantaṃ kṛpāṇapāṇiṃ suvivṛddha-manyum |
jayā mumocopari tasya śaktiṃ kṛpāṇa-ghātādapi tāṃ jaghāna
śaktiṃ hatāṃ paśya tadā jayā tu nārāca-dhārā jala vāri vāhaiḥ |
kālasya senopari sā vavarṣa kālo'pi bhinnaḥ śatavāraṇaghātaiḥ
sa devighātāhata bhū-niṣaṇṇo labdhvā tu ceṣṭāṃ suvisrabdha cetā |
ādāya vajrāśani vajrakopaḥ khuraṃ pramumoca sutīkṣṇadhāram
tamāpatantaṃ tu devī śarebhyaściccheda yānyānyapi tasya moca |
ekena yānamapareṇa aśvānanyena chatraṃ sapatākadaṇḍam
ciccheda sā kāla mahābalasya devīṃ śaraistasya vivṛddhamanyuḥ |
tathāpi kālo gadatāṃ mumoca devīmukho dhāvituṃ sampravṛttaḥ
cakreṇa taṃ kāla bhaṭasya taṃtaṃ devī vimuktena gatā svabhūmau |
kālaṃ hataṃ bhairava sannirīkṣya niṣaṇṇamṛtyuḥ sa vivṛddhamanyuḥ
gadāṃ samādāya jayāṃ pravṛttaḥ kharapraghātādapi so gatāyuḥ |
evaṃ sa kālo hata-bhairavañca cāmuṇḍapiṃgākṣa mahābalaśca
māyāvino mattamataṅgarūpā devyā samāsādya jvalantakopāḥ |
te devi vāṇāśani bhinnarakṣā gatāsavaḥ pretapathaṃ prayātāḥ
evaṃ hate kālabale aśeṣe devā mumocopari puṣpavṛṣṭim |
meghāśca śītojvalavārivindūn vātā vavāhāpi divyagandhāḥ
nṛtyanti vidyādhara-siddha-saṃghā mahāpsarā-kinnara-cāraṇāśca |

iti śrīdevīpurāṇe devyavatāre kālavadhonāma caturdaśo'dhyāyaḥ

pañcadaśo'dhyāyaḥ |

hate kāle kālabala prabhāve suhṛṣṭa devāḥ saha vāsavena |

śakra uvāca |

jaya jaya surāṇāṃ paritrāṇabhūte mahāhare saṅgarasupratāpe |
samasta bhītān parirakṣaṇāya tvāṃ devīṃ muktvā aparo na cāsti
mahābalaṃ ghorabalaṃ pradhānaṃ yamasya vahnera'pi saṃcitāram |
vayaṃ sabrāhmaṇāḥ savāyuyakṣāstvayā punardevi divaṃ niviṣṭāḥ
sarve'pi bhītā bhavatīṃ praṇamya bhayebhya muñcantyavicāraṇena |
mahārṇave siṃha-gajābhi bhūtāstvāmāśritā vītabhayā bhavanti
jvālaughakālānala-sampravṛddhaṃ yaṃ brahmaviṣṇorapi mohakarttā |
taṃ prekṣya devī sahasā mahāntaṃ samaṃ gataṃ prāvṛṣiṇeva pāṃśu
yaṃ dundubhiḥ brahmajanārddanaiśca na nirjjitaṃ bhāskara-vāyu-yakṣaiḥ |
jalesarakṣaiḥ sahasā vibheti taṃ devī dṛṣṭvā bhasmīprayātam
tvaṃ bhūmi vāyu kha jalaṃ hutāśaṃ diśo divaṃ sāgara ṛkṣacakram |
yāṃ sarvvadevāḥ satataṃ namanti tāṃ devadevīṃ śaraṇaṃ vrajāmi
yāṃ dhyānayogairapi yogaśavatyā dhyāyanti nityaṃ paratattva devīm |
vedānta vādī satataṃ ca kṛtsnāṃ yāṃ yājino nityamaśveṣu yajvāḥ
yāṃ sāṃkhyayogaiḥ sapatañjalākhyaiḥ siddhānta-mantrairapi mantravādī |
yā ḍākinī bhūtagrahaiḥ praśastān sattvān samastānapi mocayeti
na cādirasya na ca madhyamantaṃ na rūpakāntirna ca stotramanyat |
yāṃ śaṃṅkaraḥ sarvvagato'pi satauti tāṃ devadevīṃ śaraṇaṃ prapadye
evaṃ tāṃ toṣayāñcakre jayāṃ kālanivarhaṇām |
pradadau sā varaṃ tasya devarājasya vāsava
idaṃ ghorabalaṃ hatvā bhūyo'pi surasattamaḥ |
tava puṣṭiṃ kariṣyāmi sarvvakālaṃ purandara
yo hyetadvijayā stotraṃ bhaktitaḥ sampaṭhiṣyati |
praṇaṣṭa-rājyadravyāṇi punareva labhiṣyati
brahmovāca |

śrutvā hataṃ tadā kālaṃ bhairavaṃ piṅgalam |
vajradaṇḍastadā kruddho devyā yoddhuṃ vyadhāvata
pāśa-mudgaradaṇḍābja kunta-bāṇa-kṛpāṇabhṛt |
vavarṣa sahasā bajraḥ prāvṛṇmegha ivāmvubhiḥ
na diśo na tadākāśaṃ na ca bhūvāyugocaram |
lakṣyate bāṇadhārodhairvajradaṇḍamahādhvanaiḥ
devyā dhanuṣi vajreṇa śarāḥ pañcāśat preritāḥ |
tairvividhya dhanurdevyā kopānala-sudīpitā
vimokṣe vāruṇaṃ śastraṃ mahāmegha-samaprabham |
taṃ nadantaṃ mahāghoraṃ vidyutpūrvvāṃ diśo daśa
vavarṣa plavate sarbvā dānavīṃ vāhinīṃ tadā |
taṃ dṛṣṭvā vajradaṇḍedaṃ mahāmāyā-samudbhavam |
vāyuṃ mumoca meghānāṃ tena te śamitā ghanāḥ
dṛṣṭvā ghanān vajrānilena śāntān devī tadā krodhavivṛddhamanyuḥ |
meghādrimālā iva droṇatulyān sabhūdharān sarvvadiśo vicikṣipe
taṃ vāyuśastraṃ sahasā nirudhya vajrāśaniṃ rvāṇa-śilā vavarṣaiḥ |
hatvā tadaśvān yadarakṣarakṣam saṃsārathiṃ chatra dharaṃ ca daṇḍam
jighāṃsa vajraṃ vala-vajra-vīryyam śareṇa hemadala patritena |
hatantu vajraṃ sahasā ca dṛṣṭvā yamāntako yatra jayā jayantam
mumoca vāṇān sahasā sakopāt devyāhataḥ so'pi paraṃ prayāti yamāntakaḥ pretapathaṃ mahāntam

stutā hyevaṃ purā devī devadevena śambhunā |

vavarṣu puṣpamālābhirbhavānyāścaraṇāmbuje

devī-kara-vimuktena lāghavena balena ca
niśceṣṭaṃ dānavaṃ sainyaṃ tadā hyāsīt purandara |
evaṃ kātyāyanīṃ vāṇairniṣprabhaṃ ghorajaṃ balam

suṣeṇastu tadā kruddho manyumāsthāya vāsava

yāṃ yāṃ cakāra daityendro māyāṃ māyāvidāṃ varaḥ |

śakti-traya-samopetaḥ pauruṣeṇa samanvitaḥ |

śakra uvāca |

yadā hi balavān daiva ekaḥ śatruvalaṃ jayet |
tadā gajāśvayodhānāṃ vyarthatā hyanumīyate
na dharmmo nāpi cādharmmo na mantrī na purohitaḥ |
daiva eva hi karttā tu śubhāśubhaphalapravaḥ
aśvamedhādi yajñā ye brahmahatyādi pātakāḥ |
daiva eva hi karttā ca na puṇyaṃ na ca dīṣabhāk
bhiṣak samvat sarāmādyai rna hi kiñcit prayojanam |
kṛṣi karmmānu vārtā ca daivaṃ sarvvaṃ karoti hi
yadetat kathanārambhe devyā ādyavatāraṇam |
tata karoti vidhirbrahman kimetad bhavatā kṛtam
anenaivānumānena śuśrūṣā vinayena hi |

evaṃ pūrvvaṃ bhavānāsīt cakra brahmasya daivike

brahmovāca |

daivo hi sarvva-śaktīnāṃ balānāṃ paramaṃ balam
cintyāḥ anya padārthāḥ syurdaivaṃ kenāpi cintyatām |
daivānukūlatā śakra śakti pauruṣa ceṣṭitam
phalate sarvvalokānāṃ kṛṣervṛṣṭiriva dvayam |
tathāpi pauruṣaṃ śakra yatitavyaṃ jigīṣuṇā
nahi śayyāgatāṃ kāntāṃ daivamevāvagūhate |
tasmāt puruṣakāro'pi sidhyatyeva niyāmitaḥ
tathāpi śakti yuktena balāyato samanvitaiḥ |
paraṃ puruṣakārasya yatitavyaṃ sadā vibho
deva dānava gandharvvā ṛṣayo mānavāḥ surāḥ sarvve daivavaśāḥ śakra daivo'pi hi śivā matā
sa ca dānava rūpeṇa deva rūpeṇa vāsava |
sthityutpatti vināśāya brahma-viṣṇu-śivā tanuḥ
nānā rūpadharā bhūtvā sarvvaṃ haṃti karoti ca |
tenemāṃ dānavīṃ māyāṃ ghoro ghorāṃ pracakrame
evaṃ brahmā purā śakra śakreṇa samabhāṣata |
yāvat sā vāhinī devyā dānavena vimardditā
tathāstaṃ prāpite sūrye sandhyāyāṃ samupasthitā |
ajitā sarvvaṃdevānāmabhayāya ca preṣitā
brahma viṣṇivandrarudrāṇāṃ yoganidrā ca sā smṛtā |
sā rakṣā paramā bhūtā kāla-vandhana-kārikā
tathāgatā mahādevī devatā rakṣaṇe niśi |
kālo'pi sārddhayāme tu yāmini vigate vibho
anekākāriṇo bhūtvā bahumāyo mahābalaḥ |
prāvṛṭkāle samārambhe kālanīlānilaprabhuḥ
raktākṣo bhairavākāraḥ surāsurabhayaṅkaraḥ |
yamavāhanakoṭīnāṃ sahyaiveko vinirmitaḥ
tasya sañcaramānasya kampate ca vasundharā |
nimnonnatāni kurute bhayaṃ jagmuḥ surāsurāḥ
ghoro mahāghora tanuṃ vidhāya devyā samaṃ jagmurmahāhavāya |
saṃkruddhakālā naladīptatatejāṃ tāṃ paśyate siṃhavare niviṣṭām
bhayāni kurvvan danijādhipasya surādhipe cābhayarūparūpām |
daityāntakīṃ sṛṣṭikarīṃ surāṇāmālokya devīṃ sahasā tu ghoraḥ
pādānta randhreṣu girīn sa kṛtvā candrārkatārāṇiśire dhvanitvā |
siṃhena yoddhuṃ sahasā pravṛttaḥ siṃhe'pi tañjāṅghranaravaiviṃvidhya
nakhaprahārairmahiṣasya kāye asṛk pravāhaugha-vinirgatā ye |
divaukasaistaiḥ sahasā pradiṣṭāṃ kuruṇḍa mālā iva vadhya-kāye
tad ghora-śṛṅgāgra-prahāra-bhinno harirnanāda sahasā ca rivannaḥ |
saṃkopitaṃ daitya-nipāta-ghātairhariḥ prajaghne narava-daṃṣṭra-ghātaiḥ
devyāḥ śire mudgarapāśaghātāt vahūn mumoca śara-daṇḍa-ghātān |
tathāpi no vādhayituṃ sa śaktaḥ pañcānanaḥ śṛṅgahataḥ papāta
taṃ ghoraghātāhata-siṃha-rājaṃ bhūmau gataṃ ghora bhaṭaiḥ pradṛṭṣvā |
te dānavāḥ krodhavaśaṃ prapannā devītanāvastravarāṇi cikṣipuḥ
dṛṣṭvā tu devīṃ taiḥ pīḍitāṅgī nivārayetām vijayā jayā ca |
nivārite ghorabale samaste māyāsamutthe tamapāyarupe
devī kṛpāṇena tamāpatantaṃ ciccheda grīvāṃ dharaṇīṃ nipātya |
dṛṣṭvā surāstaṃ nihataṃ surāriṃ puṣpāṇi devī caraṇeṣu cikṣipuḥ
tasya śiraścheda-samudbhavantaṃ raktānanaṃ raktavilocanāntam |
kruddhānanaṃ mukta-kacaṃ sughoraṃ kṛpāṇapāṇiṃ śata-ghora-kāram
devyānanaṃ tarjjana garjjamānaṃ śaṅkāvahaṃ nirbhaya devatānām |
taṃ dṛṣṭamātraṃ sahasā tu devīṃ pāśena saṃpāśya mumoca nainaṃ
śūlena mūrdhni sahasā vibhinnaṃ taṃ muktavīra mapatad gṛhītam |
ṛkṣādhipe cāstagate'sureśe daityādhipāḥ pretapathaṃ prajagmuḥ
iti śrī devī purāṇe devyavatāre ghokavadho nāma viṃśo'dhyāyaḥ

brahmovāca |

samayena ṛtumāsa pakṣāhādi kramena tu |
sūkṣma-sthūla-vibhāgena devī sarvvagatā vibho
dvādaśaiva samākhyātā samā saṃkrāntikalpanāḥ |
saptadhā sā tu boddhavyā ekekaiva yathā śṛṇu
mandā mandākinī dhvāṃkṣī ghorā caiva mahodarī |
rākṣasī miśritā proktā saṃkrāntiḥ saptadhā nṛpa
mandā dhruveṣu vijñeyā mṛdau mandākinī tathā |
kṣipre dhvāṅkṣīṃ vijānīyādugrairghorā prakīrtitā
carairmahodarī jñeyā krūrairṛkṣaistu rākṣasī |
miśritā caiva nirdiṣṭā miśritākṣaistu saṃkrame
tricatuḥ pañca saptāṣṭa nava dvādaśameva ca |
krameṇa ghaṭitā hyetāstatpuṇyaṃ pāramārthikam
atītānāgatān bhogān ādyaḥ paṃcadaśa smṛtāḥ |
sānnidhyaṃ bhavate tatra grahāṇāṃ saṃkrame ravau
vyavahāro bhavelloke candrasūryopalakṣitaḥ |
kālo'pi kalate sarvva brahmādya sacarācaram
puṇya-pāpa-vibhāgena phalaṃ devī prayacchati |
ekadhāpi kṛtaṃ tasmin koṭi koṭi guṇaṃ bhavet
dharmmo vivarddhate hyāyū rājyaṃ putra sukhāni ca |
adharmma vyādhi śokādi viṣuvāyana sannidhau
viṣuveṣu ca yajjaptaṃ dattaṃ bhavati cākṣayam |
evaṃ viṣṇu pade caiva ṣaḍaśīti mukheṣu ca
ayaneṣu vikalpo yastanme nigadataḥ śṛṇu |
yāvadviṃśakalā bhuṃkte tat puṇyamuttarāyaṇe
niraṃśe bhāskare dṛṣṭe dinānte dakṣiṇāyane |
arddharātre tu sampūrṇe divā puṇyamanāgatam
sampūrṇe cārddharātre tu udayāstamane'pi ca |
mānārddha bhāskaraṃ puṇyamapūrṇe śarvvarīdine
ṣaḍaśītimukhe'tīte vṛtte ca viṣuvad vaye
arddharātre vyatīte tu vijñeyā cāpare'hani |
mandā viprajane śastā mandākinyastu rājani
dhvāṃkṣī vaiśyeṣu vijñeyā ghoraśūdre śubhāvahā |
mahodarī tu caurāṇāṃ śoṇḍikānāṃ jayāvahā
cāṇḍāla-pukvaśānāntu ye cānye krūrakarmiṇaḥ |
sarveṣāṃ kārukāṇāñca miśritā dhṛtivarddhinī
nṛpān pīḍati pūrvvāhṇe madhyāhṇe ca dvijottamān |
aparāhṇe tu sā vaiśyāñchūdrānastamane raveḥ
piśācāṃśca pradoṣe tu arddharātre tu rākṣasān |
arddharātre vyatīte tu pīḍyante naṭanartakīḥ
uṣaḥkāle tu saṃkrāntau hanti go svāmino janān |
hanti pravrajitān sarvvān sandhyākāle na saṃśayaḥ
etat sthūla vibhāgantu bhakti kāmasya kīrtitam |
paramārthena yā saṃkhyā kathayāmi nṛpottama
susthe nare sukhāsīne yāvat spandati locanam |
tasya triṃśattamaṃ bhāgaṃ tatparaṃ parikīrtitam
tat parācchatabhāgaṃ tu truṭirityabhidhīyate |
truṭyāḥ sahasrabhāgārddhaṃ tatkālaṃ ravi-saṃkrame
tat kāleṣu dravībhūtaṃ trailokyaṃ sacarācaram |
vyatīpāte'pi syād bhavet puṇyaṃ samādhikam
tatra brahmāpi sandigdhamuvāca surasattama |
dānādhyayanajāpādi viśiṣṭaṃ ghora homataḥ
vasorddhārāsu labhyeta anyathā na kathañcana |
devīkālagatā vatsa yathā sūkṣmaṃ prakīrtitā
sādhakī sarvvakāmāṇāṃ mahābhaya vināśinī |
kathitā te matā sā tu kiṃ bhūyaḥ paripṛcchasi
iti śrī devīpurāṇe saṃkrāntividhirnāma caturvviṃśo'dhyāyaḥ
pañcaviṃśo'dhyāyaḥ |

vidyādhara uvāca |

yathā sā sarvagā devī sarvveṣāñca phalapradā |
tathāhaṃ śrotumicchāmi vasorddhārāṃ suvistarām
agastya uvāca |

brahmaṇā yā samākhyātā devarājasya pṛcchataḥ |
vidhiśca pāpahā śrotuḥ śṛṇuṣvāvahito mama
vasorddhārā sthitā devī sarvvakāma pradāyikā |
tathā te kathayiṣyāmi śṛṇu puṇyavivṛddhaye
sarveṣāmeva devānāṃ kathitā devī cottamā |
viśeṣeṇa tu vahṇisthā āyurārogyadā matā
vijayaṃ bhūmilābhantu priyatvaṃ sarvvamānavān |
vidyā-saubhāgya putrādi kuṇḍasthā saṃprayacchati
tasmān nṛpeṇa bhūrtyarthe vasorddhārāśritā śivā |
pūjanīyā yathā śaktyā caṇḍī kāmaphalapradā
rudrādityā grahā viṣṇurvayaṃ yakṣāḥ sakinnarāḥ |
hutāśanamukhāḥ sarvve dṛṣṭādṛṣṭa-phala-pradāḥ
godānaṃ bhūdānañca ratnaṃ sarpistalāni ca |
dānāni mahatānyāhusteṣāṃ dhārā viśiṣyate
viprāṇāṃ koṭikoṭīnāṃ bhojayitvā tu yat phalat |
tadvṛtta-nirataiḥ śāntairekenāpi ca tadbhavet
vyatīpāte na sandehaḥ sa ca sūkṣmaḥ prakīrtitaḥ |
ayane viṣuvaccaiva dinacchidraṃ tathaiva ca
duṣprāpaṃ dānaṃ homānāṃ dhārāyāṃ labhate nṛpaḥ |
tasmān nṛpeṇa vṛddhyartha dṛṣṭvādṛṣṭa jigīṣuṇā
vasorddhārā prakarttavyā sarvakāmaṃ jayāvahā |
samaṃ vā athavārddha vā ṛtumāsārddhavāsaram
kṛtvā vibhavarūpeṇa śāśvataṃ labhate phalam |
ekāhamapi yo devīṃ kalpayitvā hutāśane
pātayet sarpiṣo dhārāṃ sa labhatepsitaṃ phalam |
devī-mātṛ-samīpasthaṃ śiva-viṣṇu-samīpagam
bhānoḥ prajāpatervāpi vasorddhārā gṛhe bhavet |
guhāsu ca vicitrāsu gṛhagarbheṣu bhūmiṣu |
dattvā samīhitān kāmān vidhinā labhate nṛpaḥ
atha sāmānyato gehaṃ samasūtraṃ janonmukham |
vāstusaṃśuddhi-vinyāptamekādaśakaraṃ param
trīṇi pañcātha saptā vā daśa vā nava kārayet |
viṃśaikaṃ vā vahunāṃ vātriṃśadūrdhvaṃ na kārayet
pakveṣṭaṃ śailadārvva vā saliṅgaṃ sahatoraṇam |
pañca sapta navāsyaṃ vā gavākṣaka vibhūṣitam
sarvvato bhadravinyastaṃ krama vṛddhayāvivakṣitam |
ūrdhvadhūmasya niṣkāsaṃ saprakāśaṃ viśeṣataḥ
iti śrī devīpurāṇe toraṇavidhirnāma pañcaviṃśo'dhyāyaḥ
ṣaḍviṃśo'dhyāyaḥ |

brahmovāca |

sadaivaṃ sagrahaṃ kāryyamathavā deva toraṇam |
tasya madhye bhavet kuṇḍaṃ hastādilakṣaṇānvitam
catuṣkamatha vṛttaṃ vā paṅkajākṛti cātha vā |
pṛthivī jayadaṃ śakra vṛttaṃ kāmaphalapradam
paṅkaje jayamārogyaṃ yoga-jñāna-pradāyakam |
śeṣāḥ kāryavibhāgena kuṇḍāḥ kāryyā vijānatā
sāmānyaṃ sarvvahomeṣu śakra kuṇḍaṃ varottamam |
vistāraṃ khātatulyantu mekhalaistribhirbhūṣitam
catvāri trīṇi dve kuryyādaṅgula kuṇḍamānataḥ |
dviguṇān dviguṇe kuṇḍe homa mātreṇa kārayet
evaṃ saṃsādhayedvipra stutaḥ pātraṃ saśṛṃkhalam |
haimaṃ vā rājataṃ vāpi tāmraṃ vā lakṣaṇānvitam
catvāri kaṭakopetamayaḥ śṛṃkhala saṃgraham |
tasya madhye bhavedrandhraṃ karṇārddhasya śalākayā
homotthayā pramāṇena caturaṅgulamānayā |
dhṛtaniṣkramaṇārthāya kuryyāt samyak vipaścitaḥ
palairdaśabhirarddhonyairnānyekāntu mayā brajeta |
pañcabhistu śatairhomaḥ saptatyā ca ṣaḍasrayā
yathā pūrṇā brajed vatsa tathā kuryyānna cānyathā |
hastamātraṃ bhaved haimaṃ śṛṃkhalaṃ bhujagākṛti
randhre sūtranibaddhañca avalambya adhastanam |
maṇiṃ vā paṅkajaṃ pātramāśvatthaṃ kārayet tale
evaṃ kāryyānurūpeṇa dviguṇaṃ triguṇaṃ pivā |
kuryyāt pātraṃ dhṛtaṃ vedhaṃ pratiṣṭhā-vidhivoditama
uddeśaṃ kiñcidatrāpi kathayāmi nṛpotama |
samāyana ṛturmāsa pakṣāhorātra pūrvvavat
lagnādi viśodhayed vatsa sarvvakāma pradā yathā |
kṣaṇikeṣu ca kāryyeṣu bharktiyuktaṃ kṣaṇe śubhe
kṣaṇaṃ devī ca draṣṭavyā yathā sarvvagatā śivā |
tattvabhūtā grahā nāgāstriguṇāpi śivā guṇāḥ
nitye naimittike home mantrayogena dāpayet |
yī yasya bhaktimāsaktastasya kuryyāt tu sannidhim
sagrahān lokapālāmÌstu mātarā bhujagaṃ pivā |
kalpayet sarvvahomeṣu devī etairvyavasthitā
sthūlarūpā tu taistuṣṭaistuṣṭā devī mahāphalā |
kālādibali gandhādi pratiṣṭhāvacca kārayet
yadā sampatti sampannaḥ sarvakāle pradāpayet |
tadā mantra-graha-bhūtān lokapālān niveśayet
haima rājata tāmrā vā sunive śopalakṣitā |
vastra puṣpavalirgandhadakṣiṇādi yathākramam
mātaraṃ lokapālānāṃ grahāṇāñca yathāvidhi |
hṛdayena pradeyantu mūlamantraiḥ purātanaiḥ
athavā sarvvasāmānyāṃ vaidikāmapi kārayet |
atharvva vidhinā vatsa pūrvoktā vā yathā purā
prabhūta-mantra-naivedyai rbhūri-dakṣiṇa-saṃyutaiḥ |
kuryyānmahāprayatnena anyathā na kathañcana
chede bhayaṃ vijānīyāt tadartha tanna kārayet |
sahasrāhuti homena yatra tatra niveśayet
mūla mantreṇa devyāyāḥ śṛṃkhalā hṛdayena tu |
kavacena tathā vahṇiṃ rakṣayitvā pradāpayet |
aśvamedhena mantreṇa sarvva sarvvāsu nikṣipet
lokapālān grahān-nāgān dvādaśārddhena pūjayet |
śivādyān sanakādyāṃśca devādyānapi pūjayet
nityeṣu ca mahā prājña naimitteṣu viśeṣataḥ |
pañcakāni ca saptādi navakāni kriyādikaiḥ
agre varṇāśca gandhaśca śabdāścākṛtayastathā |
vikārāśca tathā vatsa boddhavyāḥ siddhyasiddhidāḥ
tadante ca stavaṃ kārya sarvvakāmapradāyakam |
yena sānnidhyamāyārti sarvvahomeṣu maṅgalā
sahasrārcci mahātejā namaste bahurūpiṇe |
nīlakaṇṭha śitikaṇṭha pītavāsāya pāvane
sruvamekhaladhārāya brahmaṇe dahane namaḥ |
sarvvāśine sarvvabhartre pāvakāya namo namaḥ
durgāya umārūpāya strīliṅgāya sutejase |
vasu aśvinarūpāya sarvāhārāya vai namaḥ
tvaṃ rudra ghorakarmāsi ghorahā parameśvaraḥ |
viṣṇustavaṃ jagatāṃ pālo brahmā sṛṣṭikaraḥ smṛtaḥ
tvañca sarvārthako deva yamāya piśitāśine |
varuṇānilāya somāya īśadevāya vai namaḥ
sūryyāya cātriputrāya bhūsutāya budhāya ca |
bṛhaspataye śukrāya śani rāho'tha ketave
sarvvage graharūpāya vyāla mātaṅga rūpiṇe |
vṛṣṭi sṛṣṭi sthitirbhūti karttāya varadāya ca
namaste skanda mātastvaṃ pitre cāpi namo namaḥ |
kuṇḍe vā maṇḍale vāpi sthaṃḍile vāpi tvaṃ vibho
mahānase vā tvāṃ deva hutvā iṣṭaṃ labhennaraḥ |
ghṛta-kṣīra-rasa-dhānya-tila-brīhi-yavān kuśān
bhāvādabhāvato vāpi satataṃ homayedanale |
evaṃ vidhivihīno'pi naro vigatakilviṣaḥ
rki punarnityahomaṃ tu vasorddhārā hutāśane |
sarvva maṅgala mantreṇa pūrṇāhutiṃ pradāpayet
lokapāla grahāṇāṃ tu oṃkāreṇa namo'tiṃkaiḥ |
svaiḥ svairmantraistu śeṣāṇāṃ homaṃ kāryyaṃ nṛpottama
annaṃ vicitraṃ śuṣkañca saṃskṛtaṃ ghṛtapāyasaiḥ |
homayedvidhivad vipro baliñcāpi pradāpayeta
sitavastradharo bhūpaḥ sabalaḥ sahavāhanaḥ |
pūjayet śambhuṃ rudrādīn mātaraṃ pitaraṃ dvijīn
ācāryyān brāhmaṇāṃ llokān sarvvāśramaratāśca ye |
naṭa-narttaka-veśyāśca kanyakā vidhavāḥ striyaḥ
dīnāndha-kṛpaṇāṃścaiva annadānena pūjayet |
evaṃ niveśanaṃ kṛtvā nityaṃ japyaṃ śataṃ śatam
prātarmadhyāhna saṃdhyāyāṃ stavaṃ śāntiṃ prakīrttanam |
bhavate nṛparāṣṭrasya pūrvoktaṃ phaladāyakam
iti śrī devīpurāṇe vasorddhārā-niveśanavidhiḥ nāma ṣaḍviṃśo'dhyāyaḥ |

saptaviṃśo'dhyāyaḥ |

brahmovāca |

taptahāṭakavarṇena sūryya-sindūra-kānti kṛta |
śaṅkhakundendū-padbhābho ghṛta-kṣīra nibhaḥ śubhaḥ
javābho'śoka-puṣpābho lākṣādara samanvitaḥ |
śubhadaḥ sarvvakāryāṇāṃ viparīto hyasiddhidaḥ
meghadundubhi-śaṅkhānāṃ veṇuvīṇā-svanaḥ śubhaḥ |
vṛṣendra nṛpa kākānāṃ kokilā-svana pūjitaḥ
kuṃkumāguru-karpūrasita-gandhi ca pūjitaḥ |
haṃsachatrebha-gokumbha padmākṛtikaraḥ śubhaḥ
siṃha-varhiṇa-śyenānāṃ cāmarā kṛtiriṣṭidaḥ |
sadhūmo mṛtagandhā ca mūkaḥṣaḍvaramopamaḥ
chinna jvālo'tha vā raudro neṣṭaḥ sarvveṣu pāvakaḥ |
susaṃhataśikhaḥ śakra ūrddhvaṃ vāte'pi yāti yaḥ
lelihānaḥ śubhaḥ kuṇḍo dīptimān varado'nalaḥ |
evaṃvidhaḥ sadā pārtha yajñenaivāha sthāpanaiḥ
yātrāyāṃ śakraketau ca sarvvakāryeṣu siddhidaḥ |
nyūnā yā vaheta dhārā mānāt sarpirna sā śubhā
nādhikā śasyate vipra durbhikṣa-kali-kārikā |
nudate vahamānā yā śasate ca hutāśanam
sāpi cānyaṃ nṛpamicchet yāvad ghorāyate bhuvi |
ṛá¹junādī mahārūpā manojñā priyakārikā
suvarṇā hemavarṇā ca dhārā rājya-vivṛddhaye |
satataṃ patate yātu tanotība ca pāvakam
tanoti nṛparāṣṭraṃ sā vasorddhārā na saṃśayaḥ |
sugandhi svacchaṃ vimalaṃ kṛmi-kīṭa-vivarjjitam
śasyate ca vasorddhārā sarpirgavyantu pūjitam |
abhāvād gavyalājaṃ vā hotavyantu suśobhanam
ghṛtakṣaudra payodhārā sarvapīḍā nivāriṇī |
guḍvīśa-kalairhomaṃ sahakāradalaiḥ śubhaiḥ
aśvatthā mālatī dūrvvā āyurārogyaputradā |
saubhāgyañca śriyaṃ devī prayacchatyavicāraṇāt
arkādi vā śubhā vatsa saphalā sarvvakāmikā |
hotavyā sarvakālantu mātarādavicchedinī
sarvvakālaṃ vṛtaṃ proktaṃ nimitte cātmavittamaḥ |
viśuddhi sarpiṣā yāni tāni nātra vicārayet
jvālā varṇa śubhaṃ gandhaṃ sarvvahomeṣu lakṣayet |
saṃyato saṃyatāhāraiḥ sarvvaśāstrārthapāragaiḥ
japa homaratairbhūpa dhārā deyā ca tadvidaiḥ |
pāṣanḍa vikalān luvdhān dharmmāpetān asaṃyatān
sarvvakāla-pradāyī tu na vadennāvalokayet |
mṛtyuñjayaṃ mahātattvaṃ catuḥ saptāṣṭa jāpinā
bhāvyaṃ vai nityahome tu anyathā viphalaṃ bhavet |
sāmānyā yā bhaveddhārā tasmin japyaṃ śataṃ śatam
prātarmadhyāhṇa-sandhyāsu sarvvakāma-samṛddhaye |
vasu-dravyaṃ ghṛtamājyamamṛtaṃ haviḥ kāmikam
tasya dhārā sadā deyā vasorddhārā hi sā matā |
vasunā svarga-kāmeṇa dakṣeṇa ca mahātmanā
mayā ca viṣṇunā śakra rudreṇa ca sahomayā |
ātmānañca svarūpeṇa dhārāyāntu pradāpayet
devī sānnidhyamāyātā sarvvakāma-pradāyikā |
tasmāttvamapi rājendra vasordhārāṃ prapātaya
nātaḥ parataraṃ puṇyaṃ vidyate nṛpa-sattama |
vasorddhārā pradānasya ekāhamapi yadbhavet
nṛpeṇāyuṣakāmeṇa putradārasukhārthinā |
deyā dhārā sadā vatsa ripunāśāya buddhinā
vicchedo nitya-homasya na ca kāryya kadācana |
mahādoṣamavāpnotī ye tatra vimukhāḥ narāḥ
dravyā bhāve ghṛtābhāve nṛpataskaraje bhaye |
yadi no vahate dhārā tadācchidraṃ na vidyate
homaṃ kṛtvā kṣamāveta devadevīṃ nṛpottama |
punaḥ prāptau bhavedhomaṃ pratiṣṭhā vidhicoditam
mahā āśvina māse tu aṣṭamī navamīṣu ca |
kārtikyāṃ māghacaitre tu citrāyāṃ rohiṇīṣu ca
vaiśākhyāntu pradātavyā jyeṣṭhāṃ jyaiṣṭhasya sattama |
āṣāḍhe dvādaśī homaṃ aṣṭamī pūrṇimā nabhe
nabhasye rohiṇī vatsa caturthyāṃ skandaje dine |
saṃkrāntiṣu ca sarvvāsu gurusauri bhavāsu ca
śakrocchraye pradātavyā janmapuṣyābhiṣecane
mārge vratanibandhe tu śubhe vā ketudarśane |
grahakṛtyopasargeṣu dhārā deyā śubhāvahā
evaṃ yo vāhayed dhārāṃ śāstra dṛṣṭena karbhmaṇā |
tasya bhūḥ sidhyate sarvvā sanāgā sahasāgarā
aśvamedhasamaṃ puṇyaṃ dinahomāt prajāyate |
vājapeyaśataṃ rātrāvagniṣṭomaśataṃ tathā
ādhayo vyādhayastasya na bhavanti kadācana |
āyurārogyamaiśvaryamiha cānte śinī bhavet
iti śrī devīpurāṇe vasordhārādānavidhirnāma saptaviṃśo'dhyāyaḥ |

aṣṭaviṃśo'dhyāyaḥ |

agastya uvāca |

śūlino brahmaṇā prāptamindrācca mama āgatam |
mayāpi te yathā vṛttaṃ tathā rājan prakāśitam
brahma viṣṇu śivānāñca mahābhaya vimokṣadam |
mantritaṃ śakra-govinda-vācaspati-pitāmahaiḥ
rudrastotraṃ mahādevyā viṣṇvārādhana-ghorajam |
vadhaṃ mahiṣarūpasya bhūmau devyavatāraṇam
vrataṃ vrajocchrayaṃ dhārā maṅgaleṣu paṭhet sadā |
devyāyatane devasya śaṅkarasya harerapi
goṣṭhe vā cavvare śaile gṛhe vā sumanorame |
devīṃ sampūjayitvā tu bhojayitvā kumārikāḥ
tadbhakti bhāvitān viprān-sadvṛttāñchāstratatparān |
yathāśaktyā ca pūjyet hemavastravibhūṣaṇai
tatastān svasti vācayitvā pūjayitvā tu pustakam |
sugandha-gandha-dhūpena puṣpamālyaiḥ sucandanaiḥ
ghaṇṭācāmaraśobhāḍhyai darpaṇairūpaśobhite |
dukūle vastrābharaṇe daṇḍayantre niveśayet
vācakaṃ pūjayitvā tu yathāvibhavavistaraiḥ |
vācayet tato rājā devī māhātmyamuttamam
tadante śānti śabdastu janasya sa nṛpasya ca |
kṣatra-viṭ-śūdra-bālānāṃ sarvameva śubhaṃ tu vaḥ |
anena vidhinā rājā yaḥ paṭhet śṛṇuyādapi
cintayed vācayed vāpi tasya puṇyaphalaṃ śṛṇu |
aśvamedha sahasrasya vājapeyaśatasya ca
agniṣṭoma mahāṣṭoma rājasūya mahāmakhaiḥ |
yat phalaṃ labhyate tāta tat phalaṃ śatadhā bhavet
gaṅgātoyā bhiṣekādaistīrthainaimiṣa puṣkaraiḥ |
yat phalaṃ labhyate rājaṃstat phalādayutādhikam
brahmahatyādipāpānāṃ śamanaṃ paramaṃ śatam |
varddhanañcātha-dharmmāṇāṃ kāma-mokṣa-phala pradam
putradaṃ patnidaṃ tāta jayadaṃ saukhyadaṃ param |
anena vidhinā vatsa prāpnoti śravaṇānnaraḥ |
iha kīrti śriyaṃ brāhmīṃ paratra bhavati layam
iti śrī devīpurāṇe devyāstava-paṭhana-māhātmyaṃ nāma aṣṭāviṃśo'dhyāyaḥ
ekonatriṃśo'dhyāyaḥ |

śakra uvāca |

evaṃ sarvvapradā devī yathā nātha pravaṇitā |
tasyāhaṃ śrotumicchāmi vyākhyārādhanapūjanam
brahmovāca |

na parā cāparā devī pūrva vā ca purandaram |
tasyāstvaṃ bhaktimāpannaḥ kathanādeva vāsava
yadā sadbhāvatā tasyā vyāptibhāvena vidyate |
tadā tvaṃ surarājendra śṛṇuṣvekamanodhunā
ekā eva parāśaktiḥ sarvvagā vyāpinī kila |
svabhāvāt kartṛrūpatvāt bhūtādyaiḥ pañcadhā sthitā
bhūta tanmātra-vuddhākhya karmmavarga manodhiṣu |
ahaṅkāra pradhānena prabhāvāt sā vyavasthitā
hemajantu mahaddaṇḍaṃ sahasra kiraṇojvalam |
taptahāṭaka-saṅkāśaṃ koṭyāyutasamaprabham
śatakoṭi pravistīrṇa samantāt parivarttanam |
tañca varṣa sahasreṇa dvidhābhūtaṃ punastataḥ
madhye tasyābhavad brahmā candra-sūryekṣaṇo vibhuḥ |
sakalaṃ bhū divaṃ bhūta khaṃ diśo manaugocaram
sa sisṛkṣu prajāḥ sarvvāstadādeśena vāsava |
sa eva sthitaye viṣṇuvināśe rudraḥ sobhavat
sthāvarasya carasyāsya dṛśyādṛśyasya vāsava |
jarāyujānḍaja svedānāmudbhidānā tathaiva ca
nagānada samudrāṇāṃ viśeṣe tadbhavo'bhavat |
vidyāvedana-vedānāṃ vāñjanī jananī tathā
mātā mātṛka bhedena varṇa bhedena sā sthitā |
mantra-tantra-kriyā-mudrā-viṣa-bhūta-jvarādiṣu ||029: 012
anyāpi tat prabhāveṇa śamante bhiṣajo rujaḥ |
na ca varṇāntarābhāvā āśramāṇāṃ kriyāstathā
īkṣate mantrarūpeṇa sūryyasya iva raśmayaḥ |
sā ca varṇa kramādbhūtā dvijāti brahmacāriṇī
saṅkara prabhāvāṇāñca varṇānāṃ karaṇe sthitā |
ānvikṣikī trayī vātā daṇḍākhyā sā ca kīrtitā
dīptiḥ sūryye kṣamā bhūmau kāntiścandre jale pluti |
jvālā vahnī gatirvāyau vyomni sā vyāpinī bhavet
yajamāne tathā dīkṣā dhāraṇā yogināmapi |
prajñā prajñāvatāṃ sā tu vāgmināntu sarasvatī
lakṣmī sā tu dhanāḍhyānāṃ siddhi siddhipsūnāmapi |
dayā dayāvatī sātu prīti prītimatāmapi
śarā khaḍge jyādhanuṣi śabdo vādyeṣu sā smṛtā |
parasya sā paratvena śivasya śivagāminī
bhakti mukti pradā devī brahmādīnāntu sā matā
iti śrī devīpurāṇe vyāpti praśaṃsā nāma ekonatriṃśo'dhyāyaḥ |

triṃśo'dhyāyaḥ |

brahmovāca |

śṛṇu tasyā surādhyakṣa ārādhana-rvidhiṃ parāma |
yathā sā toṣitā pūrvva śaṅkarādyaiḥ phalepsubhiḥ
karmma-yajñena deveśa tathā tvāmapi pūjayeḥ |
śambhuḥ pūjayate devīṃ mantraśaktimayāṃ śubhām
akṣamālākaro nityaṃ tenāsau vibhavavānnaraḥ |
ahaṃ śailamayīṃ devīṃ yajāmi surasattama
tena brahmatvamevedaṃ mayā prāptaṃ sudurlabham |
indranīlamayīṃ devīṃ viṣṇurarccayate sadā
viṣṇutvaṃ prāptavāṃstena adbhutaiḥ kaṃsanāśanām |
devī hemamayī kāntāṃ dhanado'rcayate sadā
tenāsau dhanado devo dhaneśatvamavāpnuyāt |
viśvedevā mahātmāno raupyāṃ devīṃ manoharām
yajanti vidhivadbhaktyā tena viśvattvamāpnuyuḥ |
vāyuḥ pūjayate bhaktyā devīṃ pittalasambhavām
vāyutvaṃ tena tat prāptamanaupamya guṇāvaham |
vasavaḥ kāmikāṃ devīṃ pūjayante vidhānataḥ
prāpnuvastanmahātmāno vasutvaṃ hi śubhāvaham |
aśvinau pārthivīṃ devīṃ pūjayeta vidhānataḥ
tena tāvaśvinau devau divya-deha-gatāvubhau |
varuṇatvaṃ hi saṃprāptaṃ tena ṛddhayā samanvitam |
devīṃ mantramayīṃ puṇyāmagniryajate bhāvitaḥ
agnitvaṃ prāptavāṃstena tejorūpasamanvitam |
tāmrāṃ devīṃ sadā kāla bhaktyā devo divākaraḥ
arccate tatra saṃprāptaṃ tena sūryyatvamuttamam |
muktāphalamayīṃ devīṃ somaḥ pūjayate sadā
tena somena somatvaṃ saṃprāptaṃ sattojjavalam |
pravālakamayīṃ devīṃ yajante guhyakādayaḥ
tena bhogabalopetāḥ prayāntīśvara-mandiram |
vajraloha-mayīṃ devīṃ yajante mātaraḥ sadā
mātṛtvaṃ prāpya tāḥ sarvvāḥ prayānti paramaṃ padam |
evaṃ devāḥ sagandharvvāḥ piśācoraṇarākṣasāḥ
pūjayanti sadākālaṃ carccikāṃ suranāyikām |
tathā tvamapi devendra yadīpsasi parāṃ gatim
śivāṃ maṇimayāṃ pūjya labhase manasepsitān |
kāmān suravarādhyakṣa kāmikaiḥ pūjitā sadā
dadāti sarvvalokānāṃ cintāmaṇiryathā śivā
iti śrī devīpurāṇe dravya-vidhi-pūjā-devīmāhātmyaṃ nāma triṃśo'dhyāyaḥ |

ekatriṃśo'dhyāyaḥ
bhakta bhojyānatapānena tatra sarvvāṃśca prīṇayet |
bhojayitvā kṣamāyeta devī me prīyatāmiti
tathā devyā rathe kṛtvā punareva gṛhaṃ nayet |
prakṣipyamāṇaiḥ kanyābhiḥ strībhiḥ maṅgalavādibhiḥ |
salilena pathi pāṃśuṃ kṛtvā paṅkaṃ pracakrire
puraśobhāṃ pathiśobhāṃ dvāraśobhāṃ gṛhe-gṛhe |
kārayīta tathā śakra sarvvavādhāṃ nivārayet
acchedyāstaravassmin prāṇihiṃsā vivarjayet |
vandhanasthā vimoktavyā vadhyā krodhādi śatravaḥ
akāla kaumudīṃ śakra rathayātrānte kārayet |
sarvvadā sarvvadevaistu, śaṅkarādyaiḥ pratiṣṭhitā
ratha yātrā tadā śakra suraiḥ svarge sadā kṛtā |
tathā kinnara-gandharvaiḥ bhū-pātāla nivāsibhiḥ
ratha yātrā prabhāveṇa modante divi devatāḥ |

agastya uvāca |

pūrvvaṃ yat kathitaṃ tāta tete sarvva mayākhilam
sthāpitaṃ nātra sandeho devī māhātmyamuttamam |
yaḥ paṭhet śṛṇuyādvāpi bhaktimān nṛpasattama
sa sukhaṃ yaśaḥ saubhāgyaṃ putra prāptiṃ yathepsitām |
labhate nātra sandeha ityevaṃ brahmaṇo'bravīt
suvalena kṛte rājye purā śakrasya kīrtitā |
dhanadasya purā proktā varuṇasya ca vāyunā
kṛte sthāne kṛtānena tathā śrutvā ca nirṛtaiḥ |

vedādyanta ṣaḍaṅga yoga vihitaṃ sāṃkhyādibhiḥ kalpitam
sarvvajñaṃ prabhumīśvaraṃ trinayanaṃ sarvvātmanā bhāvitāḥ |
te bhūyo na kalā kalaṅka gahanaṃ paśyanti yornimukham
ye tvanye sukṛtaiṣiṇaḥ pratidinaṃ protthāya bhāvānvitāḥ |
karpūrāguru candanaiḥ surucitaiḥ sragbhistathā bhūṣaṇaiḥ
kṣīrādisnapanairvidhāna vihitaiḥ kurvanti śarvvārccanam |
bhogān sarvva gatānubhūya sudhiyo gacchanti divyaṃ padam
ye kecit kupathāśritā jaḍadhiyo mandāmamajñāḥ śaṭhāḥ |
devaṃ śāntamajaṃ pradhānapuruṣaṃ nindanti mohācchivam |

mṛtyodgocaramāgatāḥ yama bhaṭairnānāvidhaiḥ śāsanaiḥ |
śāmyante narakeṣu te prativalaiścākrandamāṇā bhṛśam
dānaṃ bhūtadayā gurūpadaśanaṃ kṣāntirna caivāṃjitā |
satyaṃ śaucamahiṃsratā śamadama tyāgo'nukampā tathā
yeṣāṃ naivamihāsti mūḍhamanasāṃ śarvvāccanaṃ kvacit |
teṣāṃ naṣṭa piśāca kāgatadhiyāṃ puṃsāṃ vibhūtiḥ kutaḥ
dvaiṣṭārastu vasya ce kupuruṣā gacchanti te'dhogatim |
tāmisre krakacāsi patra narake kumbhī mahā raurave
yoni mārga sahasra khinnagamanāḥ prāpyeha mānuṣyakam |
rogārto jaḍa vāsanāndhavadhirā jāyanti yonau khalāḥ
janma-vyādhi -jarā viyoga maraṇa kleśādibhiḥ santatām |
bhūtiṃ cañcala sāgarormicapalaṃ svapnopamaṃ jīvitam
mātā-pitṛ-kalatra-putra suhṛdo ye ke'pi bandhātmakā |
jñātvaivaṃ naralokamadhruvamimaṃ śarvvaṃ sadā saṃśrayet
yairdattaṃ na dhanaṃ yathāvibhavataḥ pātreṣu dīneṣu vā |
vidyā nāgamitā yaśo na vitataṃ śīlaṃ na saṃrakṣitam
satyaṃ nādhigataṃ tapo na caritaṃ kīrtirna vikrāmitā |
teṣāṃ kṣema śivaṃ na vidyati nṛṇāṃ muktvā harārādhanam
yeṣāṃ na śambhucaraṇāgrata bhaktivādaḥ |
kṣuṇṇāṃ lalāṭa śatajarjjaritaṃ kapālam
teṣāṃ kuto bahula candana carccitāni |
muktā phalārccita vadhūstana-maṇḍalāni
ye tvāṃ vibho suparikalpana kalpiteṣu |
samyak caranti vividheṣu śivārccaneṣu
te cārū tuṅga ghanakuṅkumapiñjarīṣu |
vidyādhariṣu nivasanti kucāntareṣu
pravrajyā na kṛtā vidhāna vihitā uktā tu yā śambhunā |
śaivajñāna mahārṇavasya vidhivannaivañca pāraṃ gatam
puṣpaiśca sukarṇikāra tilakaiḥ nābhyarccitaḥ śṛladhṛka |
kālo'yaṃ para piṇḍa tarpaṇa paraiḥ kākairiva preṣitaḥ
na dhyātaṃ padamīśvarasya vidhivat saṃsāra vicchittaye |
naivābhi śrutibhi stuto'harahaḥ śambhuḥ vibhurbhūtale
naivāpyutkaṭa gandhadhūpa kusumaiḥ pūjā kṛtā śaṅkare |
dhātrā nūnamakāraṇaṃ vayamiha sṛṣṭā jagat pūraṇe
saṃsargāt kautukādvā kṣaṇamapi yaiḥ japtaṃ pādeṣu padmeṣu śambho |
yāti brahmendra viṣṇu draviṇa pati purāṃstrīnati kramya lokān
śāntyā bhāvena yastaṃ praṇamati satataṃ sarvva vinyasta sargī |
saṃchinnaḥ kleśa pāśaiḥ praviśati virajo rudra tejo nidhānam
yat kiñcāsana japya homa niratā rāgādibhiḥ varjjitāḥ |
śambhoḥ pāda nipāta ghṛṣṭa śirasaḥ pratyaṅmukhāḥ patniṣu
teṣāmeva nigūḍha nūpura varā cañcaccalan mekhalā |
sambhrāntāgraja paṅgajodyatakarā paryyeti lakṣmīḥ sthiram
yairnādyāpyanyajanmasitakuvalayaiḥ miśritābhiḥ sitābhiḥ |
mālābhiḥ mālatīnāṃ tribhiramaraguruṇārccito nolakaṇṭhaḥ
te vidyāvittahīnāḥ pracalita manasaḥ kṣuttṛṣākṣāmakaṇṭhā |
loke'smin doṣaduṣṭāḥ paribhava vibhavāste ca nityaṃ bhavanti
ye mānavā vigatarāga parāparajñā yogeśvaraṃ suraguruṃ satataṃ smaranti |
dhyānena te prahata kilviṣa mohajālā mātuḥ payodhara rasaṃ na punaḥ pivanti
tad gātraṃ praṇipātareṇudhavalaṃ sarvvasya yat sarvvadā |
te netre tapasārjjite surucire tābhyāṃ haro dṛśyate
sā vṛddhi vimalendu śaṅkha ghavalā yā śaṅkaradhyāyinī |
sā jihvā mṛdubhāṣiṇī hitakarī yā stauti nityaṃ śivam
taccitta capalaṃ cinoti kuśalaṃ yanniścalaṃ śaṅkaram |
te śrotre parame śivāmṛtarasaṃ yābhyāṃ haraḥ śrūyate
te hastāḥ śiva dharmma karmma niratāḥ pūjā pramāṇotsukā |
tau pādau samayau pradakṣiṇaratau nityaṃ vibhorbhāvitau
pāpaṃ pāpa rataṃ hyaśuddha manasaṃ nirlajja ghagnavratam |
krūraṃ taskarasīrṣakaṃ śaṭhadhiyaṃ tṛṣṇādhikaṃ nirddayam |

kāma-krodhavaśaṃ kṛtaghnacapalaṃ tṛṣṇāturaṃ jihmalam |
mūrkha hiṃsana sūcakaṃ paśupate toṣākaraṃ trāhi mām
dīnaṃ duḥkhitakaṃ kucailamalinaṃ jihmaṃ śaṭhaṃ durbhagam |
kṣudraṃ pāpamatiṃ svadharmma calitaṃ bahvāśinaṃ nirddhanam
andhaṃ vyādhita niṣṭhuraṃ vyasaninaṃ sadbhiḥ sadā ninditam |
mūrkhaṃ dharmma vivarjjitaṃ paśupate doṣākaraṃ trāhi mām
imaṃ stavaṃ śakva vinirmmitaṃ paṭhan dine-dine kratuphalamāpnuyānnaraḥ |
labha tyasau yadbhihitaṃ purātane tallakṣaye gacchati śāśvataṃ padam

īśvara uvāca |

śruṇu vatsa pravakṣyāmi devyārādhanamuttamam |
karmmayajñantu yajñānāṃ sukaraṃ sumahatphalam
sāṃvatsarī yathā pūjā sukālena samārabhet |
evaṃ nakṣatravedhādīn kuryyāt kanda phalāśinaḥ
yava sarpiḥpraghāsī ca gomūtraṃ dadhi gomayam |
pavitraṃ vihitaṃ tantre asavatānāñca bhārgava
devī vrataṃ pravakṣyāmi sarvvakāma prasādhakam |
śrāvaṇe śukla pakṣe tu aṣṭamyāṃ vāyu-bhojanaḥ
snātvā sārdrayaṭī bhūtvā jitakrodhaḥ kṣamānvitaḥ |

ālabhya rocanā mantrairdhūpo deyastu bālakam |
saṃnakhaṃ sita-tāmiśraṃ padmapuṣpaiśca arccayeta
naivedyaṃ rohitaṃ māṃsamājaṃ vā śalyakaṃ tathā |
godhūma vikṛtiṃ bhakṣyān ghṛta pakvāni dāpayet
