aṣṭacatvāriṃśo'dhyāyaḥ
brahmovāca |

rākā cānumatī caiva dvividhā pūrṇimā tathā |
sinī'vālī kuhuścaiva amāvasyā dvidhaiva tu
amā nāma rave raśmiścandraloke pratiṣṭhitā |
yasmāt somo vasatyasmāt amāvāsī tataḥ smṛtāḥ
pūrvvodite kalābhinne paurṇamāsyāṃ niśākare |
pūrṇimānumatī jñeyā yaścāstamita bhāskare
yasmāt tāmanu manyante devatā pitṛbhiḥ saha |
tasmātanumatī nāma pūrṇimā ca tadā smṛtā
yadā cāstamite sūryye pūrṇacandrasya codgamaḥ |
yugapat sottarā rākā tadānumati-pūrvvikā
rākā tāmanumanyete devatāḥ pitṛbhiḥ saha |
rañjanā caiva candrasya rāketi kavayo'vruvan
sinī vālī pramāṇantu kṣīṇa śeṣo niśākaraḥ |
amāvasyāṃ viśetyaṃrka sinīvālī tataḥ smṛtāḥ
kuhvati kokilenokte yaḥ kālastu samāpyate |
tattatkāla saṃjñā tveṣā vai amāvasyā kuhuḥ smṛtā
anumatyā sarākāyā sinī vālyā kuhuṃ vinā |
etāsāṃ dvi-navaḥ kālaḥ kumātreti kuhuḥ smṛtāḥ
kalāḥ ṣoḍaśa somasya śukle varddhayate raviḥ |
anṛ tenāmṛtaṃ kṛṣṇa pīyante daivataiḥ kramāt
prathamāṃ pivate vahṇi rdvitīyaṃ tapanaḥ kalām |
viśve devāstṛtīyāntu caturthīntu prajāpatiḥ
pañcamī varuṇāścāpi ṣaṣṭhiṃ pivati vāsavaḥ |
saptamīmṛṣayo divyā vasavoṣṭau tathāṣṭamīm
navamīṃ kṛṣṇapakṣasya pivatīndraḥ kalā mapi |
daśamīṃ marūtaścāpi rudrā ekādaśīṃ kalām
dvādaśīntu kalāṃ viṣṇurdhanadaśca trayodaśīm |
caturdaśīṃ paśupatiḥ kalāṃ pivanti nityaśaḥ
tata pañcadaśīñcaiva pivanti pitara kalām |
kalāvaśiṣṭo niṣpītaḥ praviṣṭaḥ sūryyamaṇḍalam
amāyāṃ viśati raśmau amāvāsī tataḥ smṛtā
pūrvāhne praviśatyarka madhyāhne tu vanaspati
aparāhṇe viśatyapsu svayoniṃ vāri sambhavaḥ
āpaḥ praviṣṭa somastu śeṣayā kalayaikayā |
tṛṇa gulma latā vṛkṣān niṣpādayati cauṣadhīḥ
tamoṣadhiḥ sthitaṃ gāvaścaratyo'paḥ pivanti ca |
tadaṅgānugataṃ gobhyaḥ kṣīratvamupagacchati
tat kṣīrasamavṛtaṃ bhūtvā mantrapūtaṃ dvijātayaḥ |
svāhākāravaṣaṭakāraiḥ juhvatyā hutayaḥ kramāt
hutamagniṣu devāya punaḥ somaṃ vivarddhayet
evaṃ saṃkṣīyate somaḥ kṣīṇaścāpyāyate punaḥ
tasmāt sūryyaḥ śaśāṅkasya kṣayavṛddhi rvidhedvibhuḥ
iti śrī devīpurāṇe candrakṣayavṛddhirnāma aṣṭacatvāriṃśo'dhyāyaḥ
ekonapañcāśo'dhyāyaḥ |

brahmovāca |

yadayaṃ vadate loko vāliśatvān mahāmate |
tadahaṃ saṃpravakṣyāmi candra sūryyoparāṇikam
yadi satyamayaṃ grastastejorāśi rdivākaraḥ |
tat kathantūdarasthena rāhuṇā bhasmasāt kṛtaḥ
athavā rāhuṇākramya śatruvaktraṃ praveśitaḥ |
tat kathaṃ daśanaistīkṣṇaiḥ śatadhā ca vikhaṇḍitaḥ
vimuktaśca punardṛṃṣṭastathaivākhaṇḍamaṇḍalaḥ |
na cāsyāpahṇutaṃ tejo na sthānādapasāritaḥ
yadi vāpyeṣa niṣpītaḥ kathaṃ dīptataro'bhavat
tasmānna tejasāṃ rāśī rāhorvaktraṃ gamiṣyati
bhakṣyārthaṃ sarvva devānāṃ somaḥ sṛṣṭaḥ svayambhuvā
tatrasthamamṛtañcāpi sambhavaṃ sūryatejasā |
pibanti yastūbhayaṃ devāḥ pitaraśca svadhā mṛtam
trayaśca triśataṃ caiva trayastriṃśat tathaiva ca |
trayaśca rtrisahasrāśca devāḥ somaṃ pivanti ca
rāhorapyamṛtaṃ bhāgaṃ purā sṛṣṭaṃ svayambhuvā |
tasmāt tadrāhurāgatya pātu micchati parvvasu
uddhṛtya pārthivīṃ chāyāṃ mandakāmaṃ tamomayaḥ |
pātumicchan tataścendumācchādayati chāyayā
śukle ca candramabhyeti kṛṣṇe parvvaṇi bhāskaram |
sūrya maṇḍala saṃsthastu candrameva jighāṃsati
tasmāt pivati taṃ rāhustanumasya vināśayan |
avihiṃsan yathā padmaṃ pivati bhramaro madhu
candrasya amṛtaṃ tadvad bhedādrāhuraśnute |
candrakāṃto maṇiryadvat tuhinaṃ kṣarate kṣaṇāt
kṣarannapi na hīyate tejasā naiva mucyate |
yathā sūryyamaṇiścāpi sūryyādutpādya pāvakam
na bhavatyaṅga hīno'pi tejasā nava mucyate |
evaṃ candraśca sūryyaśca chāditāvapi rāhuṇā
svatejasā na mucyete nāṅgahīnau vabhūvatuḥ |
parvvasvatha ca candrasya māṇikya kalasākṛtiḥ
somo daivata saṃyogācchāyā yogācca pārthive |
rāhośca varalabdhādvai prakṣaredamṛtaṃ śaśī
svadoha kāle saṃprāpte vatsaṃ dṛṣṭvā yathā ca gaḥ |
svāṅgadeva kṣaret kṣīraṃ tathenduḥ kṣarate'mṛtam
piteva sūryyo devānāṃ somo māte lakṣyate |
yathā mātuḥ stanaṃ pītvā jīvanti sarvvajantavaḥ
pītvāmṛtaṃ tathā somāt tṛṣyante sarvva devatāḥ |
saṃbhūtaṃ parvva yogeṣu tathāyaṃ kṣarate śaśī
taṃ kṣarantaṃ yathābhāgamupajīvanti devatāḥ |
tasmin kāle samabhyeti rāhurapyavakarṣati
sarvvaṃmarddhaṃ tribhāgaṃ vā pādaṃ pādārddhaṃmeva vā |
ākramya pārthivīṃ chāyāṃ yāvaṃtī candra maṇḍalam
smṛtaḥ sa bhāgo rāhostu deva bhāgāstu śeṣakāḥ |
tṛptiṃ vidhāya devānāṃ rāhoḥ parvvagatasya ca
candro na kṣayamāyāti tejasā naiva mucyate |
tithi bhāgāśca yāvantaḥ punastvarkaṃ pramāṇataḥ
parvvacchāyāsthitaḥ kālastāvānevaṃ prakīrttitaḥ |
adhorāhupuraḥ somaḥ somādūrdhva divākaraḥ
parvvakāle sthiti stvevaṃ viparītaḥ punaḥ punaḥ |
ataśchādayate rāhurabhavacchaśi bhāskarau
rāhurabhrakasaṃsthānaḥ somamācchādya tiṣṭhati |
uddhṛtya pārthivī chāyāṃ dhūmamegha ivotthitaḥ
candrasya yaddṛṣṭavyaṃ rāhuṇā bhāskarasya vā |
nāmnā ca khaṃḍitaṃ tasya kevalaṃ śyāmalī kṛtam
kardamena yathā vastraṃ śuklamabhyupahanyate |
ekoddeśe tu sarvva vā rāhuṇā candramāstathā
prakṣālitaṃ tadevāstu punaḥ śuklataraṃ bhavet |
rāhu muktaṃ bhavet tadvannirmmalaṃ candramaṇḍalam
rāhuṇācchāditau vāpi dṛṣṭvā candra divākarau |
viprāḥ śāṃti parā bhūtvā punarāpyāya yantritam
evaṃ na gṛhyate sūryyaścandramāstatra gṛhyate
avudhāstaṃ na paśyanti mānuṣā māṃsa cakṣuṣā
jagat sanmohanaṃ caiva grahaṇaṃ candra sūryayoḥ
iti śrī devīpurāṇe grahaṇavikalpo nāmaikonapañcāśo'dhyāyaḥ |
|
ekapañcāśo'dhyāyaḥ |

brahmovāca |

yeyaṃ devī ihāmutra hitāya samupāśritā |
svārtha siddhau parārthe vā bhavantī kathayāmite
maṅgalā śākambharī kālī devyā yā trividhā tanuḥ |
ghorahā ruruhā vatsa śubhā kandaka nāśinī
damanī mahiṣadhnī ca tathā ca mahiṣāsurā |
etā mūlagatā devyaḥ ṣaṣṭidhā koṭidhāparāḥ
eteṣāṃ śāstravettāro devī pūjāvidhau śubhā |
mātṛ maṇḍala vettā ca brāhmaṇaḥ kṣatriyo'pi vā
praticārī viśorvāpi śūdro vā tattvavidyadi |
pūjāvidhau bhavet śreṣṭho na mando na kuśīlavaḥ
na naiṣṭhiko viśāstro vā pūjako bhavate śubhaḥ |
abhidhau ya śivāṃ pūjyetā pareṇa niyājitaḥ
sa yāti narake ghoraṃ svāmī rājā ca naśyati |
tasmācchivavidhā devī viṣṇurbhārgava taiḥ śubhaiḥ
pūjitaḥ śivavataḥ sūryyaḥ śivaḥ sarvvaphala pradaḥ |
agre vā śiva siddhānta tilakādi pravedibhiḥ
māṭharokta vidhau vāpi sarvvakāma pradāyakaḥ |
ahañca veda vidhinā grahā nāgā pare surāḥ
suśāstravidhimāśritya pūjitāḥ phaladā nṛṇām |
vaiparityādbhayaṃ kuryyāt apade rājanastha ca
tasmāt parārdhyamuddiśya pūjāṃ vidhi śubhāvahā |
madhurāmlādinā kecit tuṣyante baṭukaiḥ pare
kaṣāya lavaṇaistiktairevaṃ bhinnā nṛṇāṃ matiḥ |
devā mūrttigatāḥ sthūlāḥ śabdagā dhyānagāḥ pare
svārtha siddhau parārthe vā manasā yānti cintitāḥ |
tathāpi upacāreṇa jāti bheda kriyādibhi
śive vivarjjayet kundamunmattañca harestathā |
devīnāñcārka mandārau sūryye keśayutaṃ mṛgam
evaṃ vidhiṃ samāśritya pūjayellabhato phalam |
hema pātreṇa sarvvāṇi labhate ca hitān mune
ardhyaṃ datvā tu raupyeṇa āyu rājya sutāmÌllabheta |
tāmra pātreṇa saubhāgyaṃ dharmmaṃ mṛnmaya sambhavaiḥ
vārkṣapātrāṇi pātrāṇi naiṣṭhikādiṣu kārayet |
śailāni krūra jātīnāṃ raktādi sarvvakāmikam
dhātūttamāni pātrāṇi nṛparāṣṭra vivṛddhayai |
trapusīsa kalau hāniranya jātiṣu kārayet
vivāha yajña śrāddheṣu pratiṣṭhāsu viśeṣataḥ |
pātrāṇāñcādaraḥ kāryyaḥ pātrāṇyevottamāni ca
pātreṣu pṛthivī dugdhā sudhā pātreṣu dhāryyate |
vedāḥ somaṃ kraturpajñāḥ pātrāṇyeva vidurvudhāḥ
bali homa kriyādīni binā pātre na sidhyati |
tasmād yajñāṅgamevāhuḥ pātrañcāgpraṃ mahāmune
yo yasya āyudhaḥ proktastasya tallāñchanaṃ bhavet |
vāhana dhvajacchatreṣu lāñchanaṃ parikalpayet
ṣaṭtriśadaṅgulaṃ pātrañcottamaṃ parikīrttitam |
rasa aṅgula kīnantu na pātraṃ kārayet kvacit
nānā vicitra rūpāṇi puṇḍarīkākṛtīni ca |
śaṅkha nīlotpalākārān pātrāṇi parikalpayet
vinā pātrāṇi yaḥ kuryyāt pratiṣṭhāṃ yājñikī kriyām |
viphalā bhavate sarvvā vāhanāddhi dhanāpahā
balihīne tu durbhikṣaṃ gandhahīne abhogyatā |
dhūpahīne ca udvegaṃ vastrahīne dhanakṣayam
ratnahīne haredbhāryyāṃ patākai rddaṇḍanāyakam |
chatra hīne harecchatraṃ vitāne makaraṃ bhavet
vedīhīne tu cālaṃ syānnagarasya purasya ca |
kalasai rbandhu nārāśva bhavati munisattama
toraṇānāmabhāve tu harejjātīśca vāndhavān |
sruvi kuṇḍavihīnaṃ tu yajñaṃ lupyanti rākṣasāḥ
rajohīnaṃ tu daurbhāgyaṃ prāpnuyāt kāraka sadā |
dakṣiṇā rahite sarvvaṃ bhavate avicāraṇāt
mantra vidyā vihīnantu sampūrṇamapi naśyati |
pātra mantra samāyuktaṃ sarvva doṣān nivārayet
iti śrī devīpurāṇe pātravidhirnāma ekapañcāśo'dhyāyaḥ |
|

dvipañcāśodhyāyaḥ |

manuruvāca |

śṛṇu śaunaka tattvena apa mṛtyu nivāraṇam |
sarvva kāma pradaṃ puṇyaṃ raviyāga manuttamam
grahā māghādi bhedena ādityaṃ makare yajet |
hasta mātre śubhe padme karṇikā keśarojjvale
kuṅkumādi rajairlikhyamaṣṭapatraṃ ravergraham |
ādityaṃ pūjayenmadhye pūrvvapatre niśākaram
maṅgalaṃ vahnipatrasthaṃ dakṣiṇena budhaṃ yajet |
śani nairṛta patrasthaṃ surejyaṃ varuṇālayam
vāyavye saihiṃkeyantu bhārgavañcottare yajet |
ketuṃ śivāṅge deyaṃ yāge sarvvaśubhodaye
ādi varṇa kṛtādhāraṃ ādityaṃ śambhunā yajet |
śeṣā vāruṇa varṇena aṣṭadhābhi rdivena tu
gandha puṣpaṃ pavitrantu hṛdayena pradāpayet |
varadābhaya mudrau tu madhye vyomaṃ pradarśayet
sarvva raktopacārantu ādityāya prakalpayet |
sva sva varṇaṃ grahāṇāntu deyaṃ puṣpavilepanam
homaṃ tilājyakṣaudrantu pāyasantu nivedayet |
evaṃ kṛtvā japaṃ devamādityāya susaṃkhyayā
snānaṃ śiṣyāya karttavyaṃ mantra pūtena vāriṇā |
sarvva kāmānavāpnoti yo vidhiṃ kārayedimam
iti śrī devīpurāṇe ādityayāgonāma dvipañcāśo'dhyāyaḥ |
|

tripañcāśo'dhyāyaḥ |

ādityaṃ bhāskaraṃ sūryyaṃ raviṃ bhānuṃ divākaram |
sraṣṭāraṃ tejinaṃ bhāvaṃ jayantaṃ śubhadaṃ śivam
makarādi prabhedena ādityādi śubhodayam |
yaṣṭavyā hastamātre tu dvivṛdhyā dhanuṣāvadhi
śubhado'yaṃ jayaṃ bhāgyaṃ kalyāṇamaparājitam |
maṅgalamiṣṭa siddhiñca vibhavaṃ śubhadaṃ śubham
iṣṭākhyaṃ vyādhināśantu makarādau samārabheta |
sarvvapāpaharā yāgāḥ sarvve āyurdhanapradāḥ
sarvva roga vināśāya sarvve kāryyāḥ sukhāya ca |
nityaṃ śvetopahāreṇa āyurārogyadāyakāḥ
suta saubhāgya kāmena kāryyā raktopacārikāḥ |
pītena grahanāśārthaṃ kṛṣṇaiḥ śatrunivāraṇam
grahāṇāṃ yajanaṃ kāryyaṃ samantraṃ valipūjanam |
phala ratnauṣadhī gandhavīja dhātu mṛtādibhiḥ
saptodaka samantreṇa snātvā bhāgyodayo bhavet |
gajānāṃ turagāṇāñca raviśakra samanvitam
snānaṃ homaṃ prakarttavyaṃ lakṣāyuta sahasrikam |
mātarāṇāṃ sada cakraṃ hemarājatatāmrajam
pūjanaṃ vidhinā vipra saṃvatsaraṃ bhayāpaham
iti śrī devīpurāṇe grahamātṛvidhirnāma tripañcāśo'dhyāyaḥ |
|

catuḥpañcāśo'dhyāyaḥ |

manuruvāca |

sahasra lakṣaṇopetaṃ vaidūryye kārayecchivam |
haima pīṭhaṃ suśobhāḍhyaṃ vajrāṅkaṃ tatra mātarāḥ
carccikādyāḥ prakarttavyāḥ pūrvvādi parikalpitāḥ
mahābhaya vināśāya ṛtuyāga prapūjitāḥ |
mahāvibhava sāreṇa vastra gandhaṃ supūjitam |
prayacchati śubhān kāmān mano'bhīṣṭān sadā jane
tasya pūjā prakarttavyā gehe sarvvatra kālike |
japa homārccanaṃ pūjā trikālaṃ satataṃ bhavet
kuṅkumāgurū karpūra mada candana rocanāḥ |
gandha puṣpāśca dātavyāḥ sitaniryyāsasiddhakāḥ
sarvvabhaya vināśāya pramāthī piṅgalāpi vā |
śani sūryyā ca rāhūtthā kṣayādi mahadāpadaḥ
anna janmarkṣa mṛtyusthāḥ samaṃ yāntyavicāraṇāt |
tāmre patre prakarttavyā grahabhāga prakalpitā
rakta candana miśreṇa toyena satate jitāḥ |
rakta karavīrapuṣpairmantra pūtārdha pūjitāḥ
vyome vā maṇḍale vāpi sarvvakāma phala pradā |
arka palāśa khadirā apāmārgo'tha pippalā
śrī phalā śamī dūrvvā ca kuśāgrāḥ samidho matāḥ |
dhūpaṃ guggululodhrasya sarjja cola dalaṃ param
śrīveṣṭakaṃ kuṣṭhañca vṛkṣādi guggulaṃ tathā |
guḍaudanaṃ raverdeyaṃ pāyasaṃ haviṣānvitam
dadhyodanaṃ budhe deyaṃ gurau kṣīraudanaṃ tathā |
ghṛtānnaṃ tilamāsānnaṃ māsaṃ citraudanaṃ tathā
gāṃ suraktā ravau dadyācchaṅgī some vṛṣaṃ kuje |
kāñcanaṃ vastramaśvañca gāṃ sukṛṣṇāmajāyamasama
dakṣiṇāṃ gandha puṣpādiṃ svaṃ svaṃ varṇaṃ pradāpayet |
homa grahādi pūjāyai śatamaṣṭādhikaṃ pi vā
aṣṭāviṃśāṣṭa homantu yathā prāptirvidhīyate |
lakṣahomaṃ prakarttavyaṃ sarvva pīḍā nivāraṇma
gāyatryā grahamantraiśca kuṣmāṇḍī jātavedasaiḥ |
aindra vāruṇaścāgnaiśca vāyu yāmasa vaiṣṇavaiḥ
homaṃ śatasahasrantu aṣṭautkṛṣṭaṃ vidhīyate |
sarvva pīḍā vināśāya koṭi homaṃ śubhāvaham
yava vrīhi ghṛtaṃ kṣīraṃ tilākaṅgu praśāntikaṃ |
paṅkajośīra vilvāmra dalaṃ home prakīrttitam
sarvva śāstrārthaṃ kuśalai rgrahamātṛ prapūjakaiḥ |
homaṃ kāryya sadā vipra sarvva śānti pradāyakaiḥ
graha kṛtyopasargādi ṛá¹tumāsa samāḥ śubhāḥ |
yakṣarakṣaḥ kṛtā pīḍā lakṣahomāt praśāmyati
iti śrī devīpurāṇe mātṛ grahalakṣahomavidhirnāma catuḥpañcāśo'dhyāyaḥ

pañcapañcāśo'dhyāyaḥ
śaunaka uvāca |

sarvva lokopakārāya saṃkṣepānna tu vistarāt |
utpāta śamanī śāntiṃ śrotumicchāmi tattavataḥ
manuruvāca |

apacāreṇa lokānāmupasargaṃ mahātmanām |
aparavatā vināśāya sṛjante devatā mune
utpātān vividhākārāṃstridhāvasthānupasthitān |
divyāntarīkṣān bhaumāṃśca yathāvattān nibodhata
sa prācīndiśamanvāvarttate |

atha yadāsya maṇi maṇika kumbha sthālī daraṇāmāyāso rājakula vivādo vā yānacchatra śayyāsanāvasatho dhvajagṛhaikadeśaḥ prabhajyate |

gajavāji
mukhyā pramriyante hastinī vā mādyati ityevamādīni tānyetāni sarvvāṇi indra daivatyānyadbhutāni prāyaścittāni bhavanti|
indraṃ viśvā avīvṛṣamiti sthālī pākaṃ
kṛtvāpañcabhirājyāhutiḥ juhoti |

indrāya svāhā |

śacī pataye svāhā |

vajrapāṇaye
svāhā |

īśvarāya svāhā |

sarvva pāpapraśamanāya svāheti |

vyāhṛtīśca pṛthak kṛtvā
sa dakṣiṇāṃ diśamanvā varttate |

atha yadāsya śarīre cāviṣṭāni bhavanti vyādhayo vāneka vidhāḥ |

svapnamasvapanāti bhojanamabhojanamatinidrā svālasyaṃ gṛhadvāreṇa vā sarpo'pagacchate
kapotaḥ praviśati |

strī śarīre vārohati |

kṛṣṇa strī darśan mādeśyam ityevamādīni
tānyetāni sarvvāṇi yama devatānyadbhutāni prāyaścittāni bhavanti |

sthālī pākaṃ kṛtvā pañcabhirjuhuyāt |

yamāya svāhā |

pretādhipataye svāhā |

daṇḍapāṇaye svāhā |

īśvarāya svāhā |

sarvva pāpa praśamanāya svāheti |

sarvvatrapraṇavādi svāhāntatā vyāhṛtīśca pṛthak kṛtvā
sapratīcīṃ diśamanvāvarttate |

atha yadāsya kṣetre gṛha saṃstheṣu dhānyeṣvībhaya āraṇye paśu mṛgāścā rauhanti |

ākhu pataṅga paipīlikā śāśaka bhaumaka sūkṣmaka śalabha ityevamādīni tānyetāni sarvvāṇi varuṇa devatānyadbhutāni prāyaścittāni
bhavanti |

varuṇaṃ vā viśādaṇḍamiti sthālī pākaṃ hutvā pañcabhirjuhuyāt |

varuṇāya svāhā |

apāmpataye svāhā |

pāśapāṇaye svāhā |

sarvvapāpaśamanāya svāhā |

īśvarāya svāheti |

vyāhṛtibhiśca pṛthak kṛtvā
sa pratyudīcīṃ diśamanvā varttate |

atha yadāsya maṇi kanaka rajata vastra vajra vaidūryya maṇika viyogā bhavanti |

ārambhakāṇi ca vipadyante |

mitrāṇi vā virajyante |

veśmani avāvūni vā jāyante |

valmīkāścoddhṛyante |

śuṣka vṛkṣāḥ prarohanti |

tailaṃ tyajanti |

madhūni vā pīyante |

rātrāvindradhanu draṣṭvā śvetāśvetañcavāyasaṃ |

śmaśāne dhūmo jāyate |

aśvatarī vā garbhaṃ gṛhnāti ityevamādīni tānyetāni sarvvāṇi vaiśravaṇa devatānyatyadbhutāni prāyaścittāni bhavanti |

ādityaṃ devamiti sthālīpākaṃ kṛtvā pañcabhirājyāhutibhiḥ juhuyāt |

vaiśravaṇāya svāhā |
yajñādhipataye svāhā |
hiraṇya pāṇaye svāhā |

īśvarāya svāhā |

sarvvapāpa śamanāya svāheti |

vyāhṛtibhiśca pṛthak hutvā
sa pṛthivīmanvā varttaṃte |

atha yadāsya pṛthivī sphuṭati |

kūjati, kampati, ghūmāyati akasmāt salilamudgirati |

akāle ca vṛkṣāḥ puṣpaphalāni vā varttante |

ityevamādīni tānyetāni sarvvāṇi agnidaivatyāni adbhutāni prāyaścittāni bhavanni |

agniṃ hutamiti sthālī kṛtvā pañcabhirājyāhutibhiḥ abhijuhoti |

agnaye svāhā |

arcciṣpataye svāhā |

īśvarāya svāhā |

sarvvapāpa śamanāya svāheti |

vyāhṛtibhiśca pṛthak hutvā
so'ntarīkṣamanvā varttate |

atha yadāsyāntarā varṣāṇi colkāḥ patanti |

nipatanti, ghūmāyanti, diśo dahyanti |

ketavaścottiṣṭhante |

gavāṃ śṛṅgeṣu rudhiraṃ sravanti |

atyaryaṃ himānyutpatanti |

ityevamādīni tānyetāni sarvvāṇi somadaivatānyadbhutāni prāyaścittāni bhavanti |

somaṃ rājānamiti sthālīpākaṃ kṛtvā pañcabhirājyāhutibhi rabhijuhoti pṛthak pṛthak |

somāya svāhā |

nakṣatrādhipataye svāhā |

sīrapāṇaye svāhā |

īśvarāya svāhā |

sarvvapāpa śamanāya svāheti |

vyāhṛtibhiśca pṛthaka kṛtvā
sa diva manvāvarttate |

atha yadāsya vidhātā dhāryate |

vātā vāyante |

abhreṣu karakāṇi dṛśyante kharakarabhakaṅkolūka gṛghraśyena bhāsa vāyasa kapota gomāyusaṃsthānyupala pāṃśu māṃsa paśvasthi rudhira varṣāṇi prarkttante |

ityevamādīni tānyetāni sarvāṇi vāyudaivatyānyadbhutāni prāyaścittāni bhavanti |

idaṃ viṣṇu rvicakrama iti sthālīpākaṃ kṛtvā pañcabhirājyā hutibhirabhijuhoti |

viṣṇave svāhā |

sarvvādhipataye svāhā |

cakrapāṇaye svāhā |

īśvarāya svāhā |

sarvvapāpa śamanāya svāheti vyāhṛtibhiśca pṛthak pṛthak
bhūmikampo diśāṃ dāho grahayuddhaśca jāyate |
gagane dṛśyate keturādityaścaiva kampate
ādityājjāyate cchidraṃ kṛṣṇavarṇo hi jāyate |
viparītānnadīṃścaiva rudhirañca pravāhayet
śilā vā plavate yatra ravirmadhye yadā kvacit |
gaganāt śrūyate divyaṃ nirghātaścaiva jāyate
atyadbhutaṃ mahāghoraṃ sṛṣṭi saṃhāra kārakam |
rājyopasaṃharañcaiva rājānāṃ kṣayakārakam
ityevamādīni tānyetāni sarvvāṇayadbhutāni proyaścittāni bhavanti |
gṛhe gṛhe bhavecchāntiḥ mātṛṇāṃ pūjanaṃ baliḥ |
dānaṃ rudraṃ japennityaṃ bhāskarejyā grahārccanam
lakṣahomaṃ mahāhomaṃ koṭihomaṃ puroditam |
gomū hiraṇya vastrānna tiladānaṃ śubhāvaham
pāyasaṃ dadhikṣīrājyaṃ deyaṃ sarvveṣu bhojanam |
evaṃ prajāyate śāntistato dravyāṇi āharet
tāni toyena prokṣīyodupahārāṇi yāni tu |

atha pūrvvāhṇe ca yathā vadājye cāhutiṃ hutvā dūrvvā payodadhisarpiḥ sarṣapān phalavatī apāmārga tila brīhi-yava-samidhānyetānyāhared vā snātaḥ prayataḥ śuciḥ śucivāsāḥ sthaṇḍilamupalipya nitya tantreṇodana-kṛṣara-yavāgū-saktu-pāyasaṃ-dadhimadhu dhṛtāktāḥ pṛthak ca varaḥ sarvveṣāṃ vā pāyasaṃ tataḥ agnimupasamādhāya juhuyāt yathāvaditi
iti śrī devīpuruṇe sārvvadaivikī sarvvotpāta śāntirnāma pañcapañcāśo'dhyāyaḥ

ṣaṭ pañcāśo'dhyāyaḥ
indraṃ viśvā avāvṛṣaṃ samudravya saṃśiraḥ |
rathītamaṃ rathīnāṃ vā rājānāṃ śatapatiṃ patim
nāke suparṇaṃmupatyāṃta havā revanto abhya ca kṣata tvā |
hiraṇyākṣaṃ varuṇasya dūtaṃ yamasya bhūraṇyaṃ yonau śakunam
varuṇaṃ vodhipādamṛcāmindraṃ havāmahe |
parivrajecca vāhvorjjaṃgandhāso svarṇavaṃ naram
ādityaṃ devaṃ savitā manyoḥ kavi kratumarccāmi |
ūrdh rva yasyā matibhā ādityutsavo maṇi |
hiraṇyapāṇi tvamimīte sukratuḥ kṛpāpayaḥ
agniṃ dūtaṃ vṛṇīmahe hotāraṃ viśva vetasam |
asya yajñasya sukṛtam
somaṃ rājānaṃ bhavate agnimanvārabhāmahe |
ādityaṃ viṣṇuṃ sūryyaṃ brāhmaṇañca vṛhaspatim
idaṃviṣṇu rvicakrame tredhā nidadhe padam |
samūḍhamasya pāṃśūle
vāta āvāta bheṣajaṃ śantu mayā ttanā kude |
praṇatāyuṃṣi tāriṣat
gaurīrmimāya salilāni takṣatyekapadī sā catuṣpadī
aṣṭāpadī nava padīṃ bhūmīṃ sahasrākṣaṃ vā parame vyoman
kāṇḍāt kāṇḍāt prarohantī puruṣaḥ puruṣaḥ pari |
dadhāno dūrvve pratanu sahasreṇa śatena ceti

yathaiva yajñastathaiva bandhūryāsi tanosi pratanosi athainamabhivādya vācayati
dhruvosi dhruvo'yaṃ yajamāno .asminnāyatane prajayā bhūyāsamiti
paśubhiriti caivaṃ yaṃ kāmaṃ kāmayate so'smai kāmaḥ samṛddhyate
yo jānāti na jīyate hanti śatrumabhidya sa eva bhaved vasu sahasrajit
ihaiva staṃ mā viyauṣṭaṃ dīrghamāyu vyasrutam |
krīḍantau purtrairnaṃptṛbhiḥ modamānau ca sve gṛhe
punaḥ patnī agnivadāyuṣā saha varccasā |
dīrghāyu rāsyāpaḥ patibhi rjīvāti śaradaḥ śatam
sthālīpākādikarma vidhirucyate |
parisamūhya-upalipya-ullikhya-uddhṛtya-abhyukṣya-agnimupasamādhāya-dakṣiṇato brahmāsanamāstīrya-praṇāya-paristīrya-ātmavadāsādya-pavitrīkṛtvā-prokṣanī-saṃskṛtya-ātmavat prokṣaya-nirupādhamadhistutya-paryagnikuryāt
sruvaṃ pratāpya samuhya abhyukṣya punaḥ pratāpya nidadhyāt saṃttāpyotpūya avekṣya prokṣaṇī pūrvavadupayamanān kuśānādāya samidho'bhyādhāya paryukṣya juhuyāt |
eṣa eva vidhiryatra kvaciddhaumaḥ
parisamūhanādibhirdevatā pratibhāgamaṃtrāśca vyākhyāsyāmaḥ
yaddevo devahelanamiti parisamūhanam |
mānastoketyupalepanam |
tvāṃ vṛtre jindra satpatim ityullikhya |
brajaṃ gacchetyudvṛtya |
devasya tveti abhyukṣya |
agnimṛtveti agnimupasamādhāya |
samidhāgni dravyasya ceti samidādhānaṃ dadhāt
mayi gṛhṇāmīti agrahastaṃ kṛtvā hiraṇyakarbha iti dakṣiṇato brahmā |
āpo hiṣṭheti ca uttarataḥ praṇītā |
kayānaścitrā iti praṇītya paritaḥ paristaraṇam |
pavitrastho vaiṣṇavya iti pavitrachedanī |
iṣetvetyājyanirupaṇam
trātāramiti sruvaṃ pratāpya |

satoraṇaṃ bhavet tīrthe utsargaṃ gokule'pi vā

vatsaṃ sarvvāṅgasaṃpūrṇaṃ kanyā sā lohitā bhavet
alaṅkṛtya yathā śobhā utsargaṃ kārayenmune |

i haiva sarvvakāmāni pradadyāt sarvva maṅgalā

prapārāma taḍāgāni devatāyatanāni ca |

upakalpitṣu bhāgeṣu yadi vidhnopajāyate |

vaiśākha śuklasya tu yā tṛtīyā navamyasau kārtika śukla pakṣe |

uparāge candramase raveśca taṃ misro'ṣṭa kāyāmayana dvayaṃ ca |

śrāddhaṃ kṛtaṃ tena samāḥ sahasraṃ rahasyametat pitaro vadanti |

eteṣu kāleṣu ca dāna homamutsargadhātā yatneṣu dattam |

athavā jīrṇa saṃskāra vidhiḥ puṇyo mahāmune |

tasmādanātha jīrṇeṣu kāryyaṃ saṃskaraṇaṃ mune |

svato vā parato vāpi yastu saṃskurute surān |
sa yāvaccandra sūryyau dyaustāvat kālaṃ sukhī bhavet

vasate divi hṛṣṭātmā jīrṇa saṃskāra kārakaḥ |
anāthā vā sanāthā vā pūjanīyāḥ sadā surā
viśeṣeṇa tu ye pūrvvāste te cejyā satataṃ mune |

vaiśākhe tu prakarttavyā pūjā pāṭalajaiḥ srajai |
sarvvakāmamavāpnoti jyaiṣṭhe padmārjjunaistathā
āṣāḍhe vilva kahlārairihitaṃ labhate phalam |

nomālī kusumaiḥ pūjā na bhe kāryyā mahāphalā |

kadamba campakairīṣe sarvvakāma phalapradā
pūjā paṅkajamālābhyāṃ sarvvābhyudayadāyikā |
śatapatrikayā pūjā kārttike sarvvakāmikā
mārge nīlotpalā pūjā puṣye kuṃja kajāstathā |
māghe kundakṛtā pūjā sarvvakāma pradāyikā
phālgune marupatrotthā mādhavī śubhadāyikā |
evaṃ savatsaraṃ caitryāṃ yaḥ kuryyād grahasattama
gandhapuṣpānna vastraiśca tasya puṇyaphalaṃ śraṇu |
hemago bhūmi vastrānna vidyādāna phalaṃ labhet
vājapeya mahāmedha rājasūya śatādhikam |
aśvamedhaṃ paśumedhaṃ gomedhaṃ kramaśaḥ phalam
labhate dakṣiṇā homaṃ vratānte vidhinā dadet |
pūraṇaṃ phalapuṣpaiśca vastrapaṭṭasrajānnajam
dhṛta kṣīradadhibhaktaiḥ sarvvakāma phalapradaḥ |

iti śrī devīpurāṇe pratimāpūjā nāma dviṣaṣṭitamo'dhyāyaḥ
triṣaṣṭitamo'dhyāyaḥ |

manuruvāca |

mandarasthaṃ mahādevaṃ brahmā pṛcchati śaṅkaram |
keṣu keṣu ca sthāneṣu draṣṭavyo'si mayā prabho
īśvara uvāca |

vārāṇasyāṃ mahādevaṃ prayāge tu maheśvaram |
naimiṣe devadevantu gayāyāṃ prapitāmaham
kurukṣetre viduḥ sthānaṃ prabhāse viśvarūpiṇam |
puṣkare tu ayogaṃdhaṃ viśvañca vimaleśvare
aṭṭahāse mahānādaṃ mahendre tu mahābratam |

ujjayinyāṃ mahākālaṃ mākoṭe tu mahotkaṭam |

rudrakoṭyāṃ mahāyogī mahāliṅgaṃ sthaleśvare |
harṣe ca harṣitañcaiva sarvvaṃ madhyamakeśvaram
kedāre caiva īśānaṃ rudraṃ rudre mahālaye |
suvarṇākṣe sahasrākṣaṃ vṛṣabhe vṛṣamadhvajam
bhairave bhairavākāraṃ bhava śastrapade viduḥ |
ugraṃ kanakhale caiva bhadrakarṇa hrade śivam
devadāruvaṇe diṇḍiṃ caṇḍaṃ madhyama jaṅgale |
urdhvaretaṃ turuṇḍe ca sukalānte kaparddinam
kṛttivāsañca ekāgre sūkṣmañcābhratikeśvare |

kālaṃjare nīlakaṇṭhaṃ śrīkaṃṭhaṃ maṃḍakeśvare |
|
dhyānasiddheśvare yogī gāyatrīñcottareśvare
vijayaṃ nāma kāśamīre jayantaṃ marukeśvare |
hariścandre hariñcaiva puriścandre tu śaṅkaram
jaṭiṃ rāmeśvare vidyāt saumyaṃ kukkuṭakeśvare |
bhūteśvare bhasmagotraṃ jalaliṅge jaleśvaram
bhikṣukaṃ karikāyāntu vārāhaṃ vindhyaparvvate |
tāmraṃ paścimasandhyāyāṃ virajāyāṃ trilocanam
tṛpteśvare triśūlī ca śrīśaile tripurāntakam |
jala liṅge viduḥ kālaṃ kapālī karavīrake
dīptacakreśvare vedaṃ nepāle paśupatiṃ patim |
śrīkārā rohaṇe lakuṭiṃ vedīkāyā mumāpatim
gaṅgāyāṃ sāgare tvamayamoṅkāramamarakaṇṭake |
saptagodāvare bhīmaṃ svayambhūrnakuleśvare
karṇikāre gaṇādhyakṣaṃ bhūrbhuvaṃ gandhamādane |
siddheśvarantu ākāśe pātāle hāṭakeśvaram
aṣṭaṣaṣṭistu nāmāni devadevasya dhīmataḥ |
purāṇe copagītāni brahmaṇā ca svayambhuvā
yaḥ paṭhet prātarutthāya snāto vā yadi vā śuciḥ |
mucyate sarvvapāpebhya śivalokañca gacchati
iti śrī devī purāṇe mahādevasyāṣṭaṣaṣṭināmakīrttanaṃ nāma triṣaṣṭitamo'dhyāyaḥ |

catuṣaṣṭitamo'dhyāyaḥ |

vṛṣaṃ gāvau samādāya yuvānau lakṣaṇānvitau |

durgaṃ purañca nagaraṃ karttavyaṃ maṅgalāyutam |
na ca śūnyāni vāsāni dhārayeddevatādiṣu
na gṛhaṃ vīthikā durgaṃ pure śīrṇaṃ vidhārayet |
rājabhāgaṃ bhavet tacca devatādiṣu vinyaset
devaśca śaṅkaraḥ kāryyaḥ sagaṇo maṅgalāyutaḥ |
tasmin nityotsavāḥ sarvve gṛhaprāsāda bhūṣitāḥ
vaseyururddhagā lokā bādhā śāśvatavarjitāḥ |
aṭavyādiṣu durgeṣu adhovāsaṃ na kārayet
vasaṃstṛṇādigeheṣu bhayādi parivarjjitāḥ |
adhobhāgena meghādīn dhārayenmunisattamaḥ
dhārayan mahadāpnoti bhayaṃ rājā arātijam |
rāṣṭraṃ ripuvale naiva rājā ca paripīḍyate
tasmād durgaṃ vivṛddhayarthañcordhvavāso vidhīyate |
urddharvaṃ subhṛtāvāsyāḥ kubhṛtāstu nivāsayet
mattonmattān pramattāṃśca durge na vāsayennarān |
naike kuryyāt prabhutvantu na śūdre na kuśīlave
na ca vandhakine kuryyānna co'yasi niyantrite |
kuryyād durgaṃ viśīryet yathā gehaṃ śirohatam
aindreśastu śivo durge adhorddhe tannipīḍayet |
svakāyapīḍanāddoṣaṃ śive svāmī vinaśyati
jalaje giridurge ca vādho vāso bhayāvahaḥ |
aṭavye tu viśeṣeṇa śāśvataṃ varjjayedadhaḥ
araṇyeṣu ca durgeṣu ūṣareṣu viśeṣataḥ |
vāhye vāsaṃ na kurvvīṃta araṇyeṣu tathaiva ca
araṇye dharmmahāniḥ syādūṣare'pi tathaiva ca |
aṭavye śatrujā śaṅkā tasmādvāsamadhastyajet
kṛṣikarmmātu carmmādi lohitantu gaṇāyasam |
śarayantrauṣadhādīnāṃ saṃgrahāya adho vaset
vaṇigvīthinivāsinyo dhānyameyā hiraṇyena |
urdhve cāsyā vaśīkṛtya rājñā durgahitaiṣiṇā
paṅkalaṃ kheṭakaṃ parṇaṃ durgādhaḥ karṣayet sadā |
tannivāsijanā sevane kāryyāḥ savalāḥ sadā
evaṃ na kṣīyate durgaṃ dhanadhānyena saṃbhṛtam |
varddhate ca janaḥ koṣo rājā ca sukhamedhate
yathā yathā vivardhante daivaukāni giraupari |
tathā tathā vivarddhante rājño dharmmayaśaśriyaḥ
yathāraṇyavāsināñca dharmmo bhavati dehinām |
evaṃ rājñaḥ śriyā dharmmo durge kālavaśād bhavet
durgādhaḥ kṛtrimaṃ durgaṃ kiñcit kālaṃ vivakṣayā |
vijayārthe prakarttavyaṃ yathāvat tānnibodha me
durgāśrayaṃ samālakṣya ūrdhrvaṃ durgaṃ valaṃ tathā |

jalendhanañca dhānyañca yavasamāyudhādikam |
|
tathā kuryyānmahāvāho kṛtrimaṃ vijayottamam
kāṣṭheṣṭamathavā śailaṃ khātikāracitaṃ tathā |
drumavallīlatopetaṃ garbhaṃ toyasamanvitam
vāhyatoyaṃ surakṣyaṃ vā durgayantropalādibhiḥ |
karttavyaṃ gṛhaprākāraistoraṇairupaśobhitam
vīthī pūrakasaṃyuktamathavā maṇḍapānvitam |
maṇḍapaṃ śatadaṇḍena dviguṇaṃ triguṇaṃ pivā
mānādavṛttamatha tryasramāyatendu yathāśubham |
aneka garbhagarbhāḍhyaṃ devatā mātarānvitam
sudurgaṃ nāyakaṃ kāryaṃ nāgayajñaṃ umānvitam |

aneka māṇḍameyādibhṛtaṃ kūpaprapānvitam |

sūryyāgnī dharmmato deyau śubhe cāpādi varjjite
evaṃ kālavaśāt kuryyād vijayākhyaṃ mahāpuram |
nīcocca vidhisaṃsthānaṃ lakṣayitvā gṛhaṃ valam
puraṃ durgaṃ prakarttavyaṃ maharddhiphalakāṅkṣayā |
tritrikaṃ garbhagarbhantu daṇḍaiścāndrādibheditaiḥ
pūrvvādideśaṛkṣantu dvigarbhantu dviraṣṭakam |
vāhye dvādaśakaṃ deyaṃ tatra vidyād balāvalam
praveśe bhayadāḥ krūrāḥ saumyāḥ saumyaphalapradāḥ |
niṣkāśe śubhadāḥ sarvve pure durge ca kīrtitāḥ
ekaṃ patnī vināśāya dve ca mitradhanāpahe |
trīṇi jyeṣṭhasutaṃ hanyurnīcasthānasthitā grahāḥ
na bhānau nīcage kuryāt puraprāsādakalpanām |
svāmī nāśamavāpnoti tat puraṃ naiva sidhyati
saumyaiścoccasthitaiḥ kuryyād dravyārthaṃ vijayaṃ puram |
durgaṃ krūraiḥ prakarttarvyaṃ śatrunāśāya vuddhimān
valaṃ candrārkalagnānāṃ vuddhāvāsaṃ samaṃ samam |
āyurdā yaśadā pākarājayogāṣṭavargakam
candra dṛṣṭivalaṃ karmma sadakhyā praśnasambhavān |
sotpāta daiva sattvotthaṃ jñātvā durge śubhāśubham
rājayogaṃ samāveśaṃ saṃvatsaramataṃ sphuṭam |
kriyāsādhana siddhyarthaṃ cārabhedagrahasaṃśrayam
sthāna kāla svabhāvākhyaṃ valaṃ mitragṛhāśritam |
raśmijañca tathā cānyadvalānāṃ pravaraṃ valam
vakraiḥ saumyaśataiḥ kuryyād grahai durgapurādikam |
nityañca te grahā dadyurṛá¹ddhiṃ svāmijanasya ca
drekkāṇāśaśiveśa ca navāṃśamudaye śubhe |
triṃśaddvādaśabhāge ca kārayet purakalpanām
krūraḥ krūraṃ vijānīyāt saumyaiḥ saumyaṃ vidhīyate |
tavādi vigrahairvatsa ripumitravivarjjitaiḥ
atītairastulagnaiśca na kuryyāt sanniveśanam
na kīṭāraṇyalagneṣu na ca sandhyāgatai rgrahaiḥ |
puraṃ durgaṃ prakarttavyaṃ śatrukṣetrasamāśritaiḥ
mitrarkṣa mitra sampannaiḥ puṣṭairuccābhilāṣibhiḥ |
svakṣetresvatrikoṇeṣu sthitaiḥ kāryya sadāpuram
durgaṃ durgaṃ samīpasthaṃ tasya mitratrikoṇajaiḥ |
grahaiścandravalopetaiḥ kāryyaṃ sarvvaṃ śubhāvaham
saumye dharmmārthakāmāni śeṣāḥ sthāna samāgatāḥ |
agnidāhaṃ bhayaṃ hāniṃ ripupīḍāṃ sadāratim
āgneyādi vijānīyāt pūrvvadurgo kṛte pure |
nandate pūrvvabhāgasthe īśe dharmmo vivarddhate
sarvvakāmānavāpnoti pūrvveśānottareṇa tu |
saritpūrvvai valopetaiḥ śubhā yāmyena sārataḥ
taḍāgaṃ savanaṃ paścāt saumye cendīvaraṃ dalam |

pūjayitvā haraṃ durgāṃ grahān mātṛ vināyakān |
|
prāsādoktavidhanena valiṃ datvā kuru puram
iti śrīdevīpurāṇe puradurgacintājātakriyā nāma trisaptatitamo'dhyāyaḥ |

catuḥ saptatitamo'dhyāyaḥ |

manuruvāca |

nityo vibhuḥ sthitaḥ kālo avasthā tasya hetunā |
naimittādi viśeṣaistu loke puṇyaphalapradāḥ
saṃkāntyākhya purākhyātaṃ puṇyaṃ dhārā śubhā mune |
grahaṇādiphalaṃ puṃsāṃ tīrthabhedaṃ śṛṇuṣva tat
gaṅgādvāraṃ kurūkṣetraṃ narmmadāmarakaṇṭakam |
yamunāsaṅgamaṃ puṇyaṃ vetravatī vipāśānvitā
sarayuḥ kauśikī vindhyā gaṇḍakī ca sarasvatī |
candrabhāgā mahāpuṇyā nadī godāvarī tathā
kāverī gomatī tāpi devikā varūṇāparā |
etāḥ puṇyatamā nadyo grahaṇādiṣu kīrttitāḥ
anyāśca vahavaḥ puṇyā anyakāle ca kāmadāḥ |
ayane viṣuve khyātī vyatīpāte tathaiva ca |

dinacchidre amāvasyāṃ grahāṇāṃ saṅgameṣu ca |
sanmoheṣu samājeṣu ekarkṣa saptapañcadhā
evaṃvidheṣu parvveṣu candre sarvvakalābhṛte |
tṛtīyāyāñca vaiśākhe aṣṭamyāṃ kujavāsare
caturdaśyacāñca kṛṣṇāyāṃ bhaumāhe pitṛtarpaṇam |
karttavyaṃ sarvvakāmānāṃ pūraṇāya narottamaiḥ
amāvasyāntu saṃkrāntau śivādityantu yo naraḥ |
yajate bhaktimān pūtaḥ sa pūto bhavate mune
kārttike grahaṇaṃ śreṣṭhaṃ gaṅgā yamunā saṅgame |
mārgetu grahaṇaṃ puṇyaṃ devikāyāṃ mahāmune
puṣyetu narmmadā puṇyā māghe sannihitā śubhā |
phālgune varūṇā khyātā caitre puṇyā sarasvatī
vaiśākhe ca mahāpuṇyā candrabhāgā saridvarā |
jyeṣṭhe tu kauśikī puṇyā āṣāḍhe bhāvikā nadī
śrāvaṇo sindhunāmāca proṣṭhe śreṣṭhā tu gaṇḍakī |
aśvine sarayuḥ śreṣṭhā bhūyaḥ puṇyā tu narmadā
godāvarī mahāpuṇyā candre rāhusamanvite
sūryye ca śaśinā graste tamorūpe mahāmune |
narmmadā toyasaṃsparśāt kṛtakṛtyā bhavanti te
ye sūryye sehikeyena graste vairājanaṃ narāḥ |
spṛśanti avagāhanti na te prākṛtamānuṣāḥ
snātvā rājakratuṃ lebhe dṛṣṭvā godānajaṃ phalam |
spṛṣṭvā gomedhatulyantu pītvā sautrāmaṇiṃ labhet |

snātvā vājimakhaṃ puṇyaṃ prāpnuyādavicāraṇāt
ravicandroparāge tu ayane cottare tathā |
evaṃ gaṅgāpi draṣṭavyā tadvaddevī sarasvatī
śivādityaphalaṃ yacca maṇḍale samudāhṛtam |
sagrahe maṅgalāyoge tadapi prāpnuyānnaraḥ
ūṣarāraṇya-kṣetreṣu puṇyaṃ yat samudāhṛtam |
tadatra kāla māhātmyāduparāge samādhikam
yo vā āhṛtya toyena vidhinā abhiṣecanam |
samantreṇaiva pūtena tasya puṇyaṃ tato'dhikam
ātma vittānusāreṇa pātraistaijasa pārthivaiḥ |
vārkṣaiḥ śailairatha vipra phalaṃ prāpnotyaninditam
ye vā vai mṛttikāṃ tasmiṃstīrthe āhṛtya ca mune |
prātaḥ prātaḥ samutthāya vandayanti narottamāḥ |

te sarvve pāpanirmmuktā bhavanti vigatāmayāḥ
phala puṣpopahāreṇa yo vā tasmin ravīśvaram |
snātvā saṃpūjayed vipra sa bhavedvigatāmayaḥ
mantrapūtena toyena kumbhaiḥ puṣpaphalānvitaiḥ |
saphalairvidhinā snātaḥ sarvvakāmāmÌllabheta saḥ
yadevaṃ kathitaṃ puṇyaṃ mayā vrahmamukhācchrutam |
tat samagraṃ bhavet tasya araṇyeṣūṣareṣu ca
araṇyāṇi pravakṣyāmi yathā caivoṣarāṇi ca saindhavaṃ daṇḍakāraṇyaṃ naimiṣaṃ kurūjāṅgalam
upalāvṛtamāraṇyaṃ jambūmārgo'tha puṣkaram |
himavāsastato'raṇye uttamaḥ parikīrttitaḥ
navasveteṣvaraṇyeṣu yastu prāṇān parityajet |
vrahmalokātithirbhūtvā sa yāti paramaṃ padam
karṇiko śiva cākhyeti kālikāgaṇayo śive |
kālañjare mahākāle tulyañcaitiṣu yat phalam
iti śrī devīpurāṇe grahaṇānadyaraṇyayoṣara praśaṃsā nāma catu saptatitamo'dhyāyaḥ |

pañcasaptatitamo'dhyāyaḥ |

himavaddhemakūṭe ca vindhye mahendra parvvate |
vaidiśe ujjayinye vā mahāsene'tha bhūbhṛte
gopagirau mahāpuṇye citrakūṭe'thavā mune |
kālañjare'thavā kāśyāṃ puṣpākhye veda parvvate
ujjayinyāmayodhyāyāṃ dāpayedatha maheśvare |
eteṣu puṇyadeśeṣu viṣuvāyaṇasaṅgame
puṣkare naimiṣe vatsa deyā pañcamukhe'kṣaye |
girau dhārā pradānena grahapīḍā na jāyate
bahuvakragate dehe vatsavanna bhayaṃ bhavet |
janmādhānarkṣapīḍā vā dattā dhārā vyapohate
jamvūmārge sadā pūjā dhārāpātaṃ viśiṣyate |
sarvvakāmānavāpnoti narmmadāyāṃ mahāmune
dhārādānena gaṅgāyāṃ kālindyāñca mahāhrade |
dattvā vidhānavihitāṃ na bhayaṃ jāyate kvacit
śanisūryyakṛtāṃ pīḍāṃ gurubhaumāṃ vyapohate |
yathā pūjā vidhānena prati saṃvatsarotthitām
pīḍāṃ nivārayedvatsa saṃvatsaragrahodbhavām |
mantrajāpāt sadā vatsa na bhayaṃ vidyate kvacit
ekānte duṣṭarahite pāpajantu vivarjite |
dhārā homaṃ prakarttavyaṃ yathoktaṃ śriyamicchatā
jihvāyāṃ pātayeddhārāṃ na drutāṃ na vilamvitām |
sāvadhānena manasā mṛtyuñjaya niyāmitām
mantrayogādbhavet siddhirdṛṣṭādṛṣṭa prasādhikā |
grahapūjā haret pīḍāṃ trividhāmapi utthitām
grahāśca trividhāḥ proktāḥ teṣāṃ mantrāstridhāmatāḥ |
aṅgajā mūlamantrāśca piṇḍāḥ padagatāstathā
homakāle prayoktavyāḥ pūjākāle tathaiva ca |
evaṃ siddhimavāpnoti iha svargāvargikīm
bhāvakāle kriyāyogāddhārāyāṃ labhyate mune
dhārādānaṃ prakarttavyaṃ yantrapātra ghaṭādibhiḥ |
naimitte nityahome ca pūrvaiśca kathito vidhiḥ
iti śrī devī purāṇe nimittadhārāparicchedo nāma pañca saptatitamo'dhyāyaḥ |

ṣaṭsaptatitamo'dhyāyaḥ |

nārada uvāca |

narmmadāyāṃ mayā tāta śrutaṃ snānaphalodayam |
tīrthayātrā prasaṅgena mārkaṇḍeya-tapāśramam
caturmmukhaṃ mahāpuṇyaṃ tathā māheśvaraṃ varam |
āmarākaṃ giriśreṣṭhaṃ devanadyāḥ phalodayam
vāraṇākhyaṃ mahāpuṇyaṃ tathā paścima sāgaram |
jaṭā śaile mahādevaṃ pañcamṛtyuvināśanam
gaṅgābhāgyodayaṃ nātha kedāraṃ parvvatottamam |
nandādevī gatandevaṃ mahādevī mahāphalam
naimiṣaṃ puṣkaraṃ devaṃ tathā sthāneśvaraṃ varam |
kurūkṣetraṃ mahāpuṇyaṃ sarvva pāpa praṇāśanam
ghaṭeśvaraṃ mahādevaṃ kaumāraṃ dakṣiṇārṇave |
rāmeśvaraṃ śivaṃ devaṃ vrahmahatyāvināśanam
avimuktañca kāśyākhyāṃ māyāpuryyāṃ sureśvaram |
eva tīrthāni deveśa mahāpuṇyaphalāni ca |

śrutāni aghanāśāya śataśo'tha sahasraśaḥ
abhiṣeka prasaṅgena kumārasya mahātmanaḥ |
kīrttitaṃ vaidiśe deśe bhṛṅgāraṃ divamuttamam
jambūdvīpasya caiśānyāṃ tasya paścima dakṣiṇe |
vaidiśe cottare bhāge saptagavyūti saṃsthitam |

kuṇḍaṃ śailadvayāsthaṃ ca mahāpuṇyaṃ mahodayam
vināyakānāṃ śāntyarthaṃ śakrasya ca mahātmanaḥ |
puṇyābhiṣecanaṃ cakre puṣpadanto gaṇottamaḥ
nandine mṛtyunāśāya śatasāhasramuttamam |
laḍaḍukānāṃ dadau yatra tat tīrthaṃ kathaya prabho |

lokānāṃ hitakāmāya kalau pāpapraṇāśanam
brahmovāca |

śṛṇu vatsa pravakṣyāmi yanmāṃ tvaṃ paripṛcchasi |
hitāya sarvvalokānāṃ sarvvapāpaśamāya ca
puṣpadanto gaṇopetastapastapyet sudārūṇam |
puṣpakāntaṃ giriṃ vatsa aṅgāreśasya jāyate
yatrāṇḍajaḥ purā magno gato devapuraṃ mune |
tasya nāmnā samākhyātaṃ tīrthaṃ pāpapraṇāśanam
tasmāduddhṛtya yastoyaṃ śivaliṅgābhiṣecanam |
karoti sa pumān vatsa sarvva kāmānavāpnuyāt
mayāpi tatra deveśaḥ sthāpitaścottareṇa tu |
viṣṇunā nirmmaleśastu paścime gurūṇā param
dakṣiṇena tathā devaṃ kujena īśagocare |
mātṛṇāṃ maṇḍalaṃ yatra nandinā pūjitaṃ purā
anye'pi ye mahādevaṃ carccikāṃ vā mahodayām
bhānuṃ nārāyaṇaṃ vatsa maṅgalāntena cāmbhasā |
snāpayanti mahābhāgā na te prākṛtamānuṣāḥ
ye punaścarccikāṃ kṛtvā prastarādi samudbhavān |
tathā ye cābhiṣiñcanti te labhante hitaṃ phalam
maṅgalā rūpiṇī devī mātṛbhiḥ parivāritā |
vrāhmādyā dakṣiṇe kāryyā vaiṣṇavyādyāstathottare
vrahmā viṣṇuśca rudraśca prabhāmaṇḍala saṃsthitāḥ |
kumāraṃ gaṇanāthañca grahān pīṭhādhaḥsaṃsthitān
evaṃ kṛtvā muniśreṣṭha yatra tatrejitā śivā |
prayacchati paraṃ lokaṃ puṣpāṅke ubhayātmakam
tatra bhāvānurupeṇa mṛccitrā dhātu vārkṣajāḥ |
kṛtvā yastena toyena snāpayet svāmātmanaḥ
jayahomarato dhyānī bhikṣāśī atha kṣīrathaḥ |
ekāntareṇa bhaktena upavāsa ayācitaiḥ
sa labheta hitān kāmān yadā gūḍhavrato bhavet vidyā japtena toyena ayutaṃ vā prayacchati
śivāyāḥ saṃbhaved vatsa sarvvapāpavivarjjitaḥ |
devyāḥ putraḥ sadā loke darśanāccāgha nāśanam
kalaśā hemadhātūtthā mṛnmayā vā sulakṣaṇāḥ loka kumbha caturthāṃśāḥ karttavyāḥ snāpanā śivāḥ
gṛhe ṣoḍaśabhāgena japadhyānaratasya ca |
āyāryyasya sadā vatsa homayuktiḥ prakīrttitā
nārada uvāca |

vidyāhaṃ śrotumicchāmi sarvvapāpa praṇāśinīm |
yathā snānaṃ prakarttavyaṃ devī devasya vā vibho
brahmovāca |

kathayāmi muniśreṣṭha na deyā adīkṣite kvacit |
vidyā mṛtyunjayā nāma daśāvaraṇasaṃstutā
vrāhmaṇaḥ ṣaṣṭha varṇena viṣṇunāḥ pacaṃma tathā |
vājyanāda vilomantu tena tat bhedayenmune
dvitīyaṃ bhavate varṇa viṣṇu varṇacaturthaṃ tathā |
vrahama paṃcamasaṃyuktaṃ tṛtīyaṃ parikīrtitam
vāyuvarṇa gata varṇa savisargantu paṃcamam |
caturthaḥ kīrtitaṃ vatsa sarvvakāma samṛddhaye
vedāḍhyo matimantrasthā vidyā sāvākhyarā mune |
sakṛduccaritā vatsa mṛtyuhā vidhinā bhavet
anayā snāpitā devī sarvvakāmān prayacchati |
yāge vā rudrake yājyā padme vā grahanāśinī
pratyanugaṃ ṣaṭkaṃtu dvayakṣaraṃ prathamaṃ hṛdi |
homaṃ samastamuccārya kāryaṃ svāhāṃtikaṃ sadā
nārada uvāca |

kalaśānāṃ pramāṇantu japahomena kīrtitam |
dineṣu keṣu karttavyaṃ kathayasva prasādataḥ
mārkanḍeya muniśreṣṭha purāṇe samudāhṛtam |
narmaṃdāyāṃ sarasvatyāstairdānakṣe mune'tra tu
cartudaśyāmamāvaśyā8maṣṭamyāṃ navamī tathā |
dvādaśyāṃ paurṇamāsyānca saṃkrāntau grahaṇādiṣu
vyatīpāte dinacchidre caitrādiṣu ca parvvaṣu |

tatrastā devatāḥ sarvā kunḍe santarpitā surāḥ
pitṛṇāṃ bhavate prītistajjabalane anuttamā |

sa kṛtvā daśa varṣāṇi tena santarpitā pitṛn |

tatra kunḍa gate vṛkṣaṃ samārūhya sakhīvṛtaḥ |
krīḍamāno'patat toye paṃcatvamupagatañca saḥ

tatrāhaṃ bhramamāṇā tu gatā kiṣkindhyaparvatam

mayāpi kramamādāya gṛhītumudyamaḥ kṛtaḥ |
kramānnataṃ gṛhītantu pakṣaiḥ pāṃśu nivāritā
pūrṇadattakramānneva grahītuṃ pāṃśu mārjjitā |
tāvat tasmin samāyātaḥ pūjako devalo dvijaḥ
vayaṃ naṣṭā bhayāt kālānmṛtā jātā vasorgṛhe |
candramitrasya tenaiva dattāhaṃ prathamā vadhūḥ
rājñī triṃśatsahasrānāmabhūdahaṃ tatprabhāvataḥ |
akāmā devatāgāre pakṣapātasya mārjjanāt
tena rājñī ceyaṃ yātā kāmān sammārjjanena kim |
phalaṃ bhavati yaddevyā tanna vedmi yathācyatām
evaṃ pūrvvaṃ kathecchambhu rbhārgavasya prapṛcchataḥ |

brahmaṇā devarājasya mayāpi ca tavākhilam
kathitaṃ jīrṇa saṃskāre sammārjanaphalaṃ nṛpa
iti śrī devīpurāṇe sammārjjanamāhātmyaṃ nāma ekonāśītitamo'dhyāyaḥ
aśītitamo'dhyāyaḥ |

vidyeśvara uvāca |

kathaṃ devyāḥ sadā pūjā tadbhaktai rgṛhapālakaiḥ |
karttavyā siddhimicchadbhiḥ dṛṣṭādṛṣṭaphalārthibhiḥ
agastya uvāca |

devyā bhaktaiḥ sadā devī sarvagā sarvasaṃśritā |
dṛṣṭavyā nāgagulmeṣu tṛṇapakṣisarīsṛpe
dvija-anttyaja jātiṣu duḥkhiteṣu sukheṣu ca |

na kruṣṭaḥ krodhamāgacchenna ca pūjā sukṛṣyate |
tṛṇa hema viśeṣeṇa na lobho na ca kāmitā
paradāra parasvādervācyā manakarmabhiḥ |
yasya notsahate rājan tasya devī na dūrataḥ
bhūṣito'pi varaṃ devaṃ kiṃ vane nivasan nṛpaḥ |
sakāmenaiva siddhiḥ syānniṣkāmasya gṛhaṃ vanam
yastu sarvvaprajāpālaḥ sarvavarṇāśramejyakaḥ |
svena vartmani varttteta sa durgāṃ śakyamījitum
rājovāca |

yadyevaṃ varṇajātīnāṃ devī sarvatra saṃsthitā |
tadahaṃ śrotumicchāmi āśramāṇāṃ ca pālanam
agastya uvāca |

pūrva devena brahmāya śūlinā kathitā kila |
śrutā te manudakṣādyai-rbhṛgumitro'tha kāśyapaiḥ
tathā mayāpi tebhyaśca yathā prāptā tathā tava |
kathayāmi mahārāja devyā bhaktiparo bhavān
yathā āsītpurā rājan mahākalpe narādhipaḥ |
tathā pālaya prajāḥ sarvvā sve sve dharme vyavasthitā
tasya rājasya devendraḥ pṛcchate garuḍadhvajam |
rakṣaṇāya samastasya divyasya sa hite rataḥ
praṇamya taṃ jagannāthaṃ viṣṇu kamalalocanam |
prapṛcchati samastasya brahmādyasya ci kāraṇam
śakra uvāca |

jayānantu mahābāho sarvadevanamaskṛta |
ekamūrttistrimūrttistu pītavāso jagatpriyaḥ
sarvvavyāpi mahākāya sthalabhāvānucārakaḥ |
parāvara parāvastu kāraṇātman namo namaḥ
prakṛtisthaṃ ca bhāveśa vikṛtikhyayaḥ prabhuḥ |
cintyācintyaprameyaśca kālakālanahetavaḥ
dharmādharmamahābhāga bhāvābhāvanamo namaḥ |
mahadādi guṇāvāsa sarvaguṇavivarjitaḥ
śrūyase stavase tvañca vedase vedako bhavān |
sampūjyase pūjako nātha sarvagaḥ sarvakṛtti bhūḥ
avināśa vināśitve pārthivādiprayojane |
tvaṃ bhavān kāraṇābhāva parāpara namostu te
hṛṣīkeśa gadādhārin mahādanukulāntaka |
mahāgadāsidhārāya pṛcchāmi jagaddhetave
evaṃ stutastadā rājan viṣṇuḥ provāca yācyatām |
yat te manasi vartteṃta dadāmi brūhi vāsava
śakra uvāca |

bhagavan rki parā bhaktiḥ kasya vā kriyate sadā |
kasmin dvīpe sthitau puṃbhiryaṣṭavyā sā parāparā
śrī bhagavānuvāca |

ekasmin me dine śakra brahmā yānti caturdaśa |
tisṛṇāṃ tvaṃ ca tatsaṃkhyā brahmāhena purandara
evaṃ varṣa śate pūrṇe yoganidrā parāparā |
tasmina līlayāmyahaṃ śakra punaretat sṛjāmi ca
evaṃ te ca dināḥ pakṣāḥ māsārttava tathāyane |
sa te kālaṃ ca kalpaṃ ca mahākalpaṃ tathaiva ca
bhavate sṛjate śakra yā sā paramakāriṇī |
yoganidrā mahāmāyā sarvādyā na vyavasthitā
sthāpitā parameśena yasmin kāle taducyatām |

ye sthitāstatra deveśa tān kathayasva prasādataḥ
śrībhagavānuvāca |

yathā pṛcchati māṃ śakra ūrdhvaṃ kālapurasya tu |
tathā te kathayiṣyāmi śṛṇuṣva vadato mama
ūṣmodake narakāḥ śakra koṭyaḥ paṃcāśanmānataḥ |
catvāriṃśacchataṃ teṣāṃ pradhānaṃ tannibodhata

pūtipūrṇastathā bhedaḥ stambhaṃ ca rūdhiraṃ vasā |
tāmisramapatuṇḍaśca tīkṣṇāsiśca napuṃsakaḥ

avīcīrauravakumbhīpākāḥ pacyanti pāpakān

vayaṃ kālagnirudrasya śatāṃśena pramāṇataḥ |
mamopari sthitāḥ sapta pātālā manakāmadāḥ
yatra nāgāḥ śūrāḥ rakṣāḥ tiṣṭhanti mama pūjakāḥ
rudrabhaktāstathā cānye brahmadevījyakāḥ pare |
paraṃ tattvamajānantaḥ pṛthagbhāvena bhāvitāḥ
anye sarvagatān sarvān devyāḥ śaktyāvalokitāḥ |
paśyante mama sadbhāvā mumukṣuḥ paragāminaḥ
yasmin ye saṃsthitāḥ śakra tānnibodha samāsataḥ |
ābhāsaṃ karatālaṃ ca śarkara ca gabhastimam
mahātālaṃ sutālaṃ ca saptamaṃ ca rasātalam |
sauvarṇamaṣṭakaṃ śakra na prasīdhyanti cāgamaiḥ
devyā rudraparā lokā mantratantraviśāradāḥ |
svadehānte praviśanti nāgakanyāḥ ramanti ca
aṣṭamaṃ tadvijānīyād vasuratnopaśobhitam |
vibhūti krīḍaṃ saṃkṣepāt kathayāmi surādhipa
prathamaṃ bhāsamānantu tatra hemamayī mahī |
nānāratnasamākīrṇaṃ prāsādaṃ sphaṭikojjvalam
ratnaiśca khacitāḥ stambhā dvārabandhāśca vāsava |
strīsahasrasamārkīrṇaṃ lakṣakoṭibhirekadhā
āvṛtaṃ koṭikoṭīnāṃ prādhānyāt kathayāmi te |
namūciḥ śaṃkukarṇaśca mahānādastṛtīyakaḥ
anantaḥ kūliko nāga elāpatraśca nāgakāḥ |
rākṣasāḥ śūladantaśca raktāḍhyo vikaṭastathā

aṣṭamī cāśvine kṛṣṇā ekabhaktena kārayet |
maṃgalārūpiṇīṃ devīmathavā rurūghātinīm
pūjayennavabhedena gaṃdhamālyanivedanaiḥ |
kanyakāḥ bhojayedvatsa devībhaktāṃśca mānavān
naktena navamī kāryāṃ ayācandaśamīṃ kṣapet |
upavāsamekādaśyāṃ punarevaṃ vidhirbhavet
yāvacchuklāṣṭamī śakra upavāsyā vidhānataḥ |
snānahomajapaṃ pūjā kanyābhojantu pratyaham
karttavyaṃ dvijadvandvena devyā bhaktiratena ca |
navamyāṃ paśughātantu mahiṣādi ajāvikam
karttavyaṃ bhūtavetāla na ca ātmanaḥ kāmyayā |
kanyāḥ alaṃkṛtāstatra dvijāḥ devyāḥ parāyaṇāḥ
naṭanarttakaprekṣāśca rathayātrāṃ sajāgarām |
dānaṃ deyaṃ yathā śaktyā sarveṣāmapi bhaktinā
mahābhairavarūpāṇāṃ asthimālādharāḥ narāḥ |
pūjanīyā viśeṣeṇa vastraśobhādharādiṣu
karttavyā sarvakāmārtha prāpaṇāya surottama |
anena vidhinā śakra yadṛcchaṃ labhate phalam
maṃgalā bhairavī durgā vārāhī tridaśeśvarī |
umā haimavatī kanyā kapālī kaiṭabheśvarī
kālī brāhmī māheśī ca kaumārī madhusūdanī |
vārāhī vāsavī carccā nāmānyanyāni japennaraḥ
pūjayed bhojayet kanyāḥ śāstradṛṣṭena karmaṇā |
vastrālaṃkārakāñcayādi kaṭakāḥ kaṭisūtrakāḥ
dātavyā ātmanaḥ śaktyā devībhaktaiḥ sukhārthibhiḥ |
athavā nava rātrāṇi saptapaṃcatrirekadhā
ekabhaktena naktena ayācan upavāsanaiḥ |
kṣapayedāśvine śakra yāvacchuklā tu aṣṭamī
pūjayenmaṃgalā tatra maṇḍale vidhikalpite |
sarvasadbhāvasampanne sarvāvidhividhāyike
sarvakāmaprade śakra sarvakāmānavāpnuyāt |
arthakāmasya arthaṃ tu rājyakāmasya rājyadam
putra ārogyadaṃ vatsa mahāpātakanāśanam |
sarvavarṇaiśca karttavyaṃ puṃstrībāla napuṃsakaiḥ
sarvagā sarvadā devī yasmācchakra mahāphalā |
anayā vidhinā vatsa dadate avicāraṇāt
sarveṣāṃ bratayonīnāṃ sarvabratamahāphalam |
navamyākhyaṃ mahāpuṇyaṃ tava samyak prakāśitam
nākhyeyaṃ bhaktihīnasya mūrkhasyāhetu vādine |
deyaṃ bhaktāya śāntāya śivaviṣṇuratāya ca
devībhaktaḥ sadācāraḥ kanyāpūjārato naraḥ |
ihaiva sarvakāmāni labhate avicāraṇāt
nādhayo vyādhayastasya na ca śatrubhayaṃ bhavet |
saṅgare vijayo nityaṃ mahāneko'pi jāyate
śravaṇātsarvakāmāni labhate avicāraṇāt
iti śrī devīpurāṇe aṣṭamī navamī vrataṃ nāmaikonanavatitamo'dhyāyaḥ

navatitamo'dhyāyaḥ |

śakra uvāca |

yadyevaṃ sarvadevānāṃ paramā mātarā vibho |
tadahaṃ śrotumicchāmi teṣāñca vidhipūjanam
kāni puṣpāṇi dānāni bratāni niyamāstathā |
yena sampūjitā devyaḥ kṣipraṃ siddhi phalapradāḥ
lokānāmupakārāya asmākaṃ ca viśeṣataḥ |
etadeva yathādeśaṃ kathaya naḥ prasādataḥ
evaṃ pūrva nṛpaśreṣṭha viṣṇuḥ śakreṇa pṛṣṭavān |
tat samājñāya śakrasya brahmaṇā kathitaṃ yathā
tathāhaṃ te pravakṣyāmi vidyātattvārthapāraga |

agastya uvāca |

pure vā yadi vā grāme nagare kheṭake'pi vā
dṛṣṭādṛṣṭaphalārthibhiḥ pūjanīyāstu mātaraḥ |
ekaliṃgai nadītīre drumaśaile vane'pi vā |

pūjitāḥ sarvavidyanāṃ sādhanāya phalapradāḥ |
gṛhe catvare haṭṭānte pūjitā dhanaputradāḥ
nagaradvāra pūrvādyā vṛddhirājya sukhārthadāḥ |
gaṃgātīre'thavā vindhye sarvakāmaphalapradāḥ
veda parvata śrīśaile kiṣkindhā parvatādiṣu |
mokṣadā divadā vatsa niṣkāmāḥ phalavāñchitāḥ
ete sthānāḥ samākhyātā āśu phalasamīhakāḥ |
kālāntaraphalā devyaḥ sarvā sarvatrapūjitāḥ
kālāgniśivaparyantā yeṣāṃ vyāptimahātmanām |
tā yatra yatra pūjyante tatraiva phaladāyakāḥ
sarvadevanutā devyaḥ sarvadevaprasūtayaḥ |
śivādyā yābhirjāyante kastāḥ na pratipūjayet
yā sūte prathamaṃ śambhurbrahmaviṣṇuvivasvataḥ |
ādityavaruṇacandrārkaḥ kastāṃ na pratipūjayet
tāsāñca śubhaṛkṣāhe dārumānīya buddhimān |
maṇimauktikavaiḍūrya kāṣṭhacandana candanāḥ
madhūkapāthavilvāmra aśokatindukaśiṃśapāḥ |
śailapārthiva hemotthāstāvaddhātu śubhapradāḥ
tadvidairghaṭitā vatsa tadvedibhiḥ pratiṣṭhitāḥ |
tāścottarānanāḥ sthāpyāḥ sarvakāmaphalepsubhiḥ
sarvaśailaiṣṭakāṣṭotthaṃ gṛhaṃ vāstuvibhājitam |
valabhī maṇḍapaṃ vatsa maṭhaṃ vā sthāpane śubham
gandhaṃ naivedya dhūpena valimālyavibhūṣaṇaiḥ |
adhivāsana pūrvāstu sthāpanīyā yathā kramam
vedadhvani mahāghoṣaiḥ strīsaṃgītopaśobhitam |
karttavyaṃ sthāpanaṃ teṣāṃ vahuvāditranāditam
rātrau jāgaraṇaṃ tatra devyā pūjārthavṛdvaye |
ākhyānairmātarā śāstraiḥ rudrakrīḍākaraiḥ śubhaiḥ
daśāvatārapūrvāstu kathā vācyā yathākramam |
evaṃ pratyūṣasi samprāpte baliṃ saṃdhyāsu dāpayet
yathā mātṛgaṇaṃ pūjyaṃ devabhairavarūpiṇam |
strīsaṃghāḥ kanyakā viprā pūjanīyāḥ svaśaktinā
maṭhañca kārayettatra devyāḥ pūjārthavṛddhaye |
sarvalakṣaṇasaṃpūrṇaṃ sarvopakaraṇānvitam
vāpīkūpaṃ taḍāgaṃ vā vāṭikāvana śobhitam |
veśyātūryopasampannaṃ dhvajachatra vibhūṣitam
ghaṇṭādarpaṇadīpādyaṃ deyaṃ dravyānurūpataḥ |
ghaṭikāyantrayaṣṭyādi dinasaṃkhyārthasiddhaye
karttavyānekamekaṃ vā yathākālaparicchade |
anena vidhinā vatsa mātarāḥ sthāpayennaraḥ
ihaiva pūjanīyāstu mṛto yāti parāṃ gatim
ye tasya dāsakarmāṇi dāsyo veśyādikā gṛhe |

te'pi yānti divaṃ vatsa kiṃ punastasya vāndhavāḥ
iti śrī devīpurāṇe mātṛpratiṣṭhā mahābhāgyaṃ nāma navatitamo'dhyāyaḥ

ekanavatitamo'dhyāyaḥ |

agastya uvāca |

brāhmaṇaḥ kṣatriyo vaiśyaḥ śūdro vā yadi vā striyaḥ |
pūjayenmātaro bhaktyā sa savāmÌllabhatepsitān

ekāṃ vā yadi vā devī devaṃ vā vallakīkaram |
gajānanayutaṃ skandaṃ sarvakāmaphalapradam
brāhmī ca vaiṣṇavīṃ devīṃ kaumārīṃ śakradharmajām |
pūjyamāno avāpnoti aihikaṃ phalamuttamam

brahmāpi pūjayate yāṃ viṣṇurdevastrilocanaḥ |
tāṃ pūjaya sadā devīṃ suraśatrunivarhiṇīm

ekoccāreṇa bhūdānaṃ dattaṃ bhavati bhūmipa |

vidyādānaṃ dadadvatsa ekadhā daśadhā bhavet |
śatadhā koṭidhā gacchedihāpi vidyāpāragaḥ
rājñā taskara dāyārderjala vahni sarisṛpaiḥ |
sarvadānāni kriyante vidyā kenāpi na kriyate
vidyādānena dānāni nahi tulyāni vuddhimān |
vidyā eva paraṃ manye yattat padamanuttamam
śṛṇvannutpadyate bhaktirbhaktyā gurumupāsate |
sa ca vidyāgamān vakti vidyā granthāśritā nṛpa
vidyāvivekavodhena śubhāśubhavicāriṇaḥ |
vindate sarvakāmāpti tasmādvidyā parāgatā
vidyādānātparaṃ dānaṃ na bhūtaṃ na bhaviṣyati |
yena dattena cāpnoti śivaṃ paramakāraṇam
vidyāvicāratattvajño rājñaḥ sanmārgagāminaḥ |
bhuñjate'pi hi bhogāni gacchanti paramāṃ gatim
antyajā api yāṃ prāpya krīḍante graharākṣasaiḥ |
sā vidyā kena mīyeta yasyāḥ sarpāḥ na sarpiṇaḥ
yavena kuñjaraṃ hanti sarṣapena turaṃgamam |
makṣikāpadamātrasya viṣasya viṣamā gatiḥ
evaṃvidhaṃ viṣaṃ vatsa vidyāmantraprabhāvataḥ |
jīryate bhakṣitaṃ pumbhistasmādvidyā parāparā
na hi vidyā kulaṃ jātiṃ rūpaṃ pauruṣapātratām |
eṣā te sarva lokānāṃ paṭhitā upakārikā
bhūtairgrahītā vidhvastā daṣṭā vā mahāpannagaiḥ |
vidyā utthāpayedvatsa antyajasyāpi saṃsthitā

kṣatriyāṇāṃ tu vīryeṇa viprāṇāṃ śāstrapāragaḥ

caturhastapramāṇena śubhaṃ tu caturasrakam |

śakra uvāca |

tvameva paramo deva vedavedāntapūjitaḥ |
tvayāpi kathitā devī pūjitā śivaviṣṇunā
sā ca sarvaṃgatā śāntā śivakālāgnivyāpakā |
yatra yatra ca pūjyet tatra tatra phalapradā
kṛtaṃ divasasāmarthyaṃ tretāyāṃ yajña karmaṇā |
dvāpare yajanādhyayanāt sidhyante hyavicāraṇāt
evaṃ pūrva tvayā nātha sūcitaṃ na prakāśitam |
kalā ghore mahāprāpte yuge ca tamasāvṛte
viṣṇoḥ kṛṣṇatvamāpannai kathaṃ devī varapradā |
kasmin sthāne sthitā nityaṃ dvīpe vā pṛthivītale
etadākhyāhi me tāta prasīta surasattama
brahmovāca |

sādhu sādhu mahāprājña nigūḍhārtha vivecaka |
sandehavinivṛtyarthaṃ pṛṣṭhakaṃ śubhamicchatā
yathaiva bhavatā pṛṣṭaṃ devī sarvatragā śivā |
yathā ca nātra saṃdehastathaiva kathayāmi te
yā sā ghoravadhārthāya sarvaṃ deva namaskṛtā |
vindhyādrau saṃsthitā devī sā ca pūjyā yathāvidhiḥ
mantrādravya kriyādhyānānmahāsiddhikarā nṛṇām |
strī bāla vikalāndhānāṃ sā bhavet sūkṣmasiddhidā
sarvakāmapradā loke sarvaiṣāmapi vāsava |
himavatyacale nandā devī pratyakṣasiddhidā
sā ca saṃsmaraṇāt dhyānāt yātrāniyamakarmaṇi |
sidhyate yena vidhinā śivena kathitā purā
devyāyāṃ mama govinda ṛṣīṇāṃ paripṛcchatām |
tathā te kathayiṣyāmi śṛṇu tattvena vāsava
agastya uvāca |

evaṃ pṛṣṭaḥ purā brahma devarājena vidyapa |
mahābhāgyantu devyāyāḥ nandāyā yatphalaṃ punaḥ
tīrthayātrāphalaṃ puṇyaṃ yathā devyā prapṛcchitam |
tatte'haṃ saṃpravakṣyāmi yathāvadanupūrvaśaḥ |

sūryalokaṃ labhedrājan brahmaṇā kathitaṃ yathā
iti śrīdevīpurāṇe devīmāhātmyaṃ nāma dvinavatitamo'dhyāyaḥ |

trinavatitamo'dhyāyaḥ |

agastya uvāca |

kailāśaśikhare ramye nānādhātuvicitrite |
anekāśiravarākīrṇe gaṇagandhasevite
sahasrakiraṇopete taptakāñcana bhūṣite |
devatāṛá¹ṣibhiścaiva sadāsiddha niṣevite
vimāna koṭisaṃcchanne vitānadhvaja śobhite |
nṛtyanti tatra vai kecit kecidvadanti dundubhim
gāyanti gaṇagandharvā nṛtyanti devayoṣitaḥ |
stotramudīrayantyanye anye vijayamaṃgalaiḥ
stuvanti bhagavandevamṛṣayaśca mahātapāḥ |
candrādityagrahāścaiva tathā tārāgaṇā api
ye cānye tridaśāḥ siddhā yogasiddhā mahāmakhaiḥ |
śakrādyā lokapālāśca brahmaviṣṇumarūdgaṇāḥ
sarve basanti tatraiva divyaiśvaryasamanvitāḥ |
praṇamya prāñjalirdevī idaṃ vacanamabravīt
kautuhalaṃ mahādeva utpannaṃ me maheśvara |
marttyaloke mahādeva guptasthānāni kathyatām
kathayasva prasādena lokānāṃ hitakāmyayā |
anivarttakāni tīrthāni guhyasthānāni me prabho
tanme brūhi sureśāna yadyahaṃ tava vallabhā |
śrotumicchāmyahaṃ praśnaṃ nandādevyā mahātmanā
kathaṃ deva praviṣamaṭo'sau himavaṃte mahāgirau |
tīrthayātrāphalaṃ deva kīdṛśaṃ bhavati prabho
anivarttakāni mārgāni kuṇḍapraveśameva ca |
prasīdati yathā devī sukṛteneha karmaṇā
narake pacyamānānāṃ narāṇāṃ parameśvara |

īśvara uvāca |

śṛṇudevi pravakṣyāmi yathā devī vyavasthitā
śṛṇvantu devatāḥsarvā ye cānye ca tapodhanāḥ |
kathyamānāṃ ca tīrthānāṃ yathā devyā pracoditam
evaṃ śrutvā tathā brahmā śivasya vacanaṃ śubham |
sarve caivāgatāstatra śivasya purataḥ sthitāḥ
ahopūrvāṇi kathyante sarve kautuhalānvitāḥ |
āgataste samīpe tu devāsuramahoragāḥ
bhāvitātmānaśca te sarveṃ hṛṣṭaromā samudgatāḥ |
pārvatyāstu praśaṃsante yayedaṃ pṛcchitaḥ śivaḥ
mātā devāsurāṇāñca vandyā ca parameśvarī |
paśūnāñca hitārthāya mokṣārthañca tapasvinām
pṛcchate ca tato devī nandāśāstraṃ sudurlabham |
kotuhalānvitā devyā śṛṇvantu śivabhāvitā
kṛtāñjalipuṭāḥ sarve sarve praṇatamūrttayaḥ
īśvara uvāca |

himavatyacale ramye nānā siddhaniṣevite |
apsarogaṇasaṃkīrṇe nānāvṛkṣasamākule
kinnarīgaṇasaṅkīrṇe ṛṣayaśca tapodhanāḥ |
nityaṃ sevanti tatsthānaṃ parvataṃ bhūdhareśamavaram
tasminpuṇyāni tīrthāni guhyasthānāni yāni ca |
anivarttakāni catvāri tāni śṛṇvantu devatāḥ
bhairavaṃ caiva kedāraṃ tathā rudraṃ mahālayam |
nandādevī caturthaṃ tu paṃcamaṃ nopalabhyate
śivatīrthāni guhyāni kathitāni mahītale |
adhunā sampravakṣyāmi nandātīrthasya yatphalam
yathā gaṃgā nadīnāntu uttamatvena saṃsthitā |
tadvadbhagavatī nandā uttamatve vyavasthitā
nagendrāṇāṃ yathā meruruttamo vai vyavasthitaḥ |
tārakāṇāṃ yathā candraḥ prabhutvena mahātape |

tīrthānāñca tathā nandā prabhutvena vyavasthitā
grahānāñca yathā prabhutvena vyavasthitaḥ |
tadvat kṣetraṃ mahādevī nandāyāḥ parameśvari
khagendrāṇāṃ prabhuryadvat suparṇo acalātmaje |
tadvat tīrthaṃ mahādevī nandāyāḥ uttamaṃ priye
phaṇīndrāṇāṃ yathā rājā vāsukistridaśārcite |
tīrthānāmuttamaṃ tadvat naṃdākhyaṃ surasundari
ṛṣīṇāṃ ca yathā vandyaḥ kaśyapo bhṛgureva ca |
nandātīrthaṃ mahādevī vandyaṃ puṇyaṃ ca kīrttitam
yoṣitānāṃ yathā bhadre rājñī tvaṃ suranāyaki |
devatānāmahaṃ devi nandātīrthaṃ tathā priye
tasmāt kiṃ bahunoktena varṇitena punaḥ punaḥ |
mokṣasthānaṃ yathā devi anaupamyaṃ surārccite
anaupamyaṃ tathā tīrthaṃ nandākhyaṃ parameśvari |
pṛthivyāntu sthito vāpi nandādevīṃ prakīrttayet
mucyate sarvapāpebhyo yaḥ smaredbhāvitātmanaḥ |
nandāsthānaṃ narāḥ prāpya na te prākṛta mānuṣāḥ
ye brajanti ca tatraiva anivarttaṃpathe sthitāḥ |
aśvamedhaphalaṃ teṣāṃ narāṇāṃ tu pade pade
ye mṛtāstu pathe devī kuṇḍe vā narapuṃgavāḥ |
na teṣāṃ vidyate martye punarāgamanaṃ priye
sarvatīrtheṣu yatpuṇyaṃ sarvayajñeṣu yatphalam |
sarvadāneṣu yatproktaṃ tapaścāndrāyaṇādibhiḥ
koṭi koṭi guṇaṃ kṛtvā yatpuṇyaṃ sakalaṃ bhavet |
nandā sandarśanāddevi bhavate suvicāraṇāt
devyuvāca |

aśvamedhaṃ mahāyajñaṃ tapaścāndrāyaṇādikam |
devyāḥ saṃdarśanenātha vyarthametattathāgamāḥ
parameśvara uvāca |

na bhayaṃ naiva lobho me sneho vā suravandite |
ajñatvaṃ vātha dīnatvaṃ yenāhamanṛto dhruvam
tapoyajñeṣu devānāṃ santarpaṇavidhirmataḥ |
te ca brahmādayo bhadre taistu nandā pratiṣṭhitā
yo'sāvanādimadhyāntaḥ śivaḥ śaktimayaḥ paraḥ |
tasyeyaṃ paramā nandā sarvakilbiṣanāśinī
tatprabhāvena prāpnoti tapo yajñādikaṃ phalam |
maṃtrāṇāṃ devaśaktīnāṃ na vicāro varānane
kālikā hāsyavākyāni grahabhūtaviṣāpahāḥ |
evaṃ kaliyuge ghore yasmin dehāntarā narāḥ
bhuñjanti darśanātkanyā tasya kiṃ tapasādikam |
aśvamedhādikaṃ bhadre yena tvaṃ vismayaṃ gatā
aṃguṣṭhodaramātreṇa boḍhuryanmaṇinā phalam |
na tatsahasrapāṣāṇān vahanaṃ prāpnoti mānava
veda evaṃ hi dharmāṇāṃ pravaro dharmadarśakaḥ |
tasmin sā pūjyate devī mānastoketi veda sā
devyuvāca |

lokānāṃ tu manojñānaṃ utdyotanaṃ prati prabho |
pūrvapakṣānyahaṃ nātha samyagyātrāṃ nibodhaya
parameśvara uvāca |

māse bhādrapade devi śuklapakṣe vrajetsadā |
tasyecchā śrāvaṇe'ṣāḍhe anyathā na kadācana
teṣāñca candranāgastu pīḍāṃ kuryāt sulocane |
na gacchanti surāḥ siddhāḥ kiṃ punarmānuṣādayaḥ
viṣavātahatāḥ keciddhimavātaprapīḍitāḥ |
vimucyante narā devi yānti devyā prasādataḥ
pāpakarmmā narā ye tu gaṇādhyakṣo nivārayet |
śeṣānvai candranāgastu nityaṃ rakṣati tadgataḥ
kapilaḥ piṃgalaścaiva dhūmaketurmahābalaḥ |
somakaścandranāmaśca rakṣanti baladarpitāḥ
nityaṃ rakṣanti tattīrthaṃ paṃcakoṭi samanvitāḥ
umovāca |

kiṃ purasya tu vistāraḥ kā siddhiḥ kā ca ramyatā |
ko vā vinyāso harmyāṇāṃ kena vā nirmitāni ca
kimpramāṇantu kanyānāṃ ko veṣo varṇayauvanam |
udyānāḥ kīdṛśāścaiva dīrghikā vāpi kīdṛśī
kiṃ vā vadanti tāḥ kanyāḥ nandāyāḥ purataḥ sthitāḥ |
kāntasya ca kathaṃ prāptistāsāṃ vara sureśvara
katareṇa tapenaiva marttyā bhuñjanti tāḥ striyaḥ |
kasmiṃstu pūjitā devī kṣipraṃ pratyakṣatāṃ vrajet
kasmin kṣetre drutā siddhirniyamena kena prabho |
liṃgānāṃ lakṣaṇaiścaiva yasmin sidhyanti sādhakāḥ
samayāśca kati proktā mantroddhāraśca kīdṛśaḥ |
kīdṛśaṃ yajanaṃ devyā rupakaṃ caiva kīdṛśam
etatsarvaṃ yathānyāyaṃ kathayasva prasādataḥ
īśvara uvāca |

nandā devyā purī ramyā bhogādyā suravanditā |
vasanti tatra vai kanyā satataṃ madanāturāḥ
pādapadmaṃ sadā pūjyaṃ nandāyā varavarṇini |
śocayanti sadātmānaṃ nandāyā agrataḥ sthitāḥ
aśrupātajalaughena soṣṇena tu varāṃganāḥ |
nandāyā pādapadmau tu ajasraṃ kṣālayanti tāḥ
kanyakā ūcūḥ
kiṃ kāryaṃ jalakrīḍāyāṃ dolākrīḍanakena kim |
udyānakrīḍanairvāpi dyūtakrīḍanakena kim
pustakavācanenāpi kāvyākhyāyikakrīḍayā |
vīṇā śāstreṇa kiṃ kāryaṃ citrapatraparicchadaiḥ
unmattaceṣṭitaṃ sarvaṃ patihīnaṃ mahātape |
mṛdaṃgapaṭahai śabdairvallakīpanavādibhiḥ
nṛtyavāditrakaṃ sarvaṃ patihīnaṃ na rājate |
veṇu vīṇāninādena vipaściddhvanināditaiḥ
kimvā lambūkavīṇāyāṃ kāryaṃ piñjalakena kim |
vyādhitasya yathākrandastadvat tartrordhvaniḥ smṛtā
araṇyaruditaṃ sarva vidhavānāṃ sureśvari |
kiṃ vā rūpeṇa karttavyaṃ kāryaṃ yauvanena ca
makarīkarapatraiśca payodharakapolayoḥ |
lalāṭairtilakairvāpi vinyastaiḥ kiṃ prayojanam
ko vā āgatya marttyo'smin yaḥ pariṣvajya marddayet |
vastrairvilepanairdivyaiḥ sragdāma bhramarākulaiḥ
mukuṭaiścuṭakairvāpi kimvā lalāṭapaṭṭikaiḥ |
yadvadbhittiṣu citrāṇāṃ maṇḍanaṃ tadvanniṣphalam
dayāṃ kuru surādhyakṣe nānyastrātā sureśvari |
evaṃ yācanti deveśi bharttāraṃ nandamandire
udyānadīrghikairvāpi pravālāṅkura śobhitaiḥ |
kvacitsphaṭikasopānaiḥ kvacinmarakata sañcitaiḥ
kvacidhāṭakasambhūtaiḥ indranīlamayaiḥ kvacit |
rajovarttamayairdivyaiḥ kvacidvajravinirmitaiḥ
tapanīyodbhavaiḥpadmaiḥ kvacidvidru masannibhaiḥ |
sitāsitaistathā raktaiḥ śrīmukhairmukharaistathā
haṃsasārasasaṃgītaiḥ jīvaṃ jīvakanāditaiḥ |
nānāpakṣigaṇaiḥ ramyaiḥ śobhante dīrghikāḥ sadā
kāntahīnā mahādevi vani ca puṣkariṇīva |
