varaṃ martyā ca vanitā patimāśritya saṃsthitā
patihīnā na śobhante ambike kalpajīvitā |
ayutaṃ yojanānāntu nandādevyāḥ purī priye
koṭi koṭibhiḥ strīṇāntu samantāt pūritā purī |
citrāmbaradharāḥ sarvāścitragandhānulepanāḥ
citramālyadharāḥ nityaṃ citrābharaṇabhūṣitāḥ |
citravarṇadharāḥ sarvāḥ vicitragatigāmini
nānāvādyaratā nityaṃ nānāgandharvatatparāḥ |
nānākrīḍāpramattāstu nānālekhyaratāḥ sadā
nānā śāstrārtha saṃpannā nānālekhyaratāḥ striyaḥ |
akṣīṇayauvanāḥ sarvā jarāmṛtyuvivarjitāḥ
nandā puravare kanyāḥ madhyamādhamavarjitā
umovāca |

rūpātiśayasampanā nānāguṇasamanvitāḥ |
kimarthaṃ dukhitāḥ jātā kāntasaukhyavivarjitāḥ
īśvara uvāca |

damayantī yathā sītā rūpātiśayapāragā |
duḥkhitāstena saṃjātā kāntasaukhya vivarjitāḥ
ahalyā baṃdhakī jātā gotamasya tu yoṣitā |
rūpasya tu prabhāveṇa dāsī jātā tilottamā
tasmādrūpaṃñca necchanti lakṣaṇajñāstapodhanāḥ |
atirūpeṇa svalpāyuḥ puruṣo yoṣito'pi vā
athavā saumyahīnastu jāyate tu mahātape |
nandāpuravare devi kanyakānāntu ceṣṭitam
udāhṛtaṃ mayā bhadre yathā pṛṣṭhaṃ tvayā priye |
pūjāsthānāni vakṣyāmi yasmin sānnidhyatāṃ vrajet
liṃgasthāṃ pūjayeddevīṃ sthaṇḍilasthāṃ tathaiva ca |
pustakasthāṃ mahādevīṃ pāduke pratimāsu ca
citre ca triśikhe khaḍge jalasthāṃ vāpi pūjayet |
agnisthāṃ pūjayetprājño hṛdaye vā suśobhane
ebhiḥ sthānairmahādevī pūjitā varadā bhavet |
mama pārśve śrutaṃ yaistu jñātaṃ devi tapodhanaiḥ
te'pi vandyā ahaṃ yadvacchivadharmaparāyaṇāḥ |
talliṃgamāśrayenmantrī śukrādyairyatpratiṣṭhitam
kacādyairyat kṛtaṃ liṃgaṃ varjaṃnīyantu sādhakaiḥ |
kalpasaukhyapradaṃ proktaṃ vedamantraiḥ pratiṣṭhitam
sādhikāraṃ tu yalliṃgaṃ muktabhogaṃ tathaiva ca |
jñātavyaṃ sādhakendreṇa siddhidaṃ cāpyasiddhidam
sādhikāraṃ tu yalliṃgaṃ vedamantraiḥ pratiṣṭhitam |
nivarttitavikārañca uktaṃ śaṃbhuṃ svayaṃbhuvam
kurvanti bhakti vātsalyaṃ lokānāṃ vāsanātmakam |
durvijñeyamidaṃ jñānaṃ yogināmapyagocaram |

marttyairjaḍadhiyainathi kathaṃ vijñāyate prabho
īśvara uvāca |

sādhu sādhu mahādevi rahasyamidamuttamam |
yattvayā coditaṃ bhadre tathaiva ca na cānyathā
durvijñeyaṃ suraiścāpi kiṃ punarmarttya jantubhiḥ |
ādhiṣṭo sādhakaṃ jñeyaṃ hṛdayānandakārakam
indriyāṇāṃ cautsukyaṃ dadāti liṃgadarśane |
sevyamānaṃ tato liṃgaṃ nityānandapradāyakam
susvapno paśyate nityaṃ vimānasthāṃ varāṃganām |
bhairavaṃ paśyate nityaṃ krīḍantaṃ mātṛmaṇḍale
umāmaheśvaraṃ vāpi svapne paśyati sādhakaḥ |
anivartti tādhikārañca liṃgaṃ ca tribhuvaneśvaram
ākrāmanti mahāvighnāḥ sadaityāḥ rākṣasādayaḥ |
śūnyāgāraṃ yathā devi ākrāmanti narāḥ priye
anarcitantu bhuñjanti tathā liṃgantu kaśmalāḥ |
pretaṃ tathā surādhyakṣe ākrāmanti piśācakāḥ |

śūnyaṃ ca vāṃgaliṃgantu āśrayanti tathā priye
śrīdevyuvāca |

paryāptañca śrutenaiva tava vākyena śaṃkara |
viśeṣotpādito mahyaṃ sutarāṃ gahanaṃ kṛtam
sūkṣmarūpā yadā vighnāḥ rākṣasā bhūtanāyakāḥ |
īdṛśīṃ tanumāsthāya liṃgaṃ bhuñjanti vai sadā
tadā te'pi manoramyaṃ sthānaṃ kurvanti śaṃkara |
sādhakasya sadānandaṃ te'pi kurvanti nityaśaḥ
svapnāṃśca śobhanān devī sādhakasya dadanti ca |
pūjārthino mahāvīryāḥ prītiṃ kurvanti sādhake
prabhāvayanti duṣṭātmā vadanti varadā bhava |
tasya varṣaśatenāpi kutaḥ siddhiḥ prajāyate
īśvara uvāca |

mahācodyaṃ mahādevi anaupamyaṃ surārccite |
brahmādyairapi deveśai rīdṛśaṃ na pracoditam
yathāvatkathayiṣyāmi mā viṣādaṃ kurū priye |
aghorāsraṃ nyaset tasmin svādakañca mahābalam
daṃṣṭraiḥ karakarāyantu jvalantaṃ vidiśairdiśaiḥ |
pakṣamekaṃ yathā devi yathāsthānaṃ sukhāvaham
arcyamānaṃ tu talliṃgaṃ svapnaṃ dadati pūrvavat |
sādhikāraṃ tu talliṃgamāśusiddhipradāyakam
ajāvikakharoṣṭraiśca ārūḍhāṃ paśyate tanum |
udvegaḥ kalaho nityaṃ sakhāpānāntu jāyate
kṛṣṇāmbaradharāṃ nārīṃ rātrau paśyati sādhakaḥ |
tasmāt kimbahunoktena talliṃgaṃ rākṣasālayam
varjanīyaṃ prayatnena mṛtyurogabhayāvaham |
upāyaṃ sampravakṣyāmi mantrahīne pratiṣṭhite
svayantu paṭhyate loke na ca tathyena sundari |
uṣare tu yathādhānyaṃ sthāpitaṃ niṣphalaṃ bhavet
liṅge mantravihīne tu pūjanaṃ niṣphalaṃ bhavet |
upāyaṃ sampravakṣyāmi tasyāpi mṛdubhāṣiṇi
prasannāṃ dhārayetprājña āveśaṃ vātha paṇḍitaḥ |
svayambhuḥ kalpitañcāpi kathitaṃ siddhibalābalam
pavargāccaturthe varge viparītasulocane |
tasyāpi prathame varge ādibījaṃ tṛtīyakam
prasannā ca sadā devi īṣṭāniṣṭaprasūcanī |
kiṃ vahunoktena svayaṃ saṃkalpite priye
āśrayastatra kurvīta āśusiddhipradāyike |
duṣṭa sattvasamākīrṇe jane bhaktivivarjite
na kuryādāśrayaṃ mantrī diṅmoho yatra jāyate |
na kuryādvidiśe tīrtha snānapānaṃ śivātmani
vāpīkūpataḍāgaṃ vā prāsādaṃ vā niketanam |
na kuryāt tṛtpikāmastu analānile nairṛte
āgneyyāṃ manasastāpye naiṛte krūrakarmakṛt |
agnidāhaṃ sadā kuryāt amānuṣacatuṣpadām
vāyavyāṃ calacittastu prīyamāṇe jale priye |
sthānasya pāvake bhāge vāpīkūpa taḍāgakam
nairṛte pīyamānastu ātmā na duḥkhito bhavet |
kanyāpi tajjalaṃ pītvā patiṃ gṛhṇāti kāmataḥ
prāsādasyottare devi vasanti naiva siddhidāḥ |
vidiśāsu ca sarvāsu chāyākrāntāpi no śubhām
dakṣiṇonnato yā kṣoṇī vāruṇī nairṛtonnatāḥ |
śubhā ca siddhidā nityaṃ sādhakasya janasya vā
dravyāmÌścaiva pravakṣyāmi yathā taiḥ pūjyate priye |
nandā bhagavatī devī siddhidā sādhakasya tu
maṇiratnamayā kāryā hemarūpya mayāpivā |
candanenāpi karttavyā pāduke pratimāpi vā
śrīparṇe śrīdrume cāpi devatārumayī parā |
ṣaḍaṃgulā ca sā kāryāṃ pāduke pūjayetsadā
paṭasya lakṣaṇaṃ vakṣye yathā sidhyanti sādhakāḥ |
granthikeśavihīṃne tu ajīrṇe samatantuke
asphāṭite arcchidre tu sthalenaiva samālikhet |
maṃgalārupiṇī kāryā jayādyaiḥ parivāritā
vīṇāhastā prasaktā tu nānālaṃkāraśobhitā |
jīrṇe tu bhavate vyādhiḥ sphoṭite maraṇaṃ bhavet
keśaiḥ suśokadaṃ vidyāt granthibhiḥ skhalanaṃ bhavet |
chidreṇa utthito vāpi sādhakasya balābale
vṛddhaṃ ca vyādhidaṃ vyāṃgaṃ dīrghaṃ sthūlaṃ kṛśaṃ tathā |
vṛddhena bhavate vṛddho vyādhite vyādhito bhavet
kurūpeṇa kurupaṃ tu mūrkhena tu na pūjyate |
lekhakasya tu yadrūpaṃ citre bhavati tādṛśam
khaḍgasya lakṣaṇaṃ vakṣye triśikhasya ca sundari |
nānāśastrodbhavaṃ kāryaṃ mṛdulauhamayaṃ pivā
sphuṭitaṃ khaṇḍitaṃ hṛsvaṃ savraṇaṃ sandhitaṃ tathā |
mṛdulauhe apūjyastu sandhite maraṇaṃ bhavet
savraṇe'pi hi hṛdroge rekhayā pātakī bhavet |
bhāryā mātā tathā putrā mriyante khaṇḍitena tu
hrasvena lāghavaṃ loke dīrgheṇāpi hyasiddhidam |
anyaśastrodbhavenāpi bhavate maraṇaṃ dhruvam
paṃcāśadaṃgulaṃ khaḍgaṃ triśikhaṃ ca sureśvari |
īdṛśaṃ kārayetprājña āśusiddhiphalapradam
kṛtvā tu pūrvavattyāgaṃ śāstradṛṣṭena karmaṇā |
ālabhetsarvadravyāṇi khaḍgādyān saptapaṃcadhā
atha sarvairya jeddevīṃ nandāṃ tribhuvaneśvarīm |
śākayāvakapiṇyāka kṣīrāśī bhikṣādo'pivā
kandamūlaphalāśī vā japaṃ kuryādvicakṣaṇaḥ |
antaritopavāsena atha naktena varjjayet
trirātreṇa tu vartteta atha cāndrāyaṇādibhiḥ |
homayellakṣamekantu ājyamiśrantu guggulam
athavā śrīphalairvāpi homaṃ kuryādvicakṣaṇaḥ |
trilakṣeṇa labhet khaḍgaṃ triśūlaṃ pāñcalakṣikam
khaḍgena bhavate rājā madhye khecara cāriṇām |
triśūlena sureśāno bhavate nātra saṃśayaḥ
pūrvameva trayo lakṣān japaṃ kṛtvā samārabhet |
anyathā tu mahādevi homaṃ naiva tu kārayet
samayā sampravakṣyāmi yaistuṣṭidaṃ phalaṃ labhet |
śaivāna pāśupatānvāpi mahābratadharāṃ pivā
kumārikāśca taduktān bhojayet pūjayet sadā |
nādyāt strī nāyakān bhaktān na nārīṃ tāḍayet kvacrit
pratāḍayenna cākrośaṃ vivastraṃ naiva kārayet |
prasuptāṃ naiva paśyeta tāḍyamānāṃ nivārayet
mūtraṃ purīṃṣaṃ kurvantīṃ na paśyenna jugupsayet |
naiva tāṃ bhūṣayenmantrī yadīcchecchāśvataṃ padam
majjanti yoṣito yatra śaucaṃ kurvanti yatra vā |
udvahanti jalaṃ yatra tattīrthaṃ pūjayet sadā
mṛdbhasmadaṇḍakāṣṭhāni tasmin tīrthe niveśayet |
sukhapādāvācarantu tattīrthaṃ kārayed budhaḥ
anena tuṣyate devī nandā cānandacāriṇī |
vastraṃ patraṃ tathā bhakṣyaṃ phalaṃ puṣpaṃ vilepanam
nānālaṅkaraṇaṃ devi yatkiṃcijjaladāyikam |
nandāmuddiśya dātavyaṃ tuṣyate tena sā priye
ataḥ paraṃ pravakṣyāmi siddhisthānāni yāni tu |
yasminnārādhitā devī kṣipraṃ bhavati siddhidā
mandāraṃ śataśṛṃgañca trikūṭaṃ parvataṃ tathā |
vindhye gaṃgāsarid yatra revatī yamunāpi vā
payoṣṇī aśvarathye tu athavā kuṇḍaleśvare |
śaṃkareśvara rāmeśe athavā amareśvare
sarasvatītaṭe puṇye sugandhāyatane'pi vā |
sthāneṣveṣu japaṃ kuryānnandā tadagatamānasaḥ
vetravatyātasṭe ramye hariścandre tathā priye |
bhairavaṃ śūlabhedañca caṇḍīśaṃ tripurāntakam
aṣṭacakrañca krauñceśaṃ kapālākṣāgranāmakam |
ajāvikakharoṣṭākhyaṃ sthānānyanyāni varjayet
brahmasyāpi bhavecchipramebhiḥ sthānairmahātapaiḥ |
ūrdhvagaḥ kalaho nityaṃ vratabhaṃgaṃ vināśakṛt
śubhābhidhānakaiḥ sthānaistatra sādhanamārabhet |
caturthīṃ cāṣṭamīṃ naiva navamī vā caturdaśī
śuklapakṣe tu karttavyaṃ devyā yajanamuttamam |
tato nandīśvaro gacchedahorātrantu kārayet
snātvā gaṃgānadī tīre kṛtvā ca udakakriyām |
nandādevīṃ namaskṛtya sarvapāpaiḥ pramucyate
cūbhikāmagame snāyānmahāpātakanāśane |
piṇḍagaṃgā kuśaṃgaṃgā tatra snātvā tu mānavaḥ
devānāṃ tarpanaṃ kuryāt piṇḍaṃ pitṛṣu dāpayet |
ghṛtena madhuvā vāpi saktūn guḍavimiśritān
tilodakaṃ tato dattvā kuśodaka samanvitam
om pitṛbhyaḥ svāhā |
oṃ pitāmahebhyaḥ svāhā |
oṃ prapitāmahebhyaḥ svāhā |
oṃ mātāmahebhyaḥ svāhā |

oṃ umāmaheśvara varebhyaḥ svāhā
piṇḍaṃ dattvā hemamantrai praṇipatya kṣamāpayet |
evaṃ devi vidhiṃ kṛtvā kulānāṃ tārayecchatam
nandāgaṃgāṃ punaḥ snātvā mucyate sarvakilviṣaiḥ |
tato vaitaraṇīṃ gatvā snānaṃ tatraiva dāpayet
devānāmudakaṃ dattvā piṇḍaṃ tatraiva dāpayet |
mahādevaṃ namaskṛtvā sa gaccheduttarāṃ diśam
mahāgaṇapatiṃ dṛṣṭvā pūjāṃ kṛtvā vidhānavit |
gacchedāyatanaṃ divyaṃ devyā bhavanamuttamam
pūjāṃ kṛtvā vidhānajño yāvat praṇatavigrahaḥ |
tāvat taṃ gagane devī vimānasthā savāsavā
abhinandate taṃ dhanyaṃ narendra puṇyabhājanam |
nandādevyāścaraṇābjaṃ yena dṛṣṭaṃ sudurlabham
sarvapāpavinirmuktaḥ śāśvataṃ bhuvanottamam |
anenaiva tu dehena devyāḥ putrantu jāyate
kārttikeyasamo bhūtvā mahāvīryaparākramaḥ |
rtiṣṭhate sūcitaṃ kālaṃ matprasādāna suvrataḥ
tadante vrajate mokṣaṃ bhuktvā bhogān yathepsitān |
devyā dakṣiṇamukho bhūtvā mūlamaṃtraṃ japed vudhaḥ
darśanaṃ jāyate tasya sādhakasya na saṃśayaḥ |
śuklāmvaradharāṃ nārīṃ rātrau paśyati sādhakaḥ
tāṃ dṛṣṭvā jāyate siddhiraṇimādiguṇāṣṭakam |
devyāḥ pradakṣiṇāṃ kṛtvā kuṇḍasya ca viśeṣataḥ
dhyātvā devīṃ tataḥ kuṇḍe praviśenmatsyavajjale |
pauruṣatvaṃ jale tatra trāsaṃ naiva tu kārayet
paśyate kṣaṇamātreṇa strīmukhaṃ dvāramuttamam |
nānāratnamayaṃ divyaṃ hemaprākāra toraṇam
maṇḍape tiṣṭhate devī dvārasyāgre suśobhane
pūrṇakumbhāśca sauvarṇāśca jalapallava maṇḍitāḥ |
nirmitā viśvakarmeṇa sarvaratnamayāḥ śubhāḥ
maṇihemamayaiḥ stambhairvimānairdhvaja śobhitaiḥ |
mauktikadāma mālābhi rmaṇimālābhirmālitam
ghaṇṭācāmara śobhāḍhyamātapatrai virbhūṣitam |
sauvarṇā murajāstatra tiṣṭhante meghanisvanāḥ
indranīlaparicchannaṃ vicitramaṇi carcitam |
śālabhañjika puṣpaiśca ratnapaṃkaja śobhitam
parijātaka mālābhiḥ samantāt parivāritam |
nandā bhagavatī devī pratimārūpa dhāriṇī
tiṣṭhate maṇḍapadvāre sahasrabhujabhūṣitā |
sarvāyudhadharā saumyā puṣpamālā vibhūṣitā
divyagaṃdhānuliptāṃgī kuṃkumāruṇavigrahā |
kuṇḍalaiḥ kaṭakaiyūrairmukuṭādivibhūṣitā
tāṃ dṛṣṭvā tu mahādevī pratimārupadhāriṇīm |
tasyā pradakṣiṇaṃ kṛtvā praṇipatya śivena tu
tasyāgre tiṣṭhate cānyā jayā ca pratihārikā |
dṛṣṭvā tu sādhakaṃ vīraṃ iṣṭastuṣṭo prabhāṣate
svāgataṃ te mahāvīra puṇyabhājo mahātapāḥ |
tiṣṭhantu sādhakā atra yāvatpratyāgamamaham
pṛcchāmi bhagavatīṃ devī tubhyañcaiva praveśanam |
evantu vadate devī jayā dvārasya pālikā
gatā śīghrantu devyāyāḥ samīpaṃ varavarṇinī |
jānubhyāṃ dharaṇīṃ gatvā jayā vadati harṣitā
jayovāca |

āgato marttyo loke'smin dvāre tiṣṭhati sādhakaḥ |
kriyate sāmprataṃ kintu ādeśaṃ vada ambike |

vihasya bhagavatī na ndā idaṃ vacanamabravīt
devyuvāca |

yathā tai pādapadmantu madīyaṃ hṛdaye kṛtam |
mamāpi ca tathā bhadre sādhakā hṛdaye sthitāḥ
mā vidhāraya tān dvāre tvaritantu praveśaya |
iṣṭātuṣṭamanā devi jayā tvaritamāgatā
āgatya sādhakasya tu samīpasthā prabhāṣate
jayovāca |

bho bho vīra mahāsattva devī varapradā |
tatastu viditaṃ vīra apsarairbhaktavatsalaiḥ
īṣṭātuṣṭamanāḥ sarvāḥ nirgatāśca varāṃganāḥ |
cāmaraiḥ kanakadaṇḍaiśca chatrairmaṇivibhūṣitaiḥ
ardhyahastāstathā cānyāḥ puṣpahastāstathā parāḥ |
āgacchanti tataḥ kanyā divyālaṃkārabhūṣitāḥ
kuṃkumāgurūgandhaiśca liptāṃgāḥ sumanoharāḥ |
tilakairardhacandraiśca hemaratnavibhūṣitāḥ
nānālaṃkārasampannāḥ sarvāḥ pīnapayodharāḥ |
padmāṃkavapuṣaḥ sarvāḥ priyaṃgu campakādayaḥ
nīlotpaladalaśyāmā anyā vidyutsamaprabhāḥ |
kāmarūpāstathā cānyā gajendra gativikramāḥ
pūrṇacandrānanāḥ sarvāḥ sarvāstāmṛtasambhavāḥ |
ardhyaṃ pādyaṃ tato dattvā bhāṣyotphullalocanāḥ |

svāgataṃ te mahāvīra ehi gacchāma sādhaka
evamuktvā tataḥ kanyā praviśanti purottamam |
hemaprākāradīptaṃ taṃ maṇitoraṇanupuram
divyagandharvagānāḍhyaṃ divyavādyasamākulam |
indranīlaparicchannaṃ bālākāryutasaṃprabham
dhvajamālākulaṃ sarvaṃ mayūracchatrabhūṣitam |
padmarāgamayai stambhaiḥ kvacit sphāṭikamayaiḥ śubhaiḥ
vidrumāḍhyaistathā cānyai nānāratnamayaistathā |
muraja vādyaśabdaiśca śaṃkhakāhalaniḥsvanaiḥ
geyaiśca madhurairdivyaiḥ śrotrendriya manoharaiḥ |
kanyānāṃ gītaśabdena nityaṃ pramuditaṃ param
dṛśyate maṇḍapaṃ ramyaṃ nāgadaṇḍa vibhūṣitam
padmarāgaparicchannaṃ cāmarairupaśobhitam |
siṃhāsanantu devyāyā nyastaṃ hemamayaṃ śubham
darpaṇairardha candraiśca mauktikāhārabhūṣitam |
anaupamyaṃ mahādevi ratnākaramivotthitam
īdṛśaṃ mandiraṃ divyaṃ nānādhātuvicitram |
tasmiṃstu maṇḍapaṃ prāpya kanyā vacanamavravīt
asmiṃstu maṇḍape vīra nimeṣaṃ tiṣṭha suvrata |
svayamāgacchate devī varaṃ tubhyaṃ prayacchati
evamukttvā tataḥ kanyāḥ praviśanti purottamam |
kṛtañjalipuṭāḥ sarvāḥ kanyāḥ vacanamabrūvan
kanyakā ucuḥ |

āgatā marttyā loke'smin dvāre tiṣṭhanti sādhakāḥ |
śaraṇāgatā mahādevi jayādevyā praveśitāḥ
tāsāṃ tadvacanaṃ śrutvā kanyakānāṃ sureśvari |
siṃhayuktaṃ rathaṃ divyaṃ svayamāruhya rnirgatāḥ
kanyākoṭi sahasrantu devyā saha vinirgatam |
kāścid gacchanti vai hṛṣṭāḥ kāścidvījanti cāmaraiḥ
nṛtyanti kanyakāḥ kāścid kāścitstotraṃ paṭhanti ca |
nānāvādyaratāḥ kāścit nānāgītaratāstathā
kāścijjayajayā śabdaiḥ stuvanti parameśvarīm |
parivāritāḥ kanyaiśca āgatā maṇḍape śubhe
praviṣṭo maṇḍape devyābhyantare bhuvaneśvarī |
siṃhāsanopaviṣṭastu śvetapadmoparisthitā
jaṭā mukuṭa vinyastā bhasmākulita vigrahā |
lalāṭanayanopetā śravaṇāyatalocanā
pūrṇacandrānanā devī payodharabharālasā |
sunitambā sumadhyā ca sarvāvayaśobhitā
bhūṣitā paṭṭamāṇikyai rdivyagandhānulepanā |
sitasragdāmavastraiśca śobhāḍhyā mṛdubhāṣiṇī
svakāntikirarṇaughena purīmudyotya saṃsthitā
śrīdevyuvāca |

praveśya sādhakān sarvānāsanaṃ caiva dīyatām |
devyāstadvacanaṃ śrutvā apsarā nirgatā drutam
ehi vīra mahāsattva praviśābhyantare pure |
tuṣṭā tu te mahādevī varaṃ tubhyaṃ prayacchati
kanyānāṃ vacanaṃ śrutvā sādhakastiṣṭhate tataḥ |
kṛtāñjali puro bhūtvā praviśed bhuvanottamam
daṇḍavat patito bhūmyāṃ devyāgre ca vyavasthitaḥ |
sagadgadaṃ vadedvākyaṃ kiñcidākulitekṣaṇaḥ
sādhaka uvāca |

tvaṃ gatiḥ śaraṇaṃ devi tvaṃ mātā parameśvari |
ahaṃ janmāntare kṣīṇastvāmeva śaraṇaṃ gataḥ
devyuvāca |

svāgataṃ bhadra bhadraṃ te varaṃ me brūhi subrata |
evaṃ sambhāṣito devyā sādhakaḥ puṇyakarmakṛt
muktvā tu mānuṣaṃ dehaṃ vidyābharaṇa bhūṣitaḥ |
bālārkāṇāṃ sahasrasya kāntirvai dhārayati saḥ
surūpaḥ subhagaḥ saumyaḥ mahābalaparākramaḥ |
idaṃ ratnapurī divyā sarva kāma phalapradā
sādhaka tvaṃ prasādena krīḍayasva yathāsukham |
skandatulyabalo bhūtvā yāvadāhūtasaṃplavam
sādhaka uvāca |

tvanmuktaśca bhaviṣyāmi janmaduḥkhavivarjitaḥ
devyuvāca |

koṭimekantu kanyānāṃ tava dattantu sādhaka |
ayutadvayaṃ tu śeṣāṇāṃ kanyakānāntu kalpitam
devyāḥ pādāmbujaṃ vatsa sādhakaḥ puṇyakarmakṛt |
gato vai sādhakaiḥ sārdhaṃ stūyamānastu maṃgalaiḥ
varaṃ dattvā mahādevī sādhakasya maheśvarī |
praviśya bhavanaṃ divyaṃ yatsurairapi durlabham
tataḥ kalakalā śabdaiḥ kanyakānāṃ purottame |
na śrūyate pure kiñcinnānā vāditra niḥsvanaiḥ
pariṣvajanti tāḥ kanyā bhramarā iva paṃkajam |
nānākrīḍāsamāyuktā divyastrī parivāritāḥ
krīḍanti sādhakāstāvat yāvadāhūtasaṃplavam
īśvara uvāca |

kathayāmi mahādevi yathā bhuñjanti tāḥ striyaḥ |
nandāpādārcanasaktā nandāsmaraṇatatparāḥ
nandādhyānaratā dityaṃ nandābhakti samanvitāḥ |
nandāsmaraṇasantuṣṭā nandādānaikatatparāḥ
nandābhaktajane bhaktā nandāyātraikatatparāḥ |
nandāmantraratā nityaṃ bratayogaratāśca ye
patayaste bhaviṣyanti kanyakānāntu subrate |
jala prākāradurbhedyaṃ himaprākāra rakṣitam
candranāga pratīhāraṃ devyā ājñā mahallakam |
antaḥpurataraṃ divyamasureśvaradurlabham
nandābhaktajanairbhīgyaṃ nijamantaḥpuramiva |
ataḥ paraṃ pravakṣyāmi mantroddhārasya lakṣaṇam
yajanañcaiva devīnāṃ rupakañca mahātape |
pavargāt paṃcame varge vājañcaiva tadantimam
uccareta prayatnena bhinnaṃ vaihāyasena tu |
punastu madhyamaṃ bījaṃ tṛtīyaṃ svarabheditam
punaḥ prathamaṃ dātavyaṃ bhinnā vaihāyasena tu |
ekādaśena sabhinnaṃ bījaṃ kuryādvarānane
tasyāpi paramaṃ devi uddharetprathamaṃ punaḥ |
tṛtīyaṃ bhūtaje naiva adhastho na tu yājayet
punardvitīyabhūtasthaṃ bhedayekādaśena tu |
tasyāpi paratare varge prathamantu samuddharet
punaścaturthabhūyasthaṃ bījaṃ yatnena uddharet |
kālakṣāntaṃ tato bījaṃ bheda ekādaśena tu
navākṣarā mahāvidyā nandāyā hṛdayaṃ priye |
sarvakāmaphalapradā nityaṃ vidyeyantu mahātape
akṣaraṃ yugmāyugmañca aṃgāni tu prakalpayet |
navamantu bhavedasraṃ kālākhyaṃ savisargajam
anayā japyamānasya kanyakāstu mahātape |
nityaṃ kurvanti ānandaṃ nandāyāstu purottame
animeṣe kṣaṇā nityaṃ ratnaṃ paśyanti sādhakāḥ |
darśanenotsukāḥ sarvāḥ kāmārttāḥ kāminīḥ priye
ataḥ paraṃ pravakṣyāmi devyāyā yajanaṃ śubham |
sādhakānāṃ hitārthāya tanme nigadataḥ śṛṇu
anantamāsanaṃ kṛtvā dharmādīśca niveśayet |
tataḥ prakalpayet padmāsanaṃ praṇavena tu
anantādīni deveśe praṇavena prakalpayet |
tata āvāhayeddevīṃ mūlamantreṇa subrate
śuklāmbaradharāṃ saumyāṃ jaṭāmukuṭa maṇḍitām |
nānālaṃkāraśobhāḍhyāṃ sitabhasmāvaguṇṭhitām
abhayavarapradāṃ devī varahastāṃ caturbhujām |
nānāpuṣpaistathā bhakṣyai rlehyavoṣyaiśca īpsitaiḥ
pūjayet parayā bhaktyā mahābhogajigīṣayā |
aṃgāni pūjayet paścāt hṛdayaṃ vahnigocaraiḥ
āgneyāntu śiraḥ pūjya naiṛtyā pūjayet śikhām |
kavacaṃ parame bhāge aiśānye'straṃ prapūjayet
pūrvapatre jayā sthāpyā vijayāṃ dakṣiṇe nyaset |
ajitāṃ paścime patre uttare aparājitām
dvibhujāṃ bālarūpāntu raktāmbaradharāṃ sadā |
vīṇāgṛhītahastāṃ tu nānālaṃkārabhūṣitām
svābhidhānābhidheyāñca bhūtyāṃśaścaiva prapūjayet |
śuklāmbaradharā hṛṣṭā dakṣiṇe varavarṇinī
paścime pītarūpā tu uttarā vṛṣarupiṇī |
rūpayauvanasampannā divyābharaṇabhūṣitā
ājñāṃ prārthayamānastu devīnāṃ tadgatā priye |
pratibhūtvā sadā kuryāt kṛtāñjali purā sthitā
svanāmaiḥ pūjayeddevīṃ vedikādyairvyaṃvasthitām |
paścimāyāṃ jayāṃ devīṃ varadābhayapāṇinīm
nandānandakarī devī bhavate sādhakasya tu |
lokapālān svanāmaistu astrāṃścaiva prapūjayet
pratibhāvaṃ yadā mantrī mantreṇa saha kārayet |
phalaṃ na vidyate tasya prabhutvena yadā sthitaḥ
ātmānaṃ prākṛtaṃ manyet mantraṃ manyed yathā śivam |
vidhireṣa samākhyātaḥ kāryaścaiva tu sādhakaiḥ
divyaprākṛtabhāvena pūjyamānā mahādhipe |
hṛdaye bhava deveśi anyathā tu nāsiddhidaḥ
pūjākāle tu karttavyamadāne mantrarūpiṇam |
anyathā yattu deveśi vighnaiḥ sa paribhūyate
evaṃ kṛtvā mahāyāgaṃ sarvasiddhipradāyakam |
ataḥ paraṃ pravakṣyāmi mudrālakṣaṇamuttamam
aṃgulāgrasthitāḥ sarvā aṃguṣṭheva tatopari |
namaskārā smṛtā mudrā devyāḥ sānnidhyakārikā |

anayā vidhinā devi devyāḥ sānnidhyatāṃ vrajet
iti śrī devīpurāṇe nandāpraśaṃsānāma trinavatitamo'dhyāyaḥ

caturnavatitamo'dhyāyaḥ |

umovāca |

mandā devyāḥ purī deva śrutā me parameśavara |
adhunā śrotumicchāmi sunandāyāḥ purottamam
kiṃ pramāṇaṃ ca kanyānāṃ praveśañca purasya tu |
kena mārgeṇa gacchanti narā ye bhāvitātmanaḥ
kena vā tuṣyate devī kathaṃ pratyakṣatāṃ bhavet |
vidhireṣa samākhyāhi mama kautuhalaṃ prabho
īśvara uvāca |

sunandāyā purī ramyā anaupamyā sureśvari |
tathāpi kathayiṣyāmi tava kautuhalaṃ priye
nānāratnopaśobhāḍhyā nānābharaṇabhūṣitā |
nānā ratnījvalā devī nānāmekhalayojitā
ratnasopānapaṃktibhiḥ sucitrā tu virājate |
nānāśayyāsanākīrṇai rnānācāmaraśobhitaiḥ
nānāvastravitānaiśca nānāvimānasaṃkulā |
nānākavāṭa-vinyastā nānāstambhasamanvitā
nānādhvajocchritā ramyā nānāghaṇṭānināditā |
nānādarpaṇavinyastā nānāsragdāmabhūṣitā
nānāvarṇarajaiḥ kīrṇā ramyā hemavatī mahī |
na nimnā nonnatā cāpi sukhapādapracāradā
nānāsaritsamākīrṇā nānānirjharakāśritā |
nānāpakṣīgaṇājuṣṭā hemadrumalatākulā
nānāpuṣpaphalopetā sundarībhiralaṃkṛtā |
kāmakārmukasaṃghuṣṭā sāyakairvidhvastacetasaḥ
stanorasi ca bharākrāntā praskhalanti pade pade |
kāmena sahasālāpaṃ nityaṃ kurvanti yoṣitaḥ
kanyakā ūcūḥ |

pātālapurasundaryaḥ kiṃ prayuktāsrilocana |
yathā kāmaṃ dahasveti evaṃ vidhvaṃsi nirdaya
alpāni hīnasattvāni aṃganānāṃ manobhavaḥ |
mlecchāpi na praharanti muktvā tvāṃ makaradhvajam
kāntaṃ dhyātvā kṛśodaryaḥ ekamevābhigṛhnitāḥ |
bhavanti lajjitā bhūyo avasāne sureśvari
anena madanārttāstu sunandāyāḥ pure priye |
kathitā yādṛśī ārttiryoṣitānāntu sundari
ataḥ paraṃ pravakṣyāmi devyā siddhiniṣevitam |
tāvadgacchenmahātīrthaṃ yatsurairapi durlabham
gaṅgātīre mahādevī paśyate marukeśvaram |
tatra gatvā tu medhāvī trirātraṃ kārayed budhaḥ
trirātre caiva sampūrṇe praṇipatya maheśvaram |
uttarābhimukho bhūtvā vrajedīśānagocaram
ūrdhvayānaṃ tataḥ paśyennadīvāme śiloccayāḥ |
pitṛṇāmudakaṃ dattvā kālakūṭaṃ vrajettataḥ
kalahaṃseśvaraṃ nāma śambhorāyatanaṃ mahat |
tatrādipūjāṃ kṛtvā tu praṇipatya punaḥ punaḥ
kauśikāyāṃ puraḥ snātvā mucyate naraḥ kilbiṣaḥ |
śūlabhedaṃ tato gacchet tatsurairapi durlabham
tatrāpi pūjāṃ kṛtvā tu ekacittastu sādhakaḥ |
tadvasanbhavanaṃ gacchet kedāraṃ yatra krīḍitam
lokadṛṣṭena mārgeṇa sa gacchet kārtikaṃ puram |
guhyeśvaraṃ namaskṛtvā gacchedvaiśravaṇaṃ puram
brajennaṃdeśvaraṃ devamahorātrantu kārayet |
bhāgaṃ catuṣṭayaṃ kṛtvā devāgni-guru-ātmani
bhakṣayitvā tataḥ prājño gacchet taduttarāṃ diśam |
tato vaitaraṇīṃ gatvā snātvā tu vidhivat kramāt
devānāmudakaṃ dattvā piṇḍaṃ pitṛṣu dāpayet |
mahāvināyakaṃ dattvā pūjāṃ tasya prakalpayet
devyāśramantu saṃprāpya namaskṛtya maheśvaram |
pūrvabhāge tu kuṇḍasya aiśānī diśamāśritaḥ
sunandāyā śilā tatra jalamadhye pratiṣṭhitā |
puṣpargandhaistathā dhūpaiḥ pūjayet parameśvarīm
nandā kuṇḍaṃ hradaṃ tatra praviśettatra sādhakaḥ |
nandādevīṃ namaskṛtya tato vijñāpayed vudhaḥ
anivarttapathaṃ devī dehī me parameśvari |
tataḥ samīpato gacched śivena pūrvacoditam
kṛtāñjalipuṭoḥ bhūtvā praviśeta vicakṣaṇaḥ |
dhanvantarapramāṇaṃ tu praviśenmatsyavatdrutam
praviśyābhyantare vīra aiśānīdiśamāśritaḥ |
dhanvantaratrayaṃ gatvā śrīmukhaṃ tatra paśyati
praviśet tajjatāntasthaṃ śrīmukhaṃ dvāramuttamam |
dhanvantaraśataṃ gatvā paśyedāmalakaṃ drumam
tatphalaṃ bhakṣayet prājño namaskṛtvā maheśvarīm |
tatphalaṃ bhakṣamātreṇa valipalita varjjitaḥ
balaṃ nāgasahasrasya tatkṣaṇādeva jāyate |
dhanvantaraśataṃ gatvā praviśeta tato'dhikam
dṛśyate maṇḍapaṃ ramyaṃ śuddhaṃ hemamayaṃ mahat |
śuddhasphāṭikastambhāḍhyaṃ caturdvāraṃ mahāpuram
padmarāgoparicchannaṃ patākairupaśobhitam |
svayaṃ tiṣṭhati tatraiva mahākālagaṇādhipaḥ
sādhakañcāgataṃ dṛṣṭvā svāgatantu vadatyasau |
athā nandī vadedvākyamupaveśāya sādhakam
pṛcchāmi ambikāṃ yāvat tāvat tiṣṭha mahātapaḥ |
tataḥ śīghraṃ gato nandī sunandāyāḥ samīpataḥ
nandī uvāca |

āgato marttyo loke'smin tava pārśve maheśvari
sunandā uvāca |

āgacchantu mahānandī mama bhaktiparāyaṇaḥ |
devyāyāḥ vacanaṃ śrutvā tato nandī samāsataḥ
sādhakasyedaṃ vākyaṃ vadennandī subhāvitam |
dhanyo'si bho mahāvīra ehi gacchāma sādhaka
ardhyaṃ pādyaṃ tato gṛhya kanyā nirgatya veśmani |
keyūrābharaṇairdivyai rmaṇikuṇḍalabhūṣitā
campakākāravapuṣaḥ karṇānttāyatalocanāḥ |
nīlotpaladalaśyāmā nānālaṃkārabhūṣitāḥ
raktāmbaradharā kācicchuklāmvaradharāparāḥ |
pītāmvarādharā cānyā pūrṇacandranibhānanāḥ
sarvā yauvanasampannāḥ sarvāḥ pīnapayodharāḥ |
sarvāṃstāḥ kāmarūpiṇyaḥ sarvāṃstāmṛtasambhavāḥ
yāścānyāścāparāstatra nirgatāśca samantataḥ |
geyaiśca madhurairdivyai rmaṇḍalaiśca manoramaiḥ
cāmaraiḥ kanakadaṇḍaiśca maṇiratnamayaidṛḍhaiḥ |
cāmarahastātathā kācit puṣpahastāstathāparā
madārttā muditāḥ sarvāḥ īkṣanteha nimiṣekṣaṇāḥ |
pūjyante sādhakāstatra ardhyaṃpādyaiśca maṃgalaiḥ
īṣṭā tuṣṭamanāḥ sarvā avagūhana-tatparāḥ |
tatastu sādhakaṃ gṛhya praveśayanti tatpuram
vijñāpayet tato bhaktyā tvaṃ gatiḥ śaraṇaṃ mama |
tato devī vadedvākyaṃ prasanna vadanojjavalā
svāgataṃ te mahāvīra sādhakastvaṃ kṛto mayā |
evaṃ sambhāṣitā devyā sādhakāstu mahātmanaḥ
tatkṣaṇādeva jāyante sādhakā divyarupiṇaḥ |
iyaṃ divyapurī vatsa candravatyā samanvitā
krīḍasva matprasādena yāvaccandradivākarau |
tadante bhavate mokṣo matprasādena putraka
devānāntu yathā rudraṃ atiraskṛtaśāsanaḥ |
tathaiva bhavane mahyaṃ krīḍaya tvaṃ yathāsukham
evaṃ dattvā varaṃ devī sādhakasya sureśvari |
namaskṛtvā tato mantrī praviveśa surottamam
maṃgalaiḥ stūyamānastu gītavādyamanoramaiḥ |
cāmarairbījyamānastu skandatulya-parākramaḥ
puṣpayānaṃ samāruhya krīḍate bhavanottame |
yojanānāṃ sahasrantu bhavanasya ca vistaraḥ
sahasrakoṭikanyānāṃ samantāt pūritaṃ puram
iti śrī devīpurāṇe sunandāpraveśavidhirnāma caturnavatitamo'dhyāyaḥ |

paṃcanavatitamo'dhyāyaḥ |

umovāca |

sunandāyāḥ puraṃ ramyaṃ śrutaṃ me parameśvara |
adhunā śrotumicchāmi kanyakāyāḥ kathaya prabho
īśvara uvāca |

kanyakāyāḥ pathaṃ devi kathayāmi samāsataḥ |
śāka-yāvaka-payo-vāyu-ladhvāhāro athāpi vā
homayellakṣamekantu padma-vilva-samanvitam |
tato gacchenmahāvīraḥ pūrvoktena pathena tu
adhunā mantrapadāni bhavanti |
om nanda ninanda kili kili svāhā
imāṃ vidyāṃ japaṃ kuryāt tataḥ siddhiḥ prajāyate |
pūrvoktena vidhānena nityaṃ prakalpayet
tatastu kārayeddhaumaṃ guḍikairguggulasya tu |
ayutamekaṃ mahādevi tataḥ siddhiḥ prajāyate
pūrvameva eṣo lakṣān japtvā homaṃ prakalpayet |
homānte darśanaṃ rātrau siddhistasya prajāyate
tato gacchet medhāvī sādhakaiḥ sahitaḥ pathi |
devyāśramapadaṃ prāpya caruṃ tatra prasādhayet
bhāgaṃ catuṣṭayaṃ kṛtvā devi agniśivātmani |
ātmabhāgaṃ tato mantrī sādhakaiḥ saha bhakṣayet
vijñāpayet tato devīṃ praṇipatya punaḥ punaḥ |
ahaṃ duḥkhāntare bhītastāmeva śaraṇaṃ gataḥ
dehi me tvaṃ pathaṃ devi avighnena maheśvari |
evaṃ vijñāpya deveśīṃ sa gaccheduttarāṃ diśam
śarakṣepatrayaṃ gatvā dṛśyate śailamuttamam |
śuddhasphaṭikasaṅkāśā pratimā tatra tiṣṭhati
namaskṛtvā tu gantavyamaiśānyāṃ diśi saṃsthitam |
dhanvantaraśataṃ gatvā ardhacandrākṛtiḥ śilā
tatra mātṛ gṛhasthaiva uttarā diśi tiṣṭhati |
namaskṛtvā tu gantavyaṃ yāvad dṛśyaṃ nabhaḥ sthalam
karavīravanaṃ tatra hemapuṣpaṃ sugandhi ca |
ṣaṭpadāravaramyāḍhyā divyabhūmyā vyavasthitā
pratimārūpadharā sā divyahemamayā śubhā |
nānāratnojjvalā ramyā sādhakānāṃ phalapradā
tasyāḥ pūrvottare bhāge vanaṃ gīrvāṇapādapam |
aśokabakulaiścaiva śubhaistilakacampakaiḥ
priyaṃgunāgapunnāgaiḥ nānāpādapasaṅakulaiḥ |
nānā gulmasamākīrṇaṃ nānāvallī samākulam
sadā puṣpaphalopetaṃ sadā ṣaṭpadanāditam |
kokilārāvaramyantu nānāpakṣiniṣevitam
asya madhye mahādevī devyā bhavanamuttamam |
nānāratnaiśca vinyastaṃ nānādhvaja samākulam
nānā līlāvatī ramyā nupūrārāvanisvanā |
dīrghikābhiḥ suramyābhiḥ śobhitābhiḥ saroruhaiḥ
tatra mānavakanyāstu devyāḥ pādaprapūjakāḥ |
yakṣiṇyaḥ kāmarūpāstu gandharvī kinnarī tathā
vidyādharya surūpāstu devīmārādhayanti tām |
kāmārttā vihvalā nityaṃ bharttāṃraṃ prārthayanti tāḥ
aneka siddhisaṃkīrṇaṃ devyāyāḥ sthānamuttamam |
devyā vimānamāruhya āgatā kanakeśvarī
jaṭāmukuṭa ratnāḍhyā bhasmīddhūlita vigrahā |
pañcamudrāsamopetā nānāratnavibhūṣitā |

mahāvratadharā devī āgatā yatra sādhakāḥ
devyuvāca |

svāgataṃ te mahārāja vīrasattva mahātapaḥ |
madīyaṃ bhavanaṃ vatsa nānāsiddhi samākulam
vicitramaṇinā kīrṇa devānāmapi durlabham |
yadi tiṣṭhasi atraiva divyaiśvarya samākule
pātālayoṣito gṛhya yakṣiṇīṃ vātha rūpiṇīm |
kinnarīṃ vātha gṛhya vidyādharīmathāpi vā
khaḍgaṃ vā rocanāṃ vāpi guḍikāṃ vāpi pāduke |
aṣṭadhā divyasiddhināmekāṃ gṛhya yathepsayā
bhuktvā tu vipulān bhogān paścānmokṣo bhaviṣyati |
evaṃ dattvā varaṃ devyā sādhakasya tu sundari
gatā vimānamārūhya svaka yaṃ sthānamuttamam |
candrakāntamayīṃ nandāṃ pratimārūpadhāriṇīm
pūjayanti kṛśodarya kāntārthinyo gṛhe gṛhe |
muktāphalamayīṃ devīṃ sunandāyāḥ pure priye
gandhadhūpaiḥ supuṣpādyai strikālaṃ pūjayanti tāḥ |
sphāṭikāṃ śubhrarūpāntu kanakāḍhyāñca kāminīḥ
arccayanti sadākālaṃ mathitā manmathena tu |
svakīyairbhuvanairdivyaiḥ pūjāṃ kurvanti tā striyaḥ
pralaye tu samutpanne devyāḥ puravaraiḥ saha |
vidyate dve mahādevi tadā līyanti devatāḥ
ataḥ paraṃ pravakṣyāmi sakhāyānāntu lakṣaṇam |
dharmaśīlāstapoyuktāḥ satyavādi-jitendriyāḥ
mātsaryena parityaktāḥ sarvasattvahite ratāḥ |
priyavādinaḥ sotsāhā marttyaloka jugupsakāḥ
paraspara susantuṣṭā anukūlā sādhakasya tu |
īdṛśaiḥ sādhanaṃ kuryāt susaravāyaiḥ sahaiva tu
brahmovāca |

yā nandā sā śivaḥ sākṣānnandārūpadharaḥ śivaḥ |
ubhayorantaraṃ nāsti nandāyāstu śivasya ca
na nandāparamaṃ dhyānaṃ na nandāparamaṃ tapaḥ |
na nandāparamaṃ tīrthaṃ śivaḥ sākṣāt prabhāṣate
lekhye'pi tiṣṭhate yasya idaṃ dhyānaṃ mahātapaḥ |
tasyāpi prīyate devī kiṃ punarmantra pūjitā
īśvara uvāca |

nāstikāya na dātavyaṃ na śambhu-guru-nindake |
piśunāya na dātavyaṃ devyā bhaktivivarjite
guru-dvija-deva-viṣṇu-kanyā-go-nindakena ca |
dātavyantu mahādevi devyā bhaktiratasya ca
anyathā tu varārohe hīyate śāstrasantatiḥ |
snehāllobhāt pradānena narakaṃ yānti rauravam
trimantrāṃ paṭhate yastu nandābhaktiparāyaṇaḥ |
so'cireṇaiva kālena siddhimiṣṭāṃ labhennaraḥ
yathoktaścaiva karttavyamādeśaḥ parameśvari |
śravaṇādbhāvayuktasya sarvakāmān prayacchati
daśānāṃ rājasūyānāmagniṣṭomaśatasya ca |
bhāvitaḥ phalamāpnoti koṭikoṭi guṇottaram
putrārthīṃ labhate putraṃ dhanārthī dhanabhāgbhavet |
mucyate bandhanādvaddho rogī rogāt pramucyate
yān yān kāmān naro bhaktyā pūjayannabhikāṃkṣate |
tāṃstān sa labhate śakra ityevaṃ śiva abravīt
devena kathitaṃ devyā śakrasya tu pitāmahāt |
mayā tava nṛpavyāghra kiṃ bhūyaḥ paripṛcchasi
iti śrī devīpurāṇe nandāmahābhāgyaṃ nāma pañcanavatitamo'dhyāyaḥ |

ṣaṇṇavatitamo'dhyāyaḥ |

nṛpavāhana uvāca |

kena kena prakāreṇa devyā varṇāśramairvibho |
pūjanīyā svavṛttasthairetadicchāmi veditum
agastya uvāca |

sādhu rājan yathā pṛṣṭaṃ varṇāśramavibhāgataḥ |
pālanaṃ pūjanaṃ devyā pravakṣyāmi hyaśeṣataḥ
veda eva dvijātīnāṃ niḥśreyasakaraḥ paraḥ |
dṛṣṭādṛṣṭārthamicchadbhiḥ sevanīyaḥ sadā dvijaiḥ
mātṛtaḥ pitṛtaḥ śuddhaḥ pañcasapta tathā dvijaḥ |
saṃskārairgarbhadhārī ca tadā tasya kriyā tataḥ
yathā hi madyabhāṇḍasya śuddhiḥ kenāpi na vidyate |
pañcagavyaṃ na tadyāti evaṃ prāyaṃ śruteḥ kriyā
jātisaṃskārahīnasya dravyasaṃkarakāriṇaḥ |
śūdrānnabhojino rājan na vedo dadate phalam
śūdrasya annamaśitvā vedaṃ yadi udīrate |
ucchiṣṭa bhojī varṇānāṃ narake paryupāsate
cāṇḍāla caṇḍakarme ca vṛṣalīpatisannidhau |
yadi udīrate vedaṃ tadā vipro'pi tatsamaḥ
vedamantrān yadā vipraḥ śūdradravyeṇa tarpate |
sarpiṣā yavagodhūma tilapiṣṭaka śālibhiḥ
yāvatī tasya dravyasya rajoreṇu vidhīyate |
tāvatīśca mahāghore narake paryupāsate
na hi vedaṃ samāsādya vidhiṃ jahyāt dvijottama |
tasya eva hi ājñā na laṃghanīyā kadācana
cakravṛttidharā viprā uñchakāpota vṛttinaḥ |
dantolūkhālikāhārā vedānāṃ labhate phalam
nadīsaṃgamagoṣṭheṣu vicitraṣu taṭeṣu ca |
vicitrabhūmideśeṣu darbhadūrvāvṛteṣu ca
gṛheṣu śubhalipteṣu viṣṇu-sūrya-gṛheṣu ca |
paṭhitavyaḥ sadā vedaḥ svaravarṇa sulakṣitaḥ
plutadīrghakramahrasva sānusvāra sulakṣitām |
ṛcamuccārayet prājño na drutāṃ na vilambitām
śuklamālyadharo nityaṃ sugandhaḥ sukhavāsasaḥ |
netrāñjanaṃ niṣeveta dantadhāvanapūrvakam
ṛjupathe sadācāro ṛjusevī jitendriyaḥ |
paṭhanājapanāsakto likhanā śravaṇā tathā
nityaṃ daivatapūjāyāmauṣadhādhāraneṣu ca |
japahomārccane sakto vindate sukhamuttamam
na gacchenmaithunaṃ parve na devagurusannidhau |
na kuryājjale nādantu na vedyairna ca vatsaraiḥ
na pradhānajanavādaṃ nṛpākṣepaṃ kadācana |
nṛpa-bandhu-gurvamātya-bhiṣag-jyoti-purohitaiḥ
virodhānīha duḥkhāni sukhaṃ prītyā avāpnuyāt
iti śrī devīpurāṇe ācārakīrttanaṃ nāma saptanavatitamo'dhyāyaḥ |

saptanavatitamo'dhyāyaḥ |

śakra uvāca |

gomedho aśvamedhaśca paśumedhādayo makhāḥ |
teṣu prāṇivadhastāta te ca svargādisādhanāḥ |

evaṃ pūrvāṃparārtheṣu virodhaḥ sumahān bhavet |
chindhi me saṃśayaṃ nātha sarvaśāstrārthapāraga
brahmovāca |

yajñārthaṃ paśavaḥ sṛṣṭā yajñeṣveṣāṃ vadhaḥ smṛtaḥ |
anyatra ghātanāddoṣo vāṅ-manaḥ-kāya-karmabhiḥ
devārthe pitṛkāryeṣu manuṣyārthe purandara |
vadhayan na bhavedena anyathā mahākilviṣam
navakṛṣarapūpāni pāyasaṃ madhusarpiṣī |
vṛthā māṃsañca nāśnīyāddeva-pitṛ-aho-mitam
na vṛthā ceṣṭayet kiñcit trivargasya virodhayā |
na ca vācaṃ vaded duṣṭāṃ na dīnāṃ na ca karkaśām
nāsahāyo brajedrātrau na paṃke na catuṣpathe |
na śūnyāgāre tiṣṭheta na ca parvatamastake
na śmaśāne na devasya prāsādeṣu kadācana |
na ca gavi prasūtāyāṃ viśvaseta satrījaneṣu ca
na vṛkṣārohaṇaṃ kuryāt na ca kūpāvalokanam |
na godvijahutāśānnaṃ madhyena gamanaṃ kvacit
na vahṇau tāpayeta pādaṃ na ca tamamabhilaṃghayet |
na sūryamavaloketa udayāstamane kvacit
na mukhena dhamedagniṃ na ca khaḍgaṃ tu laṃghayet |
tathā caivāyudhān sarvān yatropaskara mārjanīḥ
na pramattajanākīrṇe na ca strīvālasevite |
gṛhe vāmagamaṃ kuryānna ca viśvāsa krīḍanam
na viṣaṃ bhakṣayet prājño na bhujaṃgaiśca krīḍayet |
na gurudvijavedāṃśca nindayenna ca ākṣipet
sarvaṃ bhadraṃ brūyāt sarvakālaṃ śubhānanaḥ |
śuklavāsā śuciḥ sragvī na ca keśanakhaḥ sukhī
śuklamālyadharo nityaṃ sugandhaḥ sukhavāsasaḥ |
netrāñjanaṃ niṣeveta dantadhāvanapūrvakam
ṛjupathe sadācāro ṛjusevī jitendriyaḥ |
paṭhanājapanāsakto likhanā śravaṇā tathā
nityaṃ daivatapūjāyāmauṣadhādhāraneṣu ca |
japahomārccane sakto vindate sukhamuttamam
na gacchenmaithunaṃ parve na devagurusannidhau |
na kuryājjale nādantu na vedyairna ca vatsaraiḥ
na pradhānajanavādaṃ nṛpākṣepaṃ kadācana |
nṛpa-bandhu-garvamātya-bhiṣag-jyoti-purohitaiḥ
virodhānīha duḥkhāni sukhaṃ prītyā avāpnuyāt
iti śrī devīpurāṇe ācārakīrttanaṃ nāma saptanavatitamo'dhyāyaḥ |

aṣṭanavatitamo'dhyāyaḥ |

brahmovāca |

evamācārayuktātmā satataṃ carccikārataḥ |
āpnuyāt sarvakāmāṃstu yathepsitamano'nugān
śakra uvāca |

nityaṃ ye bhagavatībhaktāstairnarairdvijasattama |
kiṃ kāryaṃ kiṃ vā no kāryaṃ tadvada pṛcchato mama
brahmovāca |

sarvā sarvagatā devī sarvadeva namaskṛtā |
yaṣṭavyā śuddhabhāvena na bhinnā pṛthageva sā
nāmabhedād bhavedbhinnā na bhinnā paramārthataḥ |
śivā nārāyaṇī gaurī carccikā vimalā umā
tārā śvetā mahāśvetā amvikā śivaśāsanāt |
yāvad dravyaṃ bhavedahaṃ tāvaddevī vyavasthitā
sā vandyā pūjanīyā ca satataṃ nandabhāvitaiḥ vijayārthaṃ nṛpaiḥ khaṅge chūrikāpādukāpaṭe
cāmuṇḍā citrarūpā vā likhitā vātha pustake |
dhvaje vā kārayecchakra sa nṛpo vijayed dviṣam
viśeṣācchrābaṇārabhya tasyāḥ pūjāntu kārayet |
pavitrārohaṇaṃ vatsa sarvaśāstreṣu gīyate
agnerbrahmasya pārvatyā gajavaktramahoragām |
skanda-bhānu-gaṇā-mātṛ-durgā-dharmeśa-go-vṛṣām
viṣṇoḥ kāmasya devasya śakrasya ca dināṃśagām |
pūjanīyā tu cāmuṇḍā caṇḍapāpavināśinī
sarvakāryādinā dattā ebhirnāmaiḥ purandara |
athavāṣāḍhamāse tu śrāvaṇe vāpi kārayet
saptamyāṃ vā trayodaśyāmadhivāsaṃ surādhipa |
sarvopahārasampannaṃ nandāyāḥ bhaktimāśritaḥ
śuklatastumayaṃ kārya pavitraṃ bahutantubhiḥ |
granthibhiḥ suvicitrābhi racitañcaiva mauktikaiḥ
sudhautaṃ bakṣayet tantuṃ rocanā śaśikuṃkumaiḥ |
tathā sarvāṇi dravyāṇi puṣpagandhaphalāni ca
naivedyāni vicitrāṇi vastrānādyābharaṇāni ca |
hematāramayān puṣpān kuśāni mṛdavastathā
susnāto mantravidhinā agnikāryaṃ tathā kuru |
tathā ca pūjayeddevīṃ pratimāṃ sthaṇḍile'pi vā
pāduke vātha khaḍge ca chūrikādhanuṣostathā |
mantradhāvananapūrvantu pañcagavyaṃ carūṃ kurū
dattvā diśāṃ baliṃ vatsa tathā kuryādhivāsanam |
sadaśairvastrapatrairvā sthāpayet tat pavitrakam
kṛtvā satrābhimantrādyaṃ naivedyaṃ ca nivedayet |
rātrau tu jāgaraṃ kuryāt sarvaśobhāsamanvitam
naṭanartakaveśyānāṃ saṃghāni muditāni ca |
tiṣṭhantu vādyagītābhiniratāni purandara
prabhātasamaye vatsa prāpte dadyāt punarvalim |
pratyūṣe vidhivat snātvā tathā devī hutāśanam
japtvā hutvātha kanyāśca striyo bhojyā dvijāstathā |
pavitrārohena vṛtte dakṣiṇāmupapādayet
yathā śaktā bhavecchakra nityaṃ kāryakāriṇā |
rājñā nānāvidhā bhakti akṣakrīḍā mṛgāvadham
dvijācāryaiśca svādhyāyaṃ na kāryaṃ kṛṣigovṛṣaiḥ |
bālai srībhiśca ca ātmīyaṃ dināni daśa paṃcavā
devyā vyāpāranāmābhiḥ karttavyaṃ satataṃ hare |
tathā sampūrṇa karttavyaṃ punaḥ kuryāt pavitrakam
evaṃ yaḥ kārayedvatsa tasya puṇyaphalaṃ śṛṇu |
sarva-yajña-vrata-dāna sarvatīthābhiṣecanam
prāpnuyānnātra sandeho yasmāt sarvagatā śivā |
nādhayo na ca duḥkhāni na pīḍā na ca vyādhayaḥ
na bhayaṃ śatrujaṃ tasya na grahaiḥ pīḍyate kvacit |
sidhyante sarvakāryāṇi api yāni mahāntyapi
nātaḥ parataraṃ vatsa manye puṇyavivṛddhaye |
narāṇāñca nṛpāṇāñca srīṇāñcāpi viśeṣataḥ
saubhāgyajananaṃ vatsa tava snehātprakāśitam |
mayāpi te nṛpaśreṣṭha yathāvadupapāditam
śravaṇādapi puṇyāya kiṃ punaḥ kāraṇādvibho
iti śrīdevīpurāṇe pavitrārohaṇaṃ nāmāṣṭanavatitamo'dhyāyaḥ |

navanavatitamo'dhyāyaḥ |

brahmovāca |

ataḥ paraṃ pravakṣyāmi sarvābhyudayavardhanam |
yatkṛtvā bhavate rājan sarvavarṇo'pi cānagha
nabhomāse tu samprāpte naktāhāro jitendriyaḥ |
prātaḥ snāyī sadādhyāyī agnikārya parāyaṇaḥ
devīṃ saṃpūjayedvatsa punnāgavilvacampakaiḥ |
dhūpantu guggulaṃ dadyānnaivedyaṃ ghṛtapācitam
kṣīrānnaṃ dadhibhaktañca athavā śākayāvakam |
japaṃ kuryāttu mantrasya sahasraṃ śatameva vā
devvāyāstraṃ samarpyeta yāvat pūrṇavrato bhavet |
pūrṇe vrate tato vatsa kanyācāryadvijān striyaḥ
bhojayet pūjayedbhaktyā hemabhūvastragovṛṣaiḥ |
abhāvāt maṃtrajāpantu nityaṃ kārya nṛpottama
yaḥ kuryāt satataṃ bhaktyā so'pi tatphalamāpnuyāt |
na ca vyādhirjarā mṛtyurna bhayaṃ cora -sambhavam
bhavate nandābhaktasya ante ca padamavyayam
atha mantrapadāni bhavanti |
oṃ nande nandinī sarvārthasādhanī |

(mūlavidyā)
oṃ nuṃ nande hṛdayam |
oṃ tuṃ nandinī śiraḥ |
oṃ sarvāni śikhā |
oṃ arthasādhinī kavacam |

oṃ nuṃ netram |
oṃ namaḥ humÌphaṭ astram |
oṃ nandinī upacārahṛdayam
tṛtīyāmatha pañcamyāṃ caturthyāmaṣṭamīṣu ca |
navamyaṃ, paurṇamāsyāñca ekādaśyāñca dvādaśīm
ṣaṣṭhyāṃ caiva vidyeṣā pūjanīyā viśeṣataḥ |
nandāmuddiśya yo dadyācchrāvaṇe govṛṣaṃ sitam
sa labhediṣṭakāmāni ante lokañca śāśvatam |
navamyāṃ yaḥ samuddiśya dadyātgāṃ kācanaṃ pi vā
sa vrajed dhūtapātastu nandālokaṃ tanukṣaye |
āśvine navarātrāṇi upavāsa ayācitaiḥ
kṛtvā devīṃ prapūjyeta aṣṭamyāmapare'hani |
hema-vastra-maṇi-puṣpa-nānācitra-vibhūṣaṇaiḥ
dānaṃ ca kācanaṃ deyaṃ nandāśāstrārthapārage |
sa dhūtapāpasaṃghātaḥ sarvakāmasamanvitaḥ
vimāne cāmarotkṣipte cārū cākṣaraśobhite |
gacchate nandalokantu yatra devī purārihā
ramate kanyā koṭibhirapsarogaṇasevitaḥ |
tadante āgataścātra pṛthivyāmekarāḍ bhavet
nandābhaktaḥ śive bhakte nandāyātraika tatparaḥ |
kārtike pūjayitvā tu devīṃ yāti gajāhvayaiḥ
annadānaṃ daded vipra kanyāyāṃ strījaneṣu ca |
śvetāni caiva vastrāṇi tathā deyāni dakṣiṇā
mucyate sarvapāpaistu janmāntarakṛtairapi |
ihatraiva bhavedyogī paratra padamavyayam
mārgasya vidhivatsnātvā devīṃ pūjaya kuṃkumaiḥ |
naivedyaṃ pūṣpapūrṇāśca deyā kanyāśca brāhmaṇe
bhojayed dakṣayed vatsa vastraiḥ kīṭakulodbhavaiḥ |
prāpnuyāt sarvakāmāni sarvapāpaiḥ pramucyate
pauṣe devīṃ samādhāya pūjayejjavajaiḥ srajaiḥ |
naivedyaṃ śālibhaktañca kanyā bhojayet bhakṣayet
pītairvastraistathā deyā śayyā devyā tulodbhavā |
anena vidhinā vatsa sākṣāddevī prasīdati
dadate kāmikān bhogān ante ca svapuraṃ nayet |
māghe tu pūjayeddevīṃ kundajairvidhiṃvat srajaiḥ
kuṃkumena sadarpeṇa tathā samupalepayet |
snāpitāṃ vidhivatpūrvaṃ tataḥ kanyāstu bhojayet
dvijāṃśca nandinī bhaktān vidhinā ghṛtapāyasaiḥ |
dakṣiṇāṃ tilahomaiśca yathāśaktyā pradāpayet
vidhūta-pāpa-kalilaḥ sarvabhoga-dhanānvitaḥ |
viśatrurbahuputraśca bhavate narasattamaḥ
dehānte nandinīlokaṃ sarvadevanamaskṛtam |
vrajate nātra sandeho anena vidhinā nṛpa
phālgunyāṃ pūjayeddevīṃ sahakārasrajaiḥ śubhaiḥ |
tathā naivedyabhakṣyāṇi śarkarāmadhunā saha
bhojayet kanyakā biprān dakṣiṇā sitavāsasī |
anena vidhinā bhogī devīlokaṃ ca gacchati
saṃprāpte caitramāse tu devīmijyād damanakaiḥ |
naivedyaṃ laḍḍukā deyāstathā kanyāśca bhojayet
striyaśca raktavastraiśca dakṣitavyā yathāvidhiḥ |
anena sarvavidhinā prāpnuyādavicāraṇāt
devīlokaṃ vrajedvatsa yatra bhogā nirantarāḥ |
vaiśākhe pūjayeddevīṃ karṇikārasrajaiḥ śubhaiḥ
naivedyaṃ saktavaḥ khaṃḍaṃ kanyāścaiva bhojayet |
śubhāni hemavastrāṇi deyāni dvijasattamaiḥ
devī suprītaye vatsa sarvadevamanuttamaiḥ |
kṛtavāmÌstu vidhireṣa tathā gandharva-kinnaraiḥ
jyeṣṭhe tu śaṃkarī pūjyā raktāśokakṛraṃṭakaiḥ |
tathā deyañca naivedyaṃ ghṛtapūrṇa ca kanyakāḥ
bhojanīyāstathā dakṣed gobhūdāna hiraṇyataḥ |
tathā deyāḥ jalakumbhāḥ sampūrṇā vāsitāḥ śubhāḥ
anena vāruṇān bhogān devī kṣipraṃ prayacchati |
āṣāḍhe pūjayeddevīṃ padmanīlotpalairdalaiḥ
naivedyaṃ śarkarābhaktaṃ sadadhi bhaktapāyasam |
kanyā dvijāḥ striyo bhojyāddakṣayecca tathā ca tān
nānā-hemāmvara-rāga-tila-bhū-aśva-mauktikaiḥ |
pūjyā bhagavatī bhaktyā sarvavarṇa-prasiddhaye
nandā sunandā kanakā umā durgā kṣamāvatī |
gaurī sarveśvarī śvetā nārāyaṇī sutārakā
ambikā ceti nāmāni śrāvaṇāderanukramāt |
ye ca kīrtyanti utthāya te narā dhūtakilviṣāḥ
bhavanti nṛpaśārdūṃlāḥ pṛthivyāṃ dhanasaṅkulāḥ |
etāni pathi-saṃgrāma-vṛddhipīḍāsu nityaśaḥ
smarrastarati ghorāṇi carciketi yaduttamam |
vratānāṃ pravaraṃ vatsa samāsārdha tu pādataḥ
māsaṃ vāpi prakarttavyaṃ śrāvaṇādi krameṇa tu |
nāpuṇyaiḥ prāpyate vatsa narairnṛpavaraistathā
prāpyate bhagavatībhāvaṃ yasya tuṣṭā tu nandinī
iti śrī devīpurāṇe nandāvrataṃ nāma navanavatitamo'dhyāyaḥ |

śatatamo'dhyāyaḥ |

agastya uvāca |

sarveṣāñcaiva pātrāṇāṃ devī pātrantu śaṃkarī |
tāntu pūjaya vidyaiṣā dṛṣṭā-dṛṣṭa-pradāyikā
brahmaśāstra vidhiḥ śakra kathitā vijayāvahā |
śakreti paurṇimā tāta śrāvaṇasya śubhā vahā
śakra uvāca |

vijayā yā samākhyātāsarvakāma prasiddhaye |
tāmahaṃ śrotumicchāmi tattvataḥ surasattamaḥ
brahmovāca |

putrārthaṃ rājyavidyārthaṃ yaśaḥ saubhāgyato'pi vā |
vijayārogyakāmāya vijayāṃ kurvīta paurṇimām
hemaṃ vā rājataṃ vāpi bhaikṣyaṃ khaḍgaṃ ca pāduke |
pratimāṃ vāpi kurvīta sarvalakṣaṇasaṃyutām
tāmādāya śubhe ṛkṣe śuklavastravibhūṣitām |
yavaśālyaṃkuropetāmātapatravibhūṣitām
devīṃ suśobhanāṃ vastraiḥ kalpayet tatra tāṃ nyaset |
hutvā hutāśanaṃ mantraistato devīṃ tu vinyaset
rocanā-candana-candrai rūpalipya prapūjayet |
nānāpuṣpaviśeṣaistu dhūpagandhānubhojanaiḥ
pūjayedvidhivaddevīṃ tathā bījāni āharet |
yavagodhūma mudgādi śāliyaṣṭika āḍhakī
tilamāṣāḥ pramāthī ca śyāmākā navavālakāḥ |
bilvāmradāḍimo coddhūmo ca kāpitthanāgarān
vadarān bījapūrāṃśca udumvara ākheṭakān |
dāpayeccaiva bhaktyā vai naivedyānyaparāni ca
phalārthantu phalā devyā jayārthaṃ yava aṃkurān |
puṣpaṃ saubhāgyakāmāya ratnānyāyurdhanāya ca
dhanuḥ śatruvināśāya priyamicchāya tat bhavān |
annaṃ sarvārthakāmāya yathālābhantu dāpayet
tataḥ kṣamāpayeddevī vidyāṃ gṛhyeva prārthitām |
putrārtha bhojayedvālān vijayāya striyo dvijān
dharmārtha ceva bhojyeta anayā vidyābhimantritām |
dakṣiṇāṃ ca gurvācārye kanyakā brāhmaṇeṣu ca
dāpayet yathāśaktyā tu tathā tamanugṛhya ca |
bhojyāgraṃ putrakāmena grāmaṃ vidyābhimantritam
bhoktavyaṃ pṛthakpātreṇa na ca kurvīta śaṃkaram |
anayā vidhipūrvaṃ tu mantramatraiva vidyate
tadyaḥ pṛthivyāṃ retastāmeha dadatu yo māṃ bhakṣitāni |
vidyā prayacchannaṣṭau putrān janayate vedavedāṃgapāragān
yo'dhītya na prayacchet so'putro'puṃsako bhavati |
ahaṃ vīryenāhaṃ valena dhanena |
oṃ namo bhagavate akṣīṇaretase svāhā
ratikāle hi cintayed daivataṃ tridaśeśvaram |
yasya retena loko'yaṃ bhūṣitaḥ pāvano bhuvi
oṃ retāya mahāretāya sarvavīrya mahābale |
kāmāya kāmadevāya mama kāmān prayacchatu-ṭhaṃṭhaṃ
anayābhi mantritaṃ śayanaṃ bhajet |

prayacchatyaṣṭau putrān yadi mohaṃ na gacchati |
evaṃ vidyāṃ gṛhītvātu devīṃ nityaṃ prapūjayet
bhavate sarvakāmānāṃ siddhimiṣṭāṃ parājitām |
yānīha phalapuṣpāṇi utpadyante tu prāvṛṣi
devyā viprāya kanyāyāṃ gurave api dāpayet |
yathālābhaṃ śrutaṃ vatsa deyaṃ puṣpaṃ phalāni ca
śrāvaṇī navamī yā sā āśvinī kārtikī pi vā |
sthātavyamanena vidhinā avaśyaṃ siddhimicchatā
homena vratacaryeṇa carumantra-prasādanāt |
aputro labhate putraṃ dhanaṃ saubhāgya jīvitam
athavā anayā vidyā lakṣaṇā bṛhatī sitā |
rājapūrakavidyāni vaṭa śṛṅgādivādarāt
nāgakeśarapuṣpāṇi tadante labhate phalam |
phalaṃ sarpiḥ jala dānāt phalaṃ prāpnoti vidyayā
ajayo bhavate loko vidyādhara-dharādhipaḥ |
etatte sarvamākhyātaṃ vijayākhyaṃ vratottamam
siddhidaṃ sarvalokānāṃ vidhinā tapasevanāt
iti śrī devipurāṇe vijayāvrataṃ nāma śatatamo'dhyāyaḥ |

ekādhikaśatatamo'dhyāyaḥ |

manuruvāca |

ataḥ paraṃ pravakṣyāmi rūpasaubhāgyakārakam |
nakṣatravidhinā vatsa yathā tuṣyati śaṃkarī
mārgādārabhya mūlena pādau jātimayaiḥ srajaiḥ |
pūjayetsopavāsastu nakṣatroktaṃ tu pāraṇam
yavānnaṃ haviṣā siddhaṃ brāhmane jaṃghe prapūjayet |
kahlārairmṛgarājaiśca tilamāṣānnabhojanam
tenaivaṃ prathamaṃ viprā aśvinyāṃ jānūni yajet |
kundaiḥ asitapuṣpaiśva bhojanaṃ dadhiśarkarā
āṣāḍhadvaye'pi tāṃ devīṃ vilvapatraiḥ prapūjayet |
nakṣatrāṃte tu bhuṃjīyāt brāhmaṇān tacca pāraṇam
yugmaṃ phālgunaṃ guhyaṃ tu pārayantyā prapūjayet |
dadhibhaktaṃ tu naivedyaṃ koṭiñca kṛtikairyajet
damanaiḥ sitapuṣpaiśca laḍḍūkā devī bhojane |
bhādrapade dvau ca pārśve pūjayetkusumaiḥ sitaiḥ
kṣīrānnaṃ devī viprāṇāṃ nakṣatrānte tu bhojanam |
pauṣyā kukṣigatā devyā sahakārasrajairyajet
ghṛtamāṣānna bhojanaṃ tu anurādhā uro yajet |
karṇikārasrajaiḥ pītairbhojanaṃ ghṛtapācitam
pṛṣṭhadeśaṃ dhaniṣṭhāsu hemapuṣpaiḥ prapūjayet |
karṇapatrañca naivedyaṃ devīṃ śākhāsu pūjayet
marupatraiḥ sugandhaiśca deyaṃ bhojyaṃ tu pāyasam |
karau kareṇa pūjyantu uśīratagarādibhiḥ
guḍaṃ kṣīraṃ tu naivedyaṃ mañjulāśca punarvasau |
kuṃkumena prapūjyeta deyaṃ bhojyantu ṣaṣṭhikam
naravān bhujaṃgadaivatye punnāgādibhiḥ pūjayet |
bhojyantuḥ mārjjitā deyā grīvāṃ jyeṣṭhāsu pūjayet
sitamālābhirdevyāyāḥ deyaṃ bhojyaṃ ghṛtādikam |
rakta puṣpadalaiḥ karṇaiḥ pūjayet bhojayeddhaviḥ
puṣye bhūyantu padmādyaiḥ śarkarānnaṃ tu bhojayet |
daśanān svātinā sevyā suraktaiḥ kuḍmalairyajet
hāsyantu śatabhiṣaijyā nāgakeśaracandanaiḥ |
kharjūraśarkarābhojyaṃ nāsikāsu maghāṃ yajet
yavapuṣpaistathā bhojyaṃ godhūmakṛtisaṃskṛtam |
mṛganetre tu devyāyāḥ sugandhaiḥ kusumairyajet
citrācitrasrajairdevyā lalāṭaṃ citrabhojanam |
bharaṇī śirasā devyāṃ campakādi srajairyajet
kṣīrānnabhojanaṃ deyamārdrakeśān prapūjayet |
jātyādi kusumairdevyāḥ sarvātmāni ca bhojanam
nakṣatramātarā hyetāḥ rūpaputrārthibhiḥ sadā |
śambhuṃ vāpyathavā viṣṇuṃ ghṛtahomānnadakṣiṇā
deyaṃ vastrayugaṃ vipre sapatnīke jitendriye |
devyāśāstrārthakuśale śivajñānaviśārade
sampūrṇa-candravadanā padma-patrāyatekṣaṇā |
śobhanā daśanā śubhrā karṇau cāpi sumāṃsalau
ṣaṭpadodaranibhaiḥ keśaistathā kokilanādinī |
tāmroṣṭhī padmapatrākṣī suhastā stananāmitā
nābhiḥ pradakṣiṇāvarttā rambhādalanibhoru ca |
suśroṇī mṛdumadhyā ca suśliṣṭāṃguliśobhanā
pramadā subhagā bhartturmanuṣyo'pi mahābhujaḥ |
pīnavakṣāḥ pṛthubhāvaḥ pūrṇacandranibhānanaḥ
sitadanto gajagāmī mahābalaparākramaḥ |
priyaḥ sarvasya lokasya padmapatrāyatekṣaṇaḥ
mṛduvākhāsyayuktaśca strīṇāṃ ca manohārakaḥ |
kāmatulyo mahāvipro vratenānena jāyate
nāriyogaśca iṣṭānāmarthānāñca śubhāgamaḥ |
nakṣatrākhyaṃ mahāpuṣyaṃ vratānāntu vratottamam
āpatsvapi na bhedaṃ tu priyaiḥ kāryaṃ yaducyate |
api doṣātmakairbhāvairna tyājyaṃ munisattama
iti śrīdevīpurāṇe nakṣatravrataṃ nāmaikādhikaśatatamo'dhyāyaḥ |

dvyadhikaśatatamo'dhyāyaḥ |

agastya uvāca |

āṣāḍhe toyadhenūṃ yo ghṛtaṃ bhādrapade tathā |
māghe tu tiladhenūḥ syātsa dattvā labhate hitam
vidyādhara uvāca |

kāni dānāni devyāyā deyāni munisattama |
kāni pātrāṇi deśaṃ vā kālaṃ dravyavidhiṃ vada
tānyahaṃ śrotumicchāmi kathayasva prasādataḥ |

agastya uvāca |

nyāyato yāni prāptāni śākānyapi nṛpottama
tāni devyāni devyāyāḥ kanyakā yoṣitāṃ sadā |
tadbhakteṣu ca vipreṣu apareṣu ca nityaśaḥ
viśeṣāt prāvṛṣi vatsa devī kāmān prayacchati |
deśaṃ nandāgayāśailaṃ gaṃgānarmadāpuṣkaram
vārāṇasyāṃ kurukṣetraṃ prayāgaṃ jambukeśvaram |
kedāraṃ bhīmanādañca daṇḍakaṃ puṣkarāhvayam
someśvaraṃ mahāpuṇyaṃ tathā amarakaṇṭakam |
kālañjaraṃ tathā vindhyaṃ yatra vāsaṃ guhasya tu
dravyaṃ bhū-hema-go-dhānyaṃ tilavastraghṛtādikam |
vidhinā upavāsena ekānnaṃ naktabhojanam
śucinā bhāvapūtena kṣānti-satya-vratādinā |
api sarṣapamātro'pi dātāraṃ tārayeddadat
yaḥ punarvidhinā vatsa devīmuddiśya prāvṛṣi |
vipreṣu viprakanyāsu tilādīn saṃprayacchati
tadā saṃtuṣyate devī acireṇa tu vidyayā |
ataḥ paraṃ pravakṣyāmi nandā devyāḥ paraṃ vratam
yena saṃprīyate vatsa acireṇa mahātmanām |
hemotthaṃ pāduke kārye yathāśaktyā tu bhāvitaḥ
āmradūrvākṣatabilvapatraiḥ pūjitamantaḥ |
devīṃ sampūjayitvā tu sthaṃḍile pratimāsu vā
tadbhaktāya ca viprāya kanyāsu ca nivedayet |
mucyate sarvapāpebhyo svargalokaṃ ca gacchati
tanukṣaye mahāprājño vidyādharapatirbhavet |
kālena cehāyātaḥ pṛthivyā nṛpasattama
bhavate nātra sandeho brahmaṇedaṃ ca bhāṣitam |
prajāpatirvaśiṣṭhena kaśyapasya ca dakṣayoḥ
tathā tvamapi rājendra kuruṣvedaṃ padavratam |
mahadaiśvaryakāṃkṣāya devīpratyakṣakāriṇe
iti śrīdevī purāṇe padavrataṃ nāma dvyadhikaśatatamo'dhyāyaḥ |
|
tryadhikaśatatamo'dhyāyaḥ |

agastya uvāca |

athātaḥ sampravakṣyāmi tava dānamanuttamam |
yena tuṣṭā purā devī śakrasya tu mahātmanaḥ
nīlāṃ vā yadi vā śvetāṃ pāṭalāṃ kapilāṃ pivā |
aduḥravāṃ vatsavālāñca sukhadohāṃ gavāṃ nṛpa
ādāya vidhivaddevīṃ pūjayet srajapaṃkajaiḥ |
dhūpañca pañcaniryāsaṃ saturuṣkāgurūcandanam
dattvā mantrapūjāntu devyā naivedyamupakalpayet |
pāyasaṃ ghṛtasaṃyuktaṃ kṣamāpayet tathā tu tām
dvijāya śivabhaktāya nivedayet savatsagām |
sahemavastrakāñcayāñca mahatpuṇyamavāpnuyāt
yāvat yadromasaṃkhyānaṃ tāvaddevyāḥ pure vaset |
ihatra vigatapāpo jāyate nṛpasattamaḥ
manunāyaṃ vidhiṃ kṛtvā prāptaṃ lokamanuttamam |
ahaṃ te kathayiṣyāmi śṛṇu rājan yathāvidhi
śubhāṃ hemamayīṃ gāvaṃ kārayedrajatakhurām |
tāṃ vastraprāvṛtāṃ kṛtvā pūjayed danudaryahām
vicitra citrapuṣpaiśca gandhadhūpanivedanaiḥ |
tathā kṣamāpayeddevīṃ tāṃ gāṃ tatraivamānayet
devī tvadīya ādeśāt tava bhakteṣu dīyate |
punastāṃ viprarājāya dāpayet śivabhāvite
akṣayaphalakāmena prāyaścitaviśuddhaye |
manunā cīrṇamāsīcca vratamanyaiḥ nṛpottamaiḥ
saptapūrvānparān vaṃśānapi kilviṣasaṃsthitān |
uddhṛtya nayate vatsa devīlokamanuttamam
iti śrī devīpurāṇe hemagovrataṃ nāma tryadhikaśatatamo'dhyāyaḥ |

caturadhikaśatatamo'dhyāyaḥ |

manuruvāca |

mārge rasottamaṃ dadyāt ghṛtaṃ poṣe mahāphalam |
tilā māghe muniśreṣṭha dhānyāḥ saptātha phālgune
vicitrāṇi ca vastrāṇi caitre dadyāt dvijottamaḥ |
vaiśākhe yavagodhūmān jyeṣṭhe toyabhṛtān ghaṭān
āṣāḍhe candanaṃ deyaṃ karpūrañaca mahāphalam |
navanītaṃ nabho māsi caitra proṣṭha pade matam
guḍaśarkaraśaṃḍādyān laḍaḍūkānaśvine mune |
dīpadānaṃ mahāpuṇyaṃ kārttike yaḥ prayacchati
sarvakāmānavāpnoti kramānmārgādudāhṛtān |
dhenūṃ pauṣe ghṛtāṃ dadyāt māghe tilamayīṃ tathā
jyeṣṭhe toyamayī dadyāt ghṛta vatsāṃ mahāphalām |
surūpāṃ śrāvaṇe dadyāt gāṃ mahāphaladāyikām
sarvahemamayaiḥ śṛṃgaiḥ raupyapādairudāhṛtām |
kāmÌsyapātrāṃ saghaṇṭāṃ tuḥ kiṃkiṇīrupaśobhitām
sayugāṃ sasrajāṃ vatsa dātavyā vidhinānayā |
devī brahmeśasūryaṃ vā viṣṇuṃ vātha yathāvidhi
svabhāvacitta sampanno pūjayitvā dvijottama |
dātavyā vītarāge tu kāmakrodhavivarjitam
ayācake sadācāre vinīte niyamānvite |
go pradātā labhet kāmān svarge loke manoramān
agastya uvāca |

tiladhenūṃ pravakṣyāmi durgā yena prasīdati |
api duṣkṛta karmāṇi yāṃ dattvā nirmalo bhavet
pratyakṣā yena devī tu rājyaputrasuravāvahā |
bhavate tvacireṇaiva tāṃ śrṛṇuṣva nṛpottama
devadevīmanujñāpya snātvā caiva jitendriyaḥ |
pūjayet puṣpa-gaṃdhānna-dhūpa-dīpa-pavitrakaiḥ
hutvā hutāśane devīṃ tathā droṇamayīṃ kuru |
āḍhakena bhavedvatsa sarvaratnavibhūṣitām
hemaśrṛṃgīṃ śaphaiḥ rupyai gaṃdhaghrāṇāṃ suśobhanām |
mukhaṃ guḍamayaṃ kāryaṃ jihvāmannamayī tathā
kambalaṃ śuklasūtrāṃ tu pādo ikṣumayāstathā |
tāmraṃ pṛṣṭhe bhavet tasyā īkṣaṇaṃ maṇimoktikaiḥ
cārupatramayau kaṇau dantaiḥ phalamayaiḥ śubhaiḥ |
navanītastanāṃ kuryāt puṣpamālāmayaṃ kuru
puñchañca maṇimuktaistu phalai śuciṃ samarpayet |
śubhāṃ vastrayugacchannāṃ cāruchatravibhūṣitām
īdṛksaṃsthānasampannāṃ kṛtvā śraddhāsamanvitaḥ |
kāmÌsyopadohanaṃ dadyāt devyā me prīyatāmiti
mantrābhimantritaṃ kṛtvā tadbhaktāya nivedayet |
yāvanti tilavastrāṇi dhātumūlaphalasya ca
vidyante rajareṇūṃṣi tāvatsvarge vasennaraḥ |
pitṛn vigatapāpāmÌstu kṛtvādhastha gatānapi
prāpya devyāḥ śubhaṃ lokaṃ sthāpayedavicāraṇāt |
tasmin me ramate vatsa yāvadācandratārakam
tathā kālādihāyāto jāyate pṛthivīpatiḥ |
vinaya-teja-sampanno bahuputraḥ sukhānvitaḥ
punardevyāvrate nityaṃ pūjane vidhivattathā |
prāpya yogamaheśvaryaṃ prāpnoti padamavyayam
iti śrī devīpurāṇe tilaghenurnāma caturadhikaśatatamo'dhyāyaḥ |

agastya uvāca |

tilābhāve pradātavyā sarpirdhenū vijānatā |
snāpayitvā bhavānīntu ghṛtakṣīrairyathāvidhiḥ
pūjayet srajamālābhi rnaivedyaiḥ sumanoramaiḥ |
āharetsarvadravyāṇi upakalpeta tatra tān
gavye sarpiṣi kumbhe tu puṣpamālāvibhūṣite |
kāṃsyapātraṃ tathā vastraischādayīta vijānatā
hiraṇyagarbhasahitaṃ maṇividrumamauktikaiḥ |
pādānikṣumayān kuryāt kuryādraupyāṃstathā śaphān
hema cakṣustathā śṛṃgo kṛṣṇāgurumayai śubhaiḥ |
saptadhānyāni tatpārśve patrorṇena ca kambalam
ghrāṇo tagarakarpūṃro stanāḥ phalamayā śubhāḥ |
mukhañca gurukṣīreṇa sitāṃ jihvāṃ prakalpayet
pucchaṃ kṣaumamayaṃ kāryaṃ romāṇi sitasarṣapaiḥ |
tāmraṃ pṛṣṭhaṃ vicitrantu sneharūpā manoramā
vidhinā ghṛtavatsaṃ ca kuryād lakṣaṇalakṣitam |
etau kṛtvā tathā nandāṃ pūjayitvā vidhānataḥ
tadbhaktāya pradātavyā maṃgalāśāstrapārage |
mātre sadopakārāya gṛhna me'nugrahāya ca
prīyatāṃ nandinī devī maṅgalā carcikā umā |
ityuktvā arcayeddhenūṃ kṛtvā nandāmanonugām
anena vidhinā deyā yavaśālīkṣūkalpitā |
hemaratnānnavastrā vā deyā gaurvidhinā nayā
mucyate sarvapāpebhyaḥ sarvakāmānavāpnuyāt |
yatra kṣīravahā nadyo yatra sarpirvahā hradāḥ
payasā kardamā yatra tasmin loke mahīyate |
teṣāṃ svāmitvamāpnoti mudayā parayā yutaḥ
diśāṃ pūrvāparāṃstāta ātmanastvekaviṃśatiḥ |
bhūyaḥ pṛthvī śatāmeti ihaloke samāgataḥ
sakāmānāmiyaṃ vyuṣṭiḥ tatastāvadudāhṛtā |
devyā lokamavāpnoti niṣkāmo ghṛtadhenudaḥ
iti śrī devīpurāṇe ghṛtadhenūrnāma pañcādhikaśatatamo'dhyāyaḥ |

ṣaḍdhikaśatatamo'dhyāyaḥ |

agastya uvāca |

toyadhenūṃ śruṇu vatsa yathā devī prasīdati |
kumbhaṃ toyasamāpūrṇaṃ ratnavastrayugānvitam
samastabījasaṃyuktaṃ dūrvāpallava śobhitam |
murābālamuśīraṃ ca kuṣṭāmalakacandanaiḥ
mālācchatramupānahaṃ tilapātraiścaturyutam |
dadhikṣaudraghṛtaṃ pātraṃ vidhānamupakalpayet
vatsakaṃ pūjayedvatsa kṛtaṃ havimayaṃ budhaḥ |
devīmambharcya vidhivat sopavāso ca naktavān
devyā bhakte pradātavyaṃ sarvakāmānavāpnuyāt |
jayārisūdanī devī devānāṃ bhayanāśinī
vedamāte vare durge sarvege śubhade namaḥ
anena vatsa mantreṇa tāṃ dānāyābhimantrayet |
devī me prīyatāṃ nityaṃ yathepsita phalā śivā
iti śrī devīpurāṇe jaladhenūrnāma ṣaḍadhikaśatatamo'dhyāyaḥ |

saptādhikaśatatamo'dhyāyaḥ |

manuruvāca |

svayambhureṣa bhagavān vedodgītaḥ purā tvayā |
śivādyāḥ ṛṣiparyantāḥ smārttā vāsthāna kārakāḥ
kathaṃ mātā bhaveddevī etatkautuhalaṃ mama
brahmovāca |

jñānaśaktiḥ kriyā dhenūrdevyārūpāḥ prakīrtitāḥ |
mātṛkā jñānaśaktistu kriyā sā tamarūpiṇī
vāmādyā sā tridhā bhūtvā jyeṣṭhā raudrā ṛjusthitā |
kuṃḍalī trikaṭākārā dvau dvau vindusamanvitā
sā prasūtāṣṭavargāṇi svarā vaso dvidhā punaḥ |
anunāsāṃśca ghoṣāṃśca ekonā śatamardditān
mātarā tasya vargasthāṃ dṛṣṭavyaḥ prathamaḥ śivaḥ |
ṣoḍaśāntavibhaktastu akāre saṃvyavasthitaḥ
akāre brahmarūpeṇa śivarūpeṇa cāpare |
viṣṇu-skanda-yama-śakra-carcikāntara-saṃsthitā
vindau candrārkasūryau tu tataḥ sā śatadhā matā |
kriyārūpā bhaveddevī vedamātā śṛṇusva te
oṃkārapraṇavā vedā gāyatrī vetasambhavā |
ṣaḍaṃgāste samākhyātā upāṃgāścaturo'pare
chandolakṣaṇasaṃyuktā mātṛkā garbhajā viduḥ
manuruvāca |

kiṃ vedo rūpamānena upāṃgaṃ saṃkhyābhedataḥ |
bhaktaṃ kiṃ vedarūpantu tanme brūhi samāsataḥ
brahmovāca |

eka eva bhavedvedaścaturbhedaḥ punaḥ kṛtaḥ |
śākhārthamalpasattvānāṃ grahaṇā yātivistarāt
saṃvibhakto mayā vatsa ṛgyajuḥ sāmātharvaṇaḥ |
atra bhedāstu ṛgvede daśa caiva prakīrtitā
āśleṣāḥ saṃkhyā carcāśca śrāvakāścarcakāstathā |
śrāvaṇīya cakramā ca puṭakramavaṭakramāḥ
daṃḍaśceti samāsena punarekaiva pāragāḥ |
śākhāśca vividhā bhūyaḥ śākalā brahmamātṛkāḥ
teṣāmadhyayanaṃ proktaṃ maṃḍalāścatuṣaṣṭikāḥ |
vargāṇāṃ parisaṃkhyātaṃ caturviśaśatāni ca
ṛcāṃ daśasahasrāṇi ṛcāṃ pañcaśatāni ca |
ṛá¹cāmaśītipādañca tatra pāraṇamucyate
ṛgvede tu bhavetsaṃkhyā yajurvedasya śrūyatām |
ṣaḍaśītivibhedena mayā bhinnaṃ śivājñayā
daśadhā carakā tatra kārakā vidradhiṣayā |
kaṭhāprācyaḥ kaṭhāścaiva kapiṣṭhalakaṭhāstathā
cārāyaṇīyāḥ śvetāśca śvetātārā maitrāyaṇīyā |
punaḥ saptavibhedena maitrāyaṇyaḥ prakīrtitāḥ
mānava-dundubha-vārāhāśchāgeyāḥ hāridravīyāḥ |
sāmasāyanīyāśca teṣāmadhyayanamucyate
aṣṭādaśasahasrāṇi paṭhan śākhāvido bhavet |
dviguṇaṃ padapāṭhī yastriguṇaṃ kramapāragaḥ
ṣaḍaṃgāni yadādhītya ṣaḍaṃgaviducyate |
śikṣā kalpo vyākaraṇaṃ niruktaṃ chando jyotiṣam
ṣaḍaṃgāni bhavantyetānyupāṃgāni śṛṇu kathyatām |
pratipadamantrapadaṃ chando bhāṣā mīmāṃsā ca
nyāyatarkasamāyuktā upāṃgāḥ parikīrtitāḥ |
pariśiṣṭāśca saṃkhyātāḥ aṣṭādaśa śṛṇusva tat
yūpalakṣaṇapratiṣṭhā tu vākyaṃ saṃkhyā caraṇavyūhaḥ |

praśamanānām, kuṭajatvak śleṣma-pitta-rakta-sāṃgrahikopaśoṣaṇānām, kārśmayaphalaṃ saṃgrāhaka rakta-pitta-praśamanānām, pṛśniparṇi sāṃgrāhika vātahara dīpanīya vṛṣyāṇām, vidārigandhā vṛṣyasarvadoṣaharāṇām, valā sāṃgrāhika-valya-vātaharāṇām, gokṣurako mūtra-kṛcchrānila harāṇām, hiṃgu niryāsa-chedanīya-dīpanīya-anulomika-vāta-kapha-praśamanānām, amlavetaso bhedanīya-ānulomika-śleṣma-praśamanānām, yāvaśūkaḥ saṃgrahaṇāya-prācanīya arśoghnānām, takrābhyāso śvāsagrahaṇīya doṣāt ghṛtavyāpta praśamanānām, kravyād māṃsābhyāso grahaṇī-doṣa śoṣośorghnānām, kṣīraghṛtābhyāso rasāyanānām, samaghṛtasaktuprāśābhyāso vṛṣyodā-varttaharāṇām, (telagaṇḍūṣābhyāso dantavalarucikarāṇām, candanoḍumbaraṃ mohanirvāpaṇopalepanānām, rāgnāgurunī śītāpanaya pralepanānām, lomajjakośīraṃ-dāha-tvagdoṣa-svedāpanayana-pralepanānām, kuṣṭhaṃ vātaharābhyaṃgopānahayoginām, madhūkaṃ cakṣuṣyavṛṣya-keśaya-kanṭhya-varṇya-virajanīya-ropanīyānām, vāyuḥ prāṇasaṃjñā-pradhānahetūnām, agniḥ āmastambha-śīta-śūla-udvavana-praśamanānām, jalaṃ stambhanīyānām, mṛdbhṛṣṭaloṣṭa nirvāpitamudakaṃ tṛṣātiyoga-praśamanānām,) atimātrāśanaṃ āmapradoṣahetunām, yathāgnyambubhyāhāro agnisandhukṣanānām, yathāsāmyaṃ ceṣṭāvyavahāraśca sevyānām, kālebhījanamārogyakarāṇām, vegasandhāraṇaṃ anārogyakarāṇām, tṛptirāhāraguṇānām, madyaṃ saumanasyajanānām, madyakṣepo dhī-dhṛtiḥ-smṛtiharāṇām,

sarveṣāṃ sādhane heturārogyaṃ samudāhṛtam |
tasmātprayatnato vatsa prathamenaṃ samabhyaset
vedāṃgānāṃ yathā jyotirvariṣṭhaḥ munisattama |
upāṃgānāṃ tathā caitadāyurvedo varaḥ smṛtaḥ
kapilo hemakukṣiśca varuṇo jaladādhipaḥ |
mekhalo niṣadho rudro dundubhiḥ pulaho hariḥ
yajanaḥ sāmakaścenduḥ kāśikā janako vapuḥ |
hemaḥ sumālī dīptitaśca bhānuvarṇaḥ prabhākapiḥ
suṣeṇo mahimā rpigo brahmā dakṣaprajāpatiḥ |
aśvinau vṛtrahā atrirete vedavidāṃvarāḥ
āyurvedārthakuśalāramaratvaṃ gatā mune |
mitrāṇāmupakārāya apakārāya śatrave
hitāhitasya vettāro dṛṣṭādṛṣṭaprasādhanam |
smāritaṃ paraprītināṃ śivena paramātmanā
khaṭvā jighāṃsatā vatsa āyurveda prakāśitaḥ
iti śrī devīpurāṇe āyurveda-nirdeśa-samāptirnāma daśādhikaśatatamo'dhyāyaḥ |

aṣṭādaśādhikaśatatamo'dhyāyaḥ |

vaśiṣṭha uvāca |

mātaro bhairavaṃ durgāṃ śīrṇa gehasamāśritām |
cālayitvā tu prāsādaṃ kuryādyastu dvijottamaḥ
pakveṣṭadāruśailaṃ vā tatra pūjāphalaṃ śṛṇu |
brahmendrarudraviṣṇūnāṃ sūryasya ca dvijottama

navabhedāḥ samākhyātāḥ ekamekena mātaraḥ |
tāsāntu mātṛkādevī cāmuṇḍā rurughātinī

kālkāvajraghorāṇāṃ damanī vā na rākṣasāḥ

niṣpanneṣu muhūrtteṣu pratiṣṭhāvidhinā viśet |
pratimā vā yadā jīrṇā pīṭhikā vātha cālayet

hemalāṃgūlakaṃ kṛtvā śivaṃ cānyaṃ vipaścitā

pratiṣṭhāvidhimāśritya sarvaṃ kuryād dvijottama

aśocyāste vijānīyād dhūtapāpāḥ mahādhipaḥ
mūlāccaturguṇaṃ puṇyamāpnuyāt jīrṇakārakāḥ |
tasmāt sarvaprayatnena jīrṇaṃ pālyaṃ vipaścitā
śūnyaṃ devālayaṃ vatsa yasmin deśe'pi tiṣṭhati |

jīrṇa dehaṃ yathā dehī tyaktvā cānyaṃ samāśrayet |
devatā jīrṇaṃ prāsādaṃ tyaktvānyatra tu yāntyapi

agastya uvāca |

japtvā tu caturaṣṭantu aṣṭāviṃśamathāpi vā |

śākayāvakakṣīrāśī karamūlaphalāśanaḥ |

parṇoṃdumbara rājīvaḥ vilvapatra kuśodakaiḥ |

ayamevāti kṛcchraḥ syāt pāṇipurānnabhojanaiḥ

dvādaśāhopavāsena parākaḥ parikīrttitaḥ

tulāpuruṣa ityeṣa jñeyaḥ pañca daśāhikaḥ

vahnervidhānaṃ paramaṃ sarvakāmaprasādhakam |

vṛhaspatiruvāca |

ekastriguṇa ākhyātaḥ sarvadeva sukhāvahaḥ |
bahudhā tatkathaṃ karma yojayanti dvijottamā
dakṣiṇāgni vibhāgaṃ tu prasūtirbahudhā tathā |
nāmabhiḥ karmabhirddeva kathayasva samāsataḥ
evamuktastu guruṇā brahmā lokapitāmahaḥ |
uvāca madhurāṃ vāṇīṃ śṛṇuṣvāvahito dvija
brahmovāca |

purā kṛtayuge vipra eka eva hutāśana |
rudramūrtti sthito nityaṃ tejo nāma mahātmanaḥ
tretāyāṃ dakṣiṇeśo vai yajñārthaṃ visṛjanmahān |
gārhapatyaṃ tamo jātaṃ havanīyaṃ tato'bhavat
havanīya prasūtistu bharatādyā mahaujasaḥ |
ekapañcāśataṃ nāma carācaravidhāyakāḥ
teṣāṃ vai nāma karmāṇi bahudhā brūhi bho dvija |
sapta sapta vibhāgena teṣāṃ santatijātayaḥ
bharatī varamāṃgalye vibhuśca bala aṃgirāḥ |
samudbhavo jayo rudraḥ saṃyugaḥ kāliko bhavaḥ
sūryo janaḥ śaśāṃkaśca viśvedevāḥ parāvasuḥ |
kalmāṣaḥ saṃcayo ghoro vaḍavāgni varāntakaḥ
dakṣo nidhīśvaraḥ kāmaḥ kālāntaka parāntakau |
bībhatso vijayo dhūmraḥ kṛṣṇavarṇo'thahāṭakaḥ
ajitaḥ śaṃkaraḥ śaṃkhaḥ śuddhido jayado guruḥ |
aparo'parājitaḥ kaśca pratāpo bahudaḥ śubhaḥ
āraṇyaḥ sarvagaḥ śambhuḥ kāmiko ripuhā śivaḥ |
garbhādhānādisaṃskāraiḥ sa bhavet sarvadakāmadaḥ
parigrahānurūpeṇa tathā homavaśena ca |
laghvāhāro viśuddhaśca nityahotā prakīrttitaḥ
kṛtvā hutāśane paṃca karmāṇi bhavate sadā |
sarvasiddhi pradāyitvādanyathā havane caruḥ
ādhāne bhavate hyagnirbara puṃsavane sthitaḥ |
sīmante maṃgalo nāma jātakarma vibhuḥ smṛtaḥ
nāme balaḥsamākhyātaḥ prāśane aṃgirā mataḥ |
cūḍe samudbhavo vahnirjayo vratanibandhane
rudro godāniko nāma vivāhe saṃyugaḥ smṛtaḥ |
agniśca kāliko nāma agnihotre vidhīyate
āvasathye bhavo jñeyaḥ pitṛṇāṃ viśvadevakaḥ |
analo jaṭharo vahniḥ kalmāṣo'mṛtabhakṣaṇe
sūryo vahnirmahāhome jalo jalaniveśane |
śaśāṃkaḥ pūrṇimāhome kṣaye samvarttako mataḥ
ghoraḥ kāṣṭha samṛddhaśca parānto veṇusambhavaḥ |
samudre vaḍavāgnistu dakṣaḥ pākavidho mataḥ
nidhīśo vasudhārāyāṃ kāmadevo'tha dhūmajaḥ |
tūṣajaḥ kāmahā tvagnau rathyāyānta parāntakaḥ
bībhatsu kṣutkaro vahnirvijayo nṛpagehajaḥ |
dhūmajo vṛkṣasamutthastu dīpe kṛṣṇapatho mataḥ
hemaṃ tāpe bhavedvādye ajito mātṛveśmajaḥ |
saṃgaro mlecchalokeṣu śaṃkho vai ceṣṭapākajaḥ
āditye śuddhiṃ vijānīyājjayaḥ śukraniveśane |
gurudīkṣāvidhau vahniraparo tiṇḍileṣu ca
kaṇṭhānukūlajo viddhi lakṣahoma parājitaḥ |
pratāpo nṛpadīkṣāyāṃ vahudānajaśoṇajaḥ
śubho grahavidhau hyagnirāraṇye araṇībhavaḥ |
sarvago vaidyuto vahniḥ śambhurmaṇisamudbhavaḥ
kāmikaḥ sādhakāgniśca ripuhā abhicārajaḥ |
koṭihome śivo vahniḥ sarvakāma prasādhakaḥ
śivatejodbhavo vipra kālāgniḥ sa ca kīrttitaḥ |
eko bahuprakāraistu nāma karmairyathāsthitaḥ
kathitaḥ pāvako vatsa kiṃ bhūyaḥ paripṛcchati
iti śrī devīpurāṇe vahnibhedonāma dvāviṃśatyadhikaśatatamo'dhyāyaḥ |

trayoviṃśatyadhikaśatatamodhyāyaḥ |

nṛpavāhana uvāca |

vahnikarmaphalaṃ vipra kathitañcāvadhāritam |
puṣpagandhaviśeṣantu śrotumicchāmi tattvataḥ
agastya uvāca |

pātrāṇāṃ hemaraupyotthaiḥ yathā prokto nṛpottama |
ghṛtahome varaṃ yadvat tilāśca madalepane
candanāguru karpūra nakhaṃ dhūpe varaṃ matam |
mada karpūra kāśmīraṃ rocanā ca catuṣṭayam
etena lepayeddevyāḥ sarvakāmānāpnuyāt |
jātī kaṃkola-patrailā-kuṣṭakuṃkuma patrikā
jātīphalo latākhyā ca snānagandhā sadādharā |
nāga keśara karpūra surāmāṃsī sabālakāḥ
udvarttanāḥ samākhyātāḥ sadaiva mātarapriyāḥ |
dhūpaṃ kalyāṇa nāgantu nityaṃ devyā priyaṃ nṛpa
candrākhyaṃ lepanaṃ deyaṃ sarvasiddhipradāyakam |
maṇimauktika mālāśca vitānañca dukūlajam
ghaṇṭādi sarvadā dattvā hemapuṣpaphalaṃ labheta |
puṣpairvāraṇya sambhūtaiḥ patraivā girisambhavaiḥ
aparyuṣitānyacchidraiḥ prokṣitairjantuvarjitaiḥ |
ātmārāmodbhavairvāpi puṣpaiḥ sampūjayecchivām
puṣpajāti viśeṣeṇa bhavetpuṇyaṃ viśeṣataḥ |
tapaḥ śīlaguṇopete pātre vedasya pārage
daśa dattvā suvarṇāni yatphalaṃ kusumeṣu tat |
mātarāṇāṃ sakṛddattvā labhate nṛpasattama
tasmāt puṣpān pravakṣyāmi patrāśca surabhīścaye |
ketakīñcātimuktaśca baka-bandhū-bakulā ṛṣiḥ
kadambaḥ karṇikāraśca sindhuvāraḥ samṛddhaye |
punnāga campakaṃ kundraṃ yūthikā navamallikā
damanā padmapatraśca śatadhā puṇyavṛddhaye |
tārārjunamallī ca bṛhatī śatapatrikā
karavīra kusuma kahlāra bilvapāṭala mālatī |
javā vijo kilāśoko raktanīlotpalāḥ sitāḥ
paṃkajaḥ śatapatraśca daśadhā puṇyavṛddhaye |
etaistu arccayeddevīmāśusiddhiḥ prayacchati
drauṇapuṣpī śamī kṣīrī nīlāpamārga patrikāḥ |
surasā barvarā bhadrā surabhī karṇamallikā
kadambairarcayedrātrau mallikā ubhayoḥ samā |
divyaśeṣāṇi puṣpāṇi yathālābhena pūjayet
kīṭakeśopaviddhāni śīrṇaparyuṣitāni ca |
saṃpatitāni ca puṣpāṇi tyajedupahatāni ca
mukulairnārca yeddevyāḥ apakvaṃ na nivedayet |
phalaṃ kvathitaṃ viddhañca yatnāt pakvamapi tyajet
alābhena ca puṣpāṇāṃ patrāṇyapi nivedayet |
patrāṇāmapyalābhe tu phalānyapi nivedayet
phalānāmapyalābhe tu tṛṇagulmauṣadhānyapi |
auṣadhīnāmalābhe tu bhaktyā bhavati pūjitā
pratyekamuktarapuṣpeṣu daśasauvarṇikaṃ phalam |
sannibaddheṣu teṣveva dviguṇaṃ phalamucyate
yaḥ sugandhai raktapuṣpaiḥ samyagdevīṃ prapūjayet |
mālābhirvāpi sumanaiḥ so'nantaṃ phalāmāpnuyāt
bilvapatrairakhaṇdairyaḥ sakṛlliṃgaṃ prapūjayet |
sarvapāpavinirmuktaḥ śivaloke mahīyate
yaḥ kuryācca śivārāmamāmrabilvādi śobhitam |
jātī vijayaparājārka karavīrābja kubjakaiḥ
punnāga nāga bakulai aśokotpala campakaiḥ |
kadalī hempuṣpādyaistasya dānaphalaṃ śṛṇu
yāvat tatpatra kusuma bījayuti phalāni ca |
tāvadvarṣasahasrāṇi devyāloke sa modate
iti śrī devīpurāṇe puṣpavidhirnāma trayoviṃśatyadhikaśatatamo'dhyāyaḥ |

caturviṃśatyadhikaśatatamo'dhyāyaḥ |

nṛpavāhana uvāca |

samasta dharma kathanaṃ tava vaktrādviniḥsṛtam |
śrutaṃ bhūyo'pi pṛcchāmi devyā gurupūjanam
agastya uvāca
bhūgṛhe gṛhamadhye vā raktākhye girikandare |
nadī-nada-samudre vā prakoṣṭhe kūpavarjite
subhakta jana saṃkīrṇe śubhavāstūpa saṃsthite |
snātvā śāstravidhānena maṃtrapūrvaṃ nṛpottama
devyāmūlāga ṣaṭakaṃtu nyasya śastreṇa saṃsthitaḥ |
mṛdu carma kṛte śastre tūlakārpāsapūrite
evaṃvidhe sthito mantrī sudhūpāsitavāsasaḥ |
vitānadhvajasaṃchanne kaṭavastravibhūṣite
manorame kṛte sthāne devyā snānādikāḥ kriyāḥ |
kṛtvā pūrvavidhānena haimarājatatāmrajaiḥ
kalaśaistoyagaṃdhādyaiḥ pṛthakdhūpasudhūpitāḥ |
madādilepitā devyo dukūlaparivāritāḥ
muktāphalakṛtāhārāḥ padmarāga vibhūṣitāḥ |
khaḍgakheṭakapāśādi churikādi niveśayet
ghṛtapūrṇāni māṃsāni naivedyamupapādayet |
pūrvoktavidhinā vatsa pūjayet parameśvarīm
dhyātvā devīṃ śubhāṃ vatsa vigrahāmaparāṃ parām |
praṇipatya tathā devīmātmānamapi tādṛśam
kṛtvā japādikaṃ kāryaṃ vividhaṃ kāryasiddhaye |
tato nivedayitvā tu vahnikarma surakṣitam
kāryaṃ pūrvavidhānena sruvasrucyādirakṣite |
kuṇḍe sulakṣaṇopete vasordhārāṃ pratiṣṭhayet
pratiṣṭhā rasapātrāṇi home sā ca vidhiḥ śubhāḥ |
balidānaṃ pradātavyaṃ gṛheṣu vividheṣu ca
śubhānāṃ lokapālānāṃ nānāyakṣavināyakān |
kṛmi kīṭa pataṃgemyo bhūmau toyānnakalpanām
kṛtvā kṣamāpayeddevīṃ gurūpūjāṃ tathā kuru
iti śrī devīpurāṇe pūjāvidhirnāma caturviṃśatyadhikaśatatamo'dhyāyaḥ |

pañcaviṃśatyadhikaśatatamo'dhyāyaḥ |

agastya uvāca |

devāgniguruvidyāyāḥ pūjāyāḥ sadṛśaṃ phalam |
gurusteṣāṃ bhavetpūjyaḥ sarvakāma prasādhakaḥ
vidyāgni devatānāñca viśeṣa upadeśakaḥ |
yarthātho nyāyavādī ca saṃdeha vinivarttakaḥ
tasyoktāni ca vākyāni śraddheyāni vipaścitaiḥ |
yathārthaṃ puṇyapāpeṣu tadaśrutvā vrajatyadhaḥ
tasmāt sarvaprayatnena śivaṃ sampūjayet gurum |
nṛbhiḥ paropakārāya ātmanaśca vimuktaye
devyā yāgavidhānena tasya pūjā vidhīyate |
hema-gau-maṇi-bhūmyādi dānāni vinivedayet
gṛhamaṇḍapavidyādi śayyādaṇḍānādibhiḥ |
deyaṃ gurorviśeṣeṇa yadyadiṣṭatamaṃ bhuvi
tena sarvamavāpnoti tuṣṭena nṛpasattama |
aśakteṣu ca sarveṣu pāpairviśleṣito'pi vā
gurorbhāvagataṃ vittaṃ mahadbhaktyopabhojayet |
dakṣasya yajñavighnaṃ tu na tasya kṛtavedine
tathāpi na caledbhaktiḥ pārthasya ca tapodhane |
janamejayasya yajñe tu anyeṣāṃ ca mahātmanām
bhavanti vighnakarttāro dhairyātteṣu varapradāḥ
iti śrīdevīpurāṇe gurudevapūjāvidhirnāma pañcaviṃśatyadhikaśatatamo'dhyāyaḥ |

ṣaḍviṃśatyadhikaśatatamo'dhyāyaḥ |

nṛpavāhana uvāca |

japādhyayanayuktānāmantarāyā bhavanti ye |
teṣāṃ saṃśamanaṃ tāta śrotumicchāmi tattvataḥ
agastya uvāca |

devyāḥ saṃsmaraṇaṃ vatsa sarvavighnavināśanam |
anekadhā samākhyātaṃ tathāpi kathayāmi te
japena cātmanaḥ śuddhiḥ agnikāryeṇa sampadaḥ |
sampadā ceha karmāṇi sidhyanti muktidāni ca
tasmājjapādi saṃśuddho agnikāryaṃ samārabhet |
āśrayaṃ sarvasiddhināmihāputra phalapradam
pūrvoktalakṣaṇe kuṇḍe pūrvanāmni hutāśane |
śruvadravyādisaṃsāra sampannastu tato'gnaye
prokṣayitvā purā prājñaḥ kuṇḍaṃ mantrodakena tu |
tatastu veṣṭayet paścāt kavacena yathākramam
punarullakhanaṃ kuryāt astra bījena bho nṛpa |
dakṣiṇottaravāruṇyāṃ madhye tisrastathottare
punarabhyukṣaṇaṃ paścāt kavacena vidhānavit |
vistaraṃ kuṇḍamadhye tu praṇavena punarnyeset
tataḥ śaktiṃ nyaset tasmin taḍitsahasra sannibhām |
kratumayīṃ viśālākṣīṃ satataṃ yonimudrayā
yugakeśavasaṃ bhintaṃ dvitīyāśramasaṃmaṃ sthitam |
keśavāntarhito devo devī eṣā hutāśane
gaṃdhapuṣpārcitaṃ kṛtvā arpayitvā vidhānavit |
devyāḥ saṃtarpaṇārthāya tato vahniṃ prakalpayet
tenaiva sa vinirmukta veṣṭagaṃ niyojitaḥ |
sa eva parasaṃjñastu vahniḥ sarvārthasādhakaḥ
tāmrapātre śarāve vā ānayitvā hutāśanam |
astreṇa prokṣayet tattu punarbījaṃ niyojayet
tatastvāveṣṭayet paścāt kavacena yathāvidhiḥ |
sthāpayitvā śivā kuṇḍe yonimārgeṇa nikṣipet
jayākhyena tu mantreṇa hṛdayantu punaryajet |
garbhādhānaṃ bhavatyevaṃ jātavedasya pārthiva
śirasābhyarcayitvā tu jayāṃ devīṃ tato yajet |
kṛtaṃ pusavanaṃ hyevaṃ sīmantonnayanaṃ śṛṇu
ajitāmarcayet pūrvaṃ śivābījaṃ tato yajet |
sīmantakaraṇaṃ vahneḥ kṛtaṃ bhavati vedikam
astreṇa tu samabhyarcya japeddevyāparājitām |
jātakarmma kṛtaṃ hyevaṃ tato nāma vinirdiśet
vighneśamarcayitvā tu kavacasya vinirdiśet |
tato'sya śrāvayennāma devyagnisthaḥ hutāśanaḥ
nādevyo devyāśca karmāṇi sādhayanti kadācana |
tena kāryeṇa rājante kāryo devāgnipāvarke
jananeva ca śūdrāśca abhayākhyā niyojane |
bodhena aṃkuśādyā tu vīṇākhyā sarvakarmasu
evaṃ vahnistu saṃskṛtya mudrāmaṃtrairyathākramam |
tato homaṃ prakurvīta śāstradṛṣṭena karmaṇā
hṛdvīje nāstared darbhān paridhīśca nighāpayet |
prāgaganuttarāgrāṃśca punardevān prapūjayet
brahmāṇaṃ śaṃkaraṃ viṣṇuṃ mantreśaṃ samanvitam |
pūrvādārabhya gāyatryā viṣṭarasthān yathākramam
āgneyīṃ diśamāśritya ājyabhāgantu dāpayet |
adhiśrayaṇaṃ purā kṛtvā paścādutplavanādikam
proddeśamātrakaṃ darbhaṃ procchinne tu nakhena tu |
aṃguṣṭhānāmike gṛhya ghṛtasyotplavanaṃ kuru
tataḥ saṃplavane mantrī sammukhaṃ ghṛtamutpunaḥ |
darbhacūḍikayā samyak araṇyoktaṃ jvalaṃ tayā |

nairājanantu bāhyena udakena spṛśettataḥ
śruvasru cāṃ pratāpāgnau parigṛhya samantataḥ |
saṃspṛśya ca kuśaṃ sarvān agramadhyānalokikān
sthāpeddakṣiṇe pārśve ājyādīni tathottare |
hṛdayena vidhānajñaḥ sarvakarma samārabhet
tato'pi dhārayet vastrān devyābhistvanupūrvaśaḥ |
punarūdghāṭanaṃ kuryāt astrabījena pārthivaḥ
niskṛtiṃ tu mahāstreṇa dattvā sarpi rnirūpayet |
śive some tathā vahnau tatastridhā parikalpayet
tarpayitvā tato vahniṃ dattvā pūrṇāhutiṃ kramāt |
tatastvāsanavinyāsaṃ prāguktaṃ parikalpayet
pūrvoktena vidhānena gaṃdhapuṣpairanukramāt |
pūjayitvā mahādevyā tato homaṃ samācaret
bahuhavye dhane śuddhe susamiddhe hutāśane |
vidhūme lelihāneca vahninā yaḥ samidhyati
mṛtyuṃjayavidhānena kṣīrahavyo prapūjayet |
virejo vigate vatsa devīnāṃ saṃmatā bhavet
iti śrī devīpurāṇe homavidhirnāma ṣaḍviṃśatyadhikaśatatamo'dhyāyaḥ |

aṣṭāviṃśatyadhikaśatatamo'dhyāyaḥ |

brahmovāca |

sarvārthasādhakaṃ śārstraṃ brahmavaktrāt vinisṛtam |
tenāpi nṛpaśārdūṃla kīrttitaṃ naravāhane
indreṇa vidhinā prāptamagastyena tathāgatam |
daśalakṣapramāṇantu śivo brahmaṇe proktavān
labdhaṃ śakrasya lokasya vidyā devena bhāṣitam |
ghorotpatti vadhādīni devyārādhanamuttamam |
|
karmayogaśca yogaśca caturvargaprasādhakam
ādyaṃ devyavatāraṃ ca vācayed yaḥ śṛṇoti vā |
sa saṃsārādvinirmuktaḥ prāpnoti paramaṃ padam
vidyāsiṃhāsane madhye vastrapuṣpādi śobhite |
pūjayitvā śivaṃ jñātaṃ śṛṇuyādvācayet tathā
śrīmaddaṃḍāsanaṃ vāpi kṛtvā hemaṃ suśobhanam |
hemapaṭṭaparicchannaṃ nānāratnavibhūṣitam
rājataṃ tāmra kāsyaṃ vā brahmarītyā vinirmitam |
tarusārasamudbhūtaṃ śṛṃgavaṃśādisambhavam
ratna hemasamāyuktaṃ śaṃkhasphaṭika moktikaiḥ |
yathāsambhava sambhūtairadhaścordhvaṃ vibhūṣitam
samutkīrṇaṃ vicitraṃ ca sūtracinha vibandhanam |
dviguṇe dvipramāṇeṣu pūrṇaca ndranibheṣu ca
citrotkīrṇaṃ suvarṇeṣu pratipādeṣu saṃsthitam |
dukūlaṃ paṭṭadevāṃgaṃ citrapaṭṭādisambhavam
viddhaṃ kusumaraktaṃ vā prākāra śikharānvitam |
caturbhiścandrakairyuktaṃ paṃcavarṇaiḥ suśobhanaiḥ
kiṃkiṇīrava kopetaiḥ catuṣkoṇa samāśritaiḥ |
giriprākāraśikharaiḥ sulakṣaiḥ paṃca varṇakaiḥ
sarvavastrasamudbhūtaiḥ kandukaiśca pralamvibhiḥ
itthamāśravaṇaṃ kṛtvā vinyaset daṇḍakāsane |
tasyopari mahāśāstraṃ devyākhyaṃ sthāpya pūjayet
vidyādānopahāreṇa śobhāṃ kṛtvā prayatnataḥ |
gandhādivāsitakaraḥ śrīmadāsanasaṃsthitaḥ
bhāvayitvā śivaṃ devyāḥ śāstre'smin parameśvaram |
svayaṃ tiṣṭhati deveśī patiṃ devanamaskṛtam
svakāyena tīrtheṣu narendra-bhavaneṣu ca |
bhāvayetparamaṃ dharmaṃ gṛhagrāme pureṣu ca
śrotāraṃ ca gurudhyānaṃ śivaṃ dhyātvā yathāvidhiḥ |
gandhapuṣpaiśca sambhāraiḥ pratyahaṃ tu yuge yuge
pūjayitvā namitvā ca kṛtāṃjalipurāḥ sthitā |
sarve nīcāsanāḥ śāntā yathāvṛddha kramānugāḥ
dharmataḥ śrotumicchanti kathāntaravivarjitāḥ |
jñānārambhe samāptau ca śrotṛbhirvā cakena ca
devyā maṃtraṃ śivākhyaṃ ca uccāryaṃ sarvasiddhaye |
ānayed dhūpapuṣpādyai ekaikaḥ śrāvakaḥ kramāt
sarvasādhujanārthāya jñānamantraprado'pi vā |
ācārebhyaḥ karaṃ dadyāt vācakaḥ kusumatrayam
te'pi tairādimadhyāntaiḥ kuryuḥ pūjāṃ tu mastake |
iti śaktyā ca bhaktyā ca pūjāṃ kṛtvā sadakṣiṇām
pravarttaṃyati yaḥ kaścit devyāḥ pustaka vācanam |
sarvasattvopakārāya ātmanaśca vimuktaye
tasya puṇyaphalaṃ vakṣye śrotṛṇāṃ vācakasya ca |
dhanamāyuḥ prajā kīrttiḥ prajñāṃ buddhiṃ priyaṃ sukham
iha samprāpya vipulaṃ dehānte śāntimāpnuyāt |
asampūjya mahājñānaṃ pradeśe cāpyasaṃsthite
vācayannarakaṃ yāti tasmāt saṃskṛtya vācayet |
prasampūjya tathā vākyaṃ devāgnigurusannidhau
mune dharmapravāhasya upakārāya buddhimān |
yathā pravarttito dharmo adharmaṃ ca parityajet
lobhādbhayānna vācyedaṃ devyāḥ śāstraṃ śivātmakam |
vācanāttu jagacchāntiravadhāryaṃ dine dine
gaccheyuḥ kuśapuṣpārthaṃ śivomāpūjanāya ca |
tataḥ śāstraṃ samāpyaṃ tu pūjāṃ kṛtvā viśeṣataḥ
devyā vidyāguruṇāṃ ca bhaktyā ca śivayoginām |
kanyakā dvijabandhūnāmanyeṣāmapi buddhimān
bhojanaṃ kalpayeccaiṣāṃ dīnārthānāṃ ca sarvaśaḥ |
mitrasvakulasādhūnāmante bhṛtyajanasya ca
gurave dakṣiṇāṃ dadyācchivo gomithunaṃ śubham |
vastra yugmāṃgulīyakaṃ ghṛtapūrṇaṃ tu bhojanam
vācakāya pradātavyaṃ dakṣiṇā pūrvabhāṣitā |
abhāṣitasya dātavyā gurorardhena dakṣiṇā
śeṣāṇāṃ ca yathāśaktyā dakṣiṇāṃ śivayoginām |
dadyāt prabodhayet paścāt pradīpādeḥ śataṃ budhaḥ
vitānañca dhvajaṃ deyaṃ devī devasya bhojanam |
yathā mantravataḥ kāryaṃ pūjā nārcā vivarjitā
nivedayecchive devyai aśeṣaṃ puṣpavādinām |
jñānaṃ puṇyaṃ mahāśāntiṃ śravaṇānnātra saṃśayaḥ
evamudyotanaṃ kṛtvā devyāḥ śāstrasya bhaktitaḥ |
śiva - dīpa - pradātā ca pranaṣṭa tama saṃcayaḥ
vidhūtapāpakalilo viśuddhaste na saṃśayaḥ |
bhavanti sarvalokāstu bhāvitā deva yonayaḥ
aśeṣapāpanirmuktaḥ śṛṇu yat phalamāpnuyāt |
kule niśaṃkamuddhṛtya bhāryā putrādibhiryutaḥ
bahubhi svajanaiḥ snigdhai rbhṛtyadāsaiḥ samāśritaiḥ |
ityebhiḥ sahitaiḥ sarvaiḥ śrīmacchivapure brajet
mahāvimānarārūḍhaḥ sarvakāmasamanvitaḥ |
tatra bhuktvā mahābhoga yāvadācandrapāvakam
dātā harttā ca karttā ca yāvatsākṣāllaye mahat |
pralayānte tataḥ jñānaṃ prāpya yogamanutta mam
tato devyā prasādena mucyate nātra saṃśayaḥ |
yasmādavagataṃ kuryāt devyāḥ pustakavācanam
bhogāpavargaṃphaladaṃ śivabhaktyā dine dine |
na mārī na ca durbhikṣaṃ na rakṣāṃsi na vyādhayaḥ
nākāle mriyate rājā hanyate na ca śaktibhiḥ |
śṛṇoti yaśca satataṃ śivadharmaṃ narādhipaḥ
tatra deśe mahāpuṇye devyāḥ sannihitā nṛpa |
śrutvā sakṛnnigadato manoyogānnarādhipa
śivaḥ sahomayā tatra krīḍate bhaktimatāṃ pure |
dadāti sarvakāmāni manasepsitaphalāni ca
sakṛcchrutvā mahāpuṇyaṃ pratiṣṭhā yājñikaṃ nṛpa |
hemante brahmalokaṃ tu śiśire viṣṇunā saha
tasmin dine mahāpuṇye tasya candramaso bhavet |
iha bhuktvākhilān bhogān parivāreṇa sa nṛpaḥ
ante devyā puravare śivena vidyutā saha |
krīḍate vipulairbhogairyāvadācandratārakam
vasante bhūṣyate devī umā sarvasukhapradā |
nidāghe vahirlokantu sarvakāmasamanvitam
tasmin bhogān mahān bhuktvā devīloke mahīyate |
prāvṛṭ kāle rudralokaṃ śruṇuyād yāti pārthivaḥ
śarat sarvānavāpnoti kāmān rājyaṃ nṛpottama |
triḥ śrutvā bhaktimāsthāya mucyate sarvapātakaiḥ
viśuddhaśca bhavedvaṃśaḥ sarvakāmaphalāvahaḥ |
paṃca śrutvā mahādhyāyī svargaloke mahīyate
mātṛsaṃghaṃ yamo nityaṃ tuṣyate avicāraṇāt |
tasya bhogaṃ varṇayituṃ mama vāṇī na śaknuyāt
ihaloke śubhaṃ bhuktvā tadante śivalokataḥ |
khaṭvāvadhaṃ tathā śrutvā vināyakasya janma ca
mātṛlokamavāpnoti krīḍate ca ciraṃ sukho |
devīṃ sampūjayitvā tu vidhinā nṛpasattama
prasādañca prakurvīta pratyakṣā ca bhavet śivā |
sadācāraḥ śubhāhāraḥ sarvasaṃgavivarjitaḥ
vācayan purāṇamettattu sarvakāmamavāpnuyāt |
vācayan śatamardhaṃ vā pratyakṣaṃ prāpnuyācchivam
etaccābhyudayapādaṃ śataistribhirnarottamaiḥ |
sahasrairdvādaśairvatsa kathitaṃ sarvasiddhidam
| oṃ namo durgāyai |

iti śrī devīpurāṇe vācanavidhirnāma aṣṭāviṃśatyadhikaśatatamodhyāyaḥ |
|
|
